SU-01 谶 / Prophecy

黑绒出，小儿苦，良田千里遍尸骨。
When black grass creeps, the children cry, a thousand fields where dead ones lie.

冬雷吼，乌云布，地裂千里鬼哀哭。
When thunder roars and dark clouds curl, the earth splits wide, the spirits swirl.

地牛眝，千鸟临，阴阳颠倒日月停。
When the dragon glares, birds take flight. Yin twists with Yang, sun and moon unite.

？？？：……涣城亡，仙人降，长生不死脱灾殃。
???: When Huanzhou falls, the immortal descends, granting longevity and the calamity's end.

？？？：这就是我收集到的关键材料——！我准备把它用在报道开头，一定能成为一个夺人眼球的好引子！
???: Talk about inspiration! I'm using this as the introduction for my feature article. The mysterious vibe's gonna have them totally glued to the pages!

？？？：当然，我还收集了其他的东西……等我完成实地考察，就立刻着手撰写。
???: Got a whole lotta other stuff too. Gonna start as soon as I wrap up this fieldwork.

？？？：请相信我，空心木女士，这一定会成为《UTTU》东方特刊的一篇精华报道——
???: Trust me, Ms. Verity. This article's gonna be the star of UTTU's special issue on the East. I guarantee it!

汇报人的声音沿着蛛丝自远处的风中传来，如实收录了她所有的兴奋和期许。
As Reed provides her update, her voice shakes a delicate strand of spider silk before being carried off in the wind.

两位编辑点了点头，其中一人率先伸出手，触碰眼前纤细的蛛丝。
The two editors nod. One reaches out and gingerly touches the silk before them.

空心木：我了解了，芦草结编辑。
Verity: I think you really have something, Ms. Reed.

空心木：一首关于灾难与“长生”的童谣，凭借着其晦涩难懂的字眼，吸引了众多探险爱好者为之着迷。
Verity: An elliptical rhyme concerning disasters and the secrets of longevity. It's no surprise that adventurers find it so intriguing.

空心木：但类似的记载并不少见。光凭这些，我看不出它有撑起一期特刊的潜力。
Verity: But stories like this are not all that uncommon. I worry it won't have enough substance to carry our special issue.

空心木：是什么让你认为这条线索有继续实地调查的价值？
Verity: What makes you so sure it's worth a field trip?

芦草结：噢，您的问题很精准——我做过一些准备了，虽然还不是很详细，但勉强够用……
Reed: Ah, great question, ma'am. Well, I did some homework. It's not that much to go on, but if you'd just hear me out ...

风忠实地传递着所有信息，包括她努力翻动纸张的声音。
The wind carries the sounds from the other side faithfully, even the soft noise of her turning pages.

芦草结：自古以来，中国就有相当多类似的谶纬童谣，比如著名的“燕飞来，啄皇孙。皇孙死，燕啄矢”，还有“豆入牛口，势不得久”……
Reed: There's been all kinds of mantic rhymes in China since, like, the dawn of recorded history, a lot of them obscure or ambiguous. Like, uh, here. There's this one about the Zhou dynasty: "He who sells bows and quivers shall bring the collapse of Zhou ..."

芦草结：它们往往用隐晦的象征来暗指事情的变化、发展，其中部分是事后编造出来的，也有部分内容模糊，仔细一想，会发现有许多种解读。
Reed: But really, it was the man's adopted daughter who married Emperor Yōu of Zhou and led to the empire's downfall, and she wasn't even the main cause! What I'm saying is, most of these mantic rhymes are laced with veiled analogy. Who knows what they could mean?

芦草结：但这首童谣描绘的画面相对具体，不少内容能和当地的县志记载对应。
而且，把它告诉我的热心人坚持说自己手里有更多信息。
Reed: But this one's different—an exact event at an exact location. It's gonna be a breeze finding more details in the local annals. And my informant promised they'd give me more information when I get there.

芦草结：跑空是常有的事，可万一错过重要线索就亏大啦。所以我买了票，下了车，到了地方——
Reed: So, yeah, this trip could be a bust, but I'll regret it for the rest of my life if I don't get to the bottom of it. So, here I am in Zhu County.

芦草结：然后，你们猜——
Reed: And guess what I found?

她得意地卖了个关子。
She pauses, savoring the suspense.

芦草结：在这座小城里，风的确有细微的迟滞！
Reed: The wind really does slow around here! Only a little, but it for sure does!

编辑们惊讶地对视了一眼，坐直了身子。
The editors exchange surprised looks and lean in.

数羊羔：你是否需要协助？
Barbara: Will you need any further assistance?

芦草结：暂时不用，我还不能完全确定，等有了新发现再告诉大家。
Reed: I'm all good for now. But I'll let you guys know.

芦草结：我打算先联系那个人，约好时间和地点见面。然后再向本地居民打听……
Reed: First, I've gotta contact my informant and set up a meeting. Then, I'll interview some locals on the street.

芦草结：如果顺利，也许我们又能找到一个安全的去处……
Reed: Who knows? We could even find another shelter if things go well.

她兴奋地讲述着自己的规划和成果，没有注意到同伴们已经安静了好一会儿。
She's so eager to share her plans that she fails to notice her colleagues have fallen quiet.

空心木：行动力强的确是她的优点，也一直被很好地继承了下来。
Verity: She's always been a go-getter in every life.

数羊羔：但你知道，对她来说，“长生”是一个难以抗拒的主题。这些事又太巧合地凑到了一起……
Barbara: But I worry for her. You know how obsessed she is about longevity. These clues she found are unlikely to be a coincidence.

空心木：不用太担心，芦草结原本就长在那片土地，对那边的环境和文化不算陌生。
Verity: You needn't worry. Reed grew up there, originally. She won't have any trouble getting accustomed.

空心木：我们保持关注就好。
Verity: But let's keep an eye on her, just to be sure.

毛茸茸的编辑仍旧抛来担忧的眼神。空心木没再开口，只示意她触碰眼前的蛛丝。
The woolly editor holds her worried expression. Verity returns it with a silent pleading glance, motioning toward the still-open silk.

数羊羔：芦草结？你能听见吗？
Barbara: Reed? Are you still there?

数羊羔：这的确是很好的题材，但若是涉及到风网的扰动，你最好——
Barbara: We trust you've made a good decision with this article, but our network isn't stable right now. You'd better ...

街道上的嘈杂声响淹没了她的话语。
The noise from the streets drowns out the rest of her words.

芦草结：不好意思，我马上让开！
Reed: My bad. Didn't mean to block the way!

芦草结：抱歉，我得先去忙了，总之时间不等人，晚些再说吧！
Reed: Cool, cool, gotta go! I'm racing against the clock here! Call you later.

数羊羔：万一……危险……
Barbara: Watch out ... danger.

芦草结：放心，我没这么莽撞——拜拜！
Reed: No worries. I'll be careful. Bye bye!

芦草结中断了通讯，将蛛网胸针扶正，侧过身子躲避拥挤的人群与穿行而过的单车。
Reed ends the connection, adjusting her spiderweb brooch as she dodges through the crowds of people and passing bikes.

她左右张望，在不远处找到了自己的目的地。
She looks around and spies her goal not far away.

芦草结：没办法，还有好多事要忙。回去的时候给小羊带些本地特产，再跟她认真解释一下。
Reed: Hate to hang up on you, Barbara, but I've got, like, no time to do this. Maybe I'll buy her some local delicacies to say sorry.

芦草结：这县城里好热闹啊。人多，店铺也多……吃的也多！终于不用专门跑去唐人街了！
Reed: Place sure is lively, so many stores, oh my God, and the restaurants! Finally, no more driving to Chinatown to get a decent meal.

芦草结：先联系那个人，噢，还得赶快买几瓶水……
Reed: Alright, first things first. Gotta find an Internet cafe to contact the informant. Oh, better get a couple bottles of water too.

编辑朝着街对面的招牌走去。
The grass-headed editor walks toward the sign across the street.

长城牌落地扇缓慢地来回转头，尽力吹开柏油马路上扩散而来的热浪。
An electric fan oscillates back and forth, attempting in vain to blow away the heat rising from the road.

芦草结在竹椅上坐下，娴熟地握住了鼠标。
Reed rests on a bamboo chair, her hand finding the mouse in a familiar motion.

编辑迅速地在脑海里整理好了刚得到的信息。
She processes the new information, immediately drawing up a mental map of her impending investigation.

芦草结：清楚详细，没什么问题。
Reed: Nice and clear. Let's go.

编辑势在必得地迈出了脚步。
Reed takes a confident step forward.

芦草结：您好，请问您知道金家水井头怎么走吗？就在牌坊边大槐树下面。
Reed: Excuse me. Do you know the way to Jīn's Well? It's under a tree by the Paifang.

中年妇女：哪块儿？没听说过啊？
Middle-Aged Woman: What well? Never heard of it.

中年妇女：小姑娘，你是过来旅游的吧？要看木雕石雕，往远点的郊区走，老房子多，又安静。
Middle-Aged Woman: If you're looking for scenic spots, go to the outskirts of town. There's a lot of beautiful sculptures and architecture out there.

中年妇女：看梅树的话就往城中公园去。其余的就真不知道喽。
Middle-Aged Woman: And the Mei trees in the central park are famous. But I don't know anything about a well.

芦草结：谢谢您。忙完了我会去这几个地方逛逛的。
Reed: Oh, thanks. I'll check them out later.

芦草结向碰上的第十五个好心人挥手道别，预料中的捷报丝毫没有出现。
She waves goodbye to the fifteenth kind person she has questioned so far. The information she's been hoping for still fails to arrive.

她站在祝县正中央，目光从东边还未竣工的崭新高楼转到西边的马头墙。
Standing in the heart of Zhu County, she lets her eyes wander from the new unfinished buildings rising in the east over to the ancient horse-head walls in the west.

芦草结：建设路……
Reed: Jianshe Road ...

路牌反射的金属光泽让她眼前一片空白。
The street sign's metallic glare blinds her for a moment.

芦草结：转了半天，整条街的铺子也都问过了。水井头找不到，王婆婆的铺子也没个影。
Reed: That's it. I've asked everyone on the street. No well, no stall, no Grandma Wáng.

芦草结：我肯定不会记错地方。要是那个人骗我……也不用特地回消息编一串找不到的地名吧……
Reed: There's no way I got the address wrong. Did my informant lie? Not likely. What good would that do them?

芦草结：钞关……大佛寺……建设路……人民路……
Reed: The northern custom house, the Great Buddha Temple, Jianshe Road, Renmin Road ...

年轻的编辑苦苦思索着这些风马牛不相及的名词。
The locations feel off to the young editor. Each one seems to have no connection to the others.

芦草结：……难道，她告诉我的都是过去的地名？
Reed: What if these are all old locations? Like, they're names of places from the past?

老人：小同志，怎么站在路中间发愣？
Elder: Hey, young comrade. What are you doing in the middle of the street?

一个声音恰到好处地响起，向这株垂着头的植物投下了善意的绿荫。
A voice speaks, bringing a tide of relief that washes over her like soft rain.

老人：你刚刚找张姨问路，我都听着了。是有什么急事？是不是要搭公交去文化宫？我正好去下棋。
Elder: You've been asking around for directions, haven't you? To the bus stop? Just follow me. I'm heading there right now.

芦草结：不用不用。我和朋友约好在金家水井头见面，您知不知道怎么过去？
Reed: No, no. I'm meeting someone by Jīn's Well. Do you know where that is?

芦草结：这可能是很久之前的叫法。要是您觉得有什么地方像，都可以告诉我，我一个一个找。
Reed: Could be an old name, like, really, really old. So, if you know of anywhere even kinda similar, that'd be great. Anything will do.

老人：水井头……水井头……我就是这里人，五六十年了，没听过。
Elder: Jīn's Well, Jīn's Well ... I've lived here almost 60 years and never heard of it.

芦草结：那时间再久些，也许隔了两代……一百来年呢？
Reed: Then, it might be more than 60 years old. Maybe a hundred or so?

老人：一百年前？哎哟，现在的世界天翻地覆，一天一个样，几十年前的事情都难找咯！
Elder: 100 years old? You've got to be kidding. Things change so fast. The whole county looks completely different every few decades, let alone a century.

老人：你不要故意和老人家开玩笑，小同志。我是真怕你误了事，才停下喊你！
Elder: You're not trying to pull a fast one on me, are you? I thought you needed help.

芦草结：那……
Reed: No, sorry.

她努力思索着每条信息，想尽可能从一团乱麻中找出方向。
She considers each piece of information, trying to find a path through their mutual confusion.

芦草结：对了，童谣！您有没有听过一首童谣？
Reed: Oh, wait, the rhyme! Have you ever heard of this rhyme?

芦草结：有黑绒、惊雷、地裂之类的异象，还提到了仙人，还说和长生有关……
Reed: It's about black grass, thunder, the earth opening up, and an immortal.

老人：哈？啥玩意儿？
Elder: What? A rhyme?

老人的语气十分鄙夷，编辑沉在地上的心又往下掉了几分。
The scorn in his voice is withering.

恍惚间，她已经看到了截稿日将近，而稿纸上还一片空白的美妙光景。
For a moment, the approaching deadline and her still blank pages seem like a freight train rushing toward her.

老人：小同志，看你也不小了，打听这哄小孩的玩意儿干什么？
Elder: Aren't you a little too old to be searching for things from fairy tales?

老人：这传说我过去也听过，说是城底下睡着一位仙人，古时候碰上地裂天崩，是祂救了城中百姓。
Elder: But I have heard it before—an immortal that slept deep beneath Zhu County. In ancient times when the sky shattered and the earth broke apart, they emerged to save the town.

老人：仙人原本能长生不死，但法门却与祂一同消失，再不见天日。徒留后世人苦苦追寻长生之法……
Elder: But the immortal disappeared right after, taking the Method of Longevity with them, and no one has ever figured out where they went.

老人：因为这，以前还老有外地人来这里乱挖，说是要找寻仙人留下的长生法宝。
Elder: Still, grave robbers turn up around here every year. Those troublemakers just won't give up.

老人：小同志，看你像个文化人，可别掺合这些牛鬼蛇神的事。现在还和你讲什么“长生”的，肯定是骗子。
Elder: You seem like a bright young lady. Surely you don't buy into this longevity nonsense, right?

SU-02 风中芦苇 / A Windblown Reed

芦草结猛地站起身，一旁的小卖部老板娘惊了一跳，朝她望过来。
Reed shoots up from her seat. The storekeeper, half-startled, looks over to her.

老板娘：丫头，你怎么了？是这网不好使了？我待会就喊我姑娘来看下，不急，不急！
Storekeeper: What's wrong? Is that computer acting up again? Don't you worry. I'll have my daughter fix it.

老板娘：瞧你脸色这么差，来，先喝口水……
Storekeeper: You look a little pale. Here, have some water.

冒着热气的塑料杯递到芦草结面前。
Hot steam rises up from the plastic cup.

老板娘：咱们这也是才用上新鲜东西不久，要时间适应的。水土不服嘛……
Storekeeper: These newfangled computer things are quite complex, you know. It takes time to understand how they work.

芦草结：您人真好——您知不知道，这里哪儿还有以前的城门？
Reed: Thank you, ma'am. Can I ask, do you know of any old gates that are still around here?

芦草结：哪怕只剩半堵墙，一块砖也行！您告诉我就成！
Reed: Even if there's just a bit of wall left, or even a single brick! Anything!

老板娘疑惑地多打量了她两眼，朝远处扬了扬下巴。
The storekeeper looks puzzled. But eventually she gestures with her chin into the distance.

老板娘：你一路急匆匆的，没注意到吧。喏。
Storekeeper: An old gate? You must've been too busy to notice it before. Over there.

老板娘：大家每天都打下边过，有什么好看的？
Storekeeper: It's just a gate like any other. Why do you ask?

芦草结：唔……
Reed: Hmm.

芦草结：我再买一箱水，姨姨，这把椅子能不能借我多坐几个钟头？
Reed: I'll have another pack of water, ma'am. Can I stay here for a couple more hours?

在沉沉的夜色中，芦草结仍能辨认出高大建筑的轮廓。
Even against the deep darkness, Reed can still make out the shape of the tall building.

她揉了揉眼睛，环顾四周。
She rubs her eyes and looks around.

一片寂静，连风的声音也止歇了。
Everything is still. Even the wind has stopped.

芦草结：在附近观察了一下午，这里的确就是风最为迟滞之处。
Reed: It's late, but this must be the place. The wind's definitely slowing down around here.

芦草结：好吧……小羊的叮嘱是对的。风网恰好在这里出现扰动，也许不是偶然……
Reed: *sigh* Barbara's right. There's gotta be a reason for this interference in the network.

芦草结叹了口气，揉了揉自己头上发黄的草叶。
Reed sighs and rubs the yellowing grass on her head.

芦草结：但我没有时间了。是牛鬼还是蛇神，都只能拉出来看看了。
Reed: I'm totally running out of time. Whoever's behind this, I gotta confront them STAT.

芦草结：你说，如果我交不上报道，却解决了编辑部的网络异常……是否也不算是白来一趟？
Reed: I guess I might miss the article deadline, but I can still solve the interface issue. That counts as a win, right?

她头顶的草叶晃了晃。一只蜘蛛小心地牵着丝线坠下来。
Her grass blades sway as she watches a spider descending down a strand of web.

芦草结用指腹抵住那根蛛丝。
Reed brushes the silk with her finger.

芦草结：风从来都是流动的，它不会无缘由地停留在某处。
Reed: The wind doesn't hover in place for no reason, let alone get tangled up.

芦草结：如果所谓的系结真的存在，一定有某种力量使那片区域静止……
Reed: So, if it gets tied up in a knot like this, there's gotta be some kind of special power making it stick.

芦草结：流经它的风会被拖慢脚步，即使只是……那么……
Reed: That power clings to any wind that passes by. The closer the wind is to the knot, the slower it becomes. So, all I need to do is ...

芦草结：一枚小点。
Reed: Find the spot where the wind's moving slowest.

芦草结：找到了！
Reed: *gasp* Over there!

编辑兴奋地喊出声来，又迅速回过神，心虚地低了低头。
She cries out with joy only to realize her surroundings as she ducks her head in embarrassment.

芦草结：哎呀，不好意思不好意思。我不是故意吵闹的。
Reed: Oops, sorry. I'll try to keep it down.

好在周围仍然空无一人。小城的夜里，似乎只有她醒着。
Luckily, at night here in this quiet neighborhood, Reed seems to be the only one awake.

她拿起手电，走向城门。
She grabs her flashlight and walks out toward the gate.

芦草结：就在附近。具体位置还得再确认……
Reed: It's close. Lemme feel for the wind again.

她伸出手，但这次并没有蛛丝及时垂落。
She reaches out her hand, but this time no silk appears.

芦草结：嗯？
Reed: Hmm?

一阵风拂动了她头顶的草叶。
A breeze stirs the grass on her head.

风中夹杂着细碎的哭声，再仔细听，多了一道由远及近的车铃。
It carries broken sobs, then the bell of an approaching bike.

芦草结：早知道你会来！出来！
Reed: I knew you'd come! C'mon! Show yourself!

手电亮光扫过，芦草结预想中的敌人并未出现。
Her flashlight beam sweeps the area, but it doesn't find her expected foe.

芦草结：不是论坛里那个人？
Reed: You're OneWithFlow, right?

芦草结：等等，如果对方本来就不是“人”，那么……
Reed: Wait. What if they aren't even human?

她顿时又打起了几分精神。
Her spirits lift a little.

芦草结：这次调查就更有价值了！我的报道将会——
Reed: I've gotta dig deeper. This'll totally make the article—

芦草结：哎呀！
Reed: Ah!

某样沉重而温暖的物件紧挨着她的小腿，发出婴孩的哭泣。
Something warm and heavy presses against her leg, letting out a cry like a baby.

她惊讶地低下头，车铃在背后响起。
She looks down, shocked. A bike bell rings behind her.

芦草结：好吧，不怪你们，是我没打招呼就闯进了你们家里。
Reed: Alright, my bad. I shouldn't have broken into your place.

芦草结：我很快就走，再看几眼就走……
Reed: I'll leave, I promise. Just gimme a sec.

光圈从头顶落回地面，芦草结敏锐地捕捉到了石墙上一闪而过的凹凸痕迹。
Reed angles her flashlight downward, taking notice of a faint mark on the stone wall.

芦草结：刻字？
Reed: Are those carvings?

芦草结：入我教门，长生有成……仙人授法，无劫无殃。
Reed: Let me see. "Step into our gate, and gain eternity. From the hands of the immortal, law descends—no calamity, no end."

芦草结：看来我真的找对地方了。
Reed: Bingo. Finally, something concrete.

她向前走了两步，左手伸向胸口，轻轻敲了敲那枚蛛网胸针。
She takes a few steps forward, her left hand reaching for the spiderweb brooch on her chest.

芦草结：我有重要的新发现。祝县古城门底下的刻字前面，风在这里几乎静止……
Reed: Hello? I've got some amazing findings to report. There's an old gate in town where the wind's almost totally frozen.

芦草结：小羊？空心木女士？
Reed: Hello? Barbara? Ms. Verity?

她想起刚接近城墙时的寂静，还有一直沉默的蜘蛛。
She finds a familiar silence as she nears the wall. The spider lies dormant and still.

芦草结：那群卡邦克鲁过来的时候还有风。
Reed: Huh, it was pretty windy when those Carbuncles popped out. They must've disturbed the air.

芦草结：它们在暗中活动，一定会带动周围的气流。就算没有蜘蛛帮忙，只要能捕捉到一丝微风……
Reed: Can't get any connection on the spider as is. Guess I've gotta make some wind myself.

她按灭了手电。
She switches off her light.

芦草结：一定有办法。
Reed: Here goes.

她用力跺了跺脚，不远处响起熟悉的车铃声。
She stomps her foot, and a familiar bike bell sounds nearby.

芦草结在心里向那群小生物道了歉。
Reed silently apologizes to the small creatures.

芦草结：接下来，引导这些风散开……
Reed: Next, guide the wind to untie the knot.

芦草结：……什么……？
Reed: What?

她的身体骤然僵硬了。
Her body stiffens.

一切都不复存在，不再有声响、光亮、气味。无止尽的黑暗毫不客气地将她吞下。
Everything vanishes. Sound, light, even smell disappear as the void swallows her whole.

而后，一道陌生的询问将她打捞而起。
Until an unfamiliar voice cuts through the darkness.

？？？：要不要尝尝看？
???: Want to try mine?

席卷着她的狂风猛然向着声音收缩、凝固，然后猝然下坠。
The wind sweeps her up and pulls her toward the voice, then stops and plummets.

SU-03 “长生之门” / "The Gate to Longevity"

？？？：来一口嘛！
???: Go on, have a taste.

芦草结：是谁？
Reed: Who's there?

倒卧的女子：你不是一直都想尝尝这家的清白盏吗，惠姑？
Reclining Lady: I was certain you'd been dying to try the clear soup, Mayfly.

芦草结：清白盏？！
Reed: Clear soup?

碗中倒映出一个皱着眉的少女。芦草结借着她的眼睛，打量着碗沿细白的糖粒。
From the reflection in the bowl, Reed sees a frown on a face that doesn't belong to her. Through that reflection's eyes, she notices a white rim of sugar that rounds the bowl.

惠姑：你倒的糖都够老板再做一大锅了，鹭鸶剪，它早就没有原先的味道啦！好糟蹋东西。
Mayfly: You just poured a whole potful of sugar in, Paper Heron. You can hardly even call it clear soup anymore. Eugh, what a waste.

鹭鸶剪：可我还觉得远远不够呢……
Paper Heron: Aha, really? I think it could use a touch more.

喧哗声灌入脑海，寒冷从衣物外透进来，粗糙的麻布无时无刻不在摩擦着皮肤，空气里尽是水和尘土的腥味。
Noise fills her head. Cold seeps through her clothes. Rough cloth rubs against her skin. The air spiced with the comfortable smell of wet dirt.

男童Ⅰ：啊——娘——我手好冷——
Boy I: *whining* Mama, my hands are cold.

古代妇女Ⅰ：那也不能塞衣领子里！叫人看见成什么样子？
Ancient Woman I: Cold or not, you don't press your hands against someone's neck! It's rude.

古代男子Ⅰ：这不是正好来看亲戚嘛！诶，你听说了没有，这次庙会好像不简单啊……
Ancient Man I: I'm visiting my cousin. Heard there will be something special at the fair this year.

小贩Ⅰ：祝县老字号！三文钱一碗暖汤，三文钱一碗！
Vendor I: Classic Zhu snacks for only three wen! Only three wen!

芦草结：这是……祝县？
Reed: Zhu County? But, this looks totally different.

惠姑：加了这么多糖，你都不嫌甜……你、你舌头坏掉啦……鹭鸶剪。
Mayfly: You want more? Have you ... Have you lost your taste, Heron?

鹭鸶剪：不止是舌头，别的地方也坏啦！所以我才走南闯北地找法子来治我这个毛病。
Paper Heron: Not just my taste, all my senses. That's why I roam the land, see. I'm seeking a cure.

惠姑：那你也是来找仙人的？
Mayfly: Then, you're here to see the immortal too?

鹭鸶剪：唔……我是来访友的。但我那朋友生得仙风道骨……我也不知道她是否能算上……
Paper Heron: Ah, no, merely seeking a companion of mine. She does have the look of an immortal, though I couldn't say for sure whether she is one.

鹭鸶剪：你说的那仙人什么样？
Paper Heron: But tell me about this immortal you seek.

惠姑想了想，不好意思地继续解释道。
Mayfly thinks for a moment, then continues shyly.

惠姑：其实我也没见过，只是大家都这么传——今年的庙会上会出现一个仙人来传授长生之法……
Mayfly: Honestly, I know very little about them. All I've heard is that an immortal is supposed to come to the fair this year to teach people the Method of Longevity.

惠姑：他们说，只要学了这种仙法，不仅能使人长生不老，还能强健人的体魄。
Mayfly: They say it grants both a long life and lasting health.

惠姑：有个老奶奶学了这个以后，冬天能在南淝河游三个来回呢……
Mayfly: Its results are said to be remarkable. An old granny learned it, and now she can swim the Nanfei River back and forth, even during winter.

惠姑：你这毛病，兴许长生之法也能治！
Mayfly: Maybe it's the cure you're looking for too!

鹭鸶剪：那好啊，我到时候仔细问问仙人……
Paper Heron: Sounds intriguing. I'll be sure to keep an eye out.

鹭鸶剪：可是你说话为什么要这么小声？
Paper Heron: But why the hushed voice?

惠姑有些担忧地看了看周围。
Mayfly looks around anxiously.

惠姑：因为有关“长生之法”的消息传出来之后，祝县县令就颁布了一张告示，让大家不要听信谣言，更不能乱传。
Mayfly: Because the guards might hear me. The magistrate posted a notice saying the rumor's false; anyone who spreads it will be punished.

鹭鸶剪：嗯，人言可畏，要是传得太过夸张，确实不好。
Paper Heron: Hmm, words do carry weight. Rumors can grow out of control if left unchecked.

惠姑：是吧……
Mayfly: True.

惠姑：这里排队的人，有好多都是冲着“长生之法”来的，我听讲……好像还有从辽东特意过来的。辽东诶，听讲那是个又冷又远的地方。
Mayfly: Still, it's drawn all sorts to Zhu County. Just look at the line behind us. Some told me they came all the way from Liaodong, far in the frozen north.

鹭鸶剪：是吗！这么厉害啊！
Paper Heron: Is that so? Good for them, eh?

惠姑：你、你小声点！不怕被抓起来呀？
Mayfly: Shhh! Keep your voice down. Aren't you afraid of the guards?

惠姑：你是道士，一会儿搞不好会细细地查你呢！
Mayfly: You're a Daoist. They'll search you head to toe.

惠姑：我听讲，有好多流民啊，方士啊，小精怪啊……为了学“长生之法”，都混进祝县去了。
Mayfly: I heard all manner of folk are trying to sneak into the town, the kinds that'll do anything for the Method of Longevity.

惠姑：那些巡捕就在查这个呢。说是因为那些坏人在县内作乱，犯下了好多杀害人命的案件……县内外，只要有人提这个，就会被抓进去盘问一番。
Mayfly: There've even been deaths. See those guards? They're checking every traveler looking for vagrants, Yao, and criminals. Speak of the Method, and you'll be locked away in an instant.

惠姑：所以现在城门处的检查都可严格了，还用上了振气铃，就为了把那些坏人隔离在外面。
Mayfly: That's why they're so strict. They've even got Reversion Bells to magically identify us Yao.

惠姑：但这只能防得住那些脑子不太灵光的，别人跟我讲，想到办法混进城去的精怪也不少。
Mayfly: But I think those things only work on the dull-witted ones. Quite a few have slipped through already.

鹭鸶剪：振气铃只能让妖现出原形，能分辨出人心好坏的可不是这个。
Paper Heron: Reversion Bells only reveal a Yao's true face. They cannot tell virtue from vice.

鹭鸶剪：别苦着脸了，我跟你讲点好玩的，这世上确实有能够分辨人好坏的东西，但却不是振气铃。
Paper Heron: Yet there are things that can: truth potions, the Immortal's Brush, even some arcane beasts.

鹭鸶剪：法器呢，谛聆水和仙茅笔都可以分辨人的好坏，灵兽呢……
Paper Heron: Hmm? You're not listening, Mayfly. Take a breath. All will be well.

惠姑：好啦好啦……我没心情听这个……
Mayfly: Eugh, frost take me. I don't need a magic lesson right now.

惠姑摇了摇头，瞥见了鹭鸶剪的骡子。
Mayfly shakes her head, letting her gaze rest on Paper Heron's mule.

惠姑：你骡子背上挂了这么多各式各样的小玩意儿，是要带去庙会摆摊吗？
Mayfly: Hey, you've got a lot of stuff packed up on that mule. You selling those things at the fair?

鹭鸶剪：不是，当时我看着觉得好玩，便也给朋友带些，可不知道她究竟喜欢什么，便都买了，总能撞到她心仪的。
Paper Heron: No, I wanted to get a gift for my friend, but I'm not so sure of her taste, so I bought whatever caught my eye. I'll let her choose whatever she likes.

惠姑：这是玉雕雪莲吗？你在西域买的？
Mayfly: Is this a snow lotus carving? Did you find it in the Western Regions?

看到从未见过的东西，惠姑的话匣子便打开了。
Caught up in the excitement of this new sight, Mayfly can't help but start asking questions, her tone alive with interest.

惠姑：那里景色怎么样？是不是很漂亮？跟我讲讲这个吧！
Mayfly: What was it like there? Is it as beautiful as they say? Please, tell me all about it.

鹭鸶剪：那地方确实好看！悬崖峭壁，万里雪飘，风光无限啊！只是我任骡子带我走遍天涯，不知那里原来是被叫作西域……
Paper Heron: Ah, the view was breathtaking. Standing at the cliff's edge, watching the world turn white with the falling snow. I didn't even realize where I was. My mule carried me there, see.

鹭鸶剪：西域，在西边吗？西边在哪里？
Paper Heron: The Western Regions, hmm, to the west, then? Where exactly is that?

鹭鸶剪环视着四周，如同一只失了磁的罗盘。
Paper Heron's eyes dart upward, forward, side-to-side, until they look like a needle on a broken compass.

惠姑：……唉。
Mayfly: *sigh*

惠姑：我都忘记了你是个指着南却要往北走的家伙，不然也不会半路上被我捡到。
Mayfly: I almost forgot how hopeless you are with directions. Lucky I found you on your way here, or rather, on your way somewhere else entirely.

惠姑：算了算了，我们还是继续排队吧。
Mayfly: Never mind. Let's get back in line.

堵上了鹭鸶剪的嘴，惠姑透过人群的缝隙望着城门，不安地捏着衣角里的什么东西。
She doesn't wait for a response. Mayfly looks over the crowd toward the city gate, her fingers rubbing a hidden object in the folds of her clothes.

烦躁隐隐浮动在人群之中，略高于鞋底被碾的砂石，略低于因无聊而四处晃动的天灵盖。
There's a low current of unease that runs through the crowd. As if they were moving along a treacherous bridge, each shift of their feet cautious as heads bob side-to-side, checking for movement.

这队伍如盘古开天辟地时就排在这里没有动过一般，不论是谁都只能远远地望一眼排头，然后深深地叹一口气。
It doesn't move. For a time, it feels like it has never moved at all. Each person taking their turn to sigh as they look ahead with a worried expression.

惠姑：要排到什么时候？我等得快发芽了……
Mayfly: *sigh* How much longer must we wait? I'll start growing roots if this line doesn't budge.

古代男子Ⅰ：往前走走了！
Ancient Man I: Move forward, will you?

巡捕Ⅰ：快快快，通过行李盘查的赶紧走，去振气铃那儿。后头还那么多人呢！
Constable I: Get moving! Those who passed the cargo check must go to the Reversion Bell! Hurry it up. There's a whole line behind you!

巡捕Ⅰ：下一个！
Constable I: Next!

巡捕不耐烦地催促着，朝后面的队列挥了挥手。
The impatient constable gestures for the static line to advance.

惠姑：……马上就轮到我了……
Mayfly: I'll be next.

惠姑用手攥着衣角内的物件，磋磨着蹭了过去。
Mayfly squeezes the little object tight beneath her robes as she edges forward.

巡捕Ⅰ：衣角里缝了什么？这么硬？
Constable I: What's that you have tucked in your sleeve? It looks solid.

惠姑：没、什么都没有，官爷。
Mayfly: N-Nothing, officer.

巡捕Ⅰ：别抓着衣角，把……
Constable I: Hands in the air. Give—

惊呼声从前面的队列传来，惠姑向声音来源望去。
A cry comes from up ahead, causing both of them to turn their heads.

惠姑：怎么了？
Mayfly: What happened?

青铜铃音在一名男子的身周凝聚了起来，并将他死死地压在地上。
A bronze bell rings, its noise emanating from a man at the front of the line, the vibrations pressing him into the ground.

平民Ⅰ：呃啊……
Civilian I: Aghh.

平民Ⅱ：爪子……他长出爪子了！
Civilian II: Claws. His hands are turning into claws!

在铃音的震慑中，男子缓缓变化，化形成了一只青面獠牙的大黄狗。
Under the bell's power, the man transforms into a large yellow dog, its features fiendish, its fangs sharp.

黄狗精：吼——
Yellow Dog: *roar*

平民Ⅱ：不好啦！精怪跑出来啦！快跑啊——
Civilian II: Run! It's a Yao! Run!

巡捕Ⅱ：拦住他！别让这个黄狗精跑了！
Constable II: Capture that monster! Don't let it get away!

平民Ⅲ：别挤我！有人摔倒了！
Civilian III: Stop pushing! Someone fell down here!

惠姑：诶……别，别挤了！
Mayfly: Hey. Stop-Stop pushing!

惠姑：那精怪呢，那精怪在……
Mayfly: Where's the Yao? Where?

鹭鸶剪：八景冥合，炁入玄玄。三光无明，皆失其路。
Paper Heron: Eight views merge, the mystery of Qi. Three lights darken, and all lose their way.

惠姑：咦……？
Mayfly: W-What?

惠姑：鹭鸶剪……你念了什么呀？我……好晕啊……
Mayfly: Heron, wh-what was that spell? I feel woozy.

鹭鸶剪：来，上骡！
Paper Heron: Come on. Hop up.

惠姑：我、大家……这是……怎么啦……
Mayfly: What's happening? I ...

鹭鸶剪：黄狗横冲直撞，城门处人又多，相互踩踏致伤可就不好了。
Paper Heron: We can't let that yellow dog tear through the crowd.

鹭鸶剪：还是都冷静一下，等我制服了这黄狗，大家便能继续进城逛庙会。
Paper Heron: I'll subdue it before harm comes to anyone. Easy now, big fellow.

黄狗精：吼——嗷——！！！
Yellow Dog: Roar!!!

鹭鸶剪：哦？你还挺能撑的嘛！
Paper Heron: Ah, you're tougher than I thought.

鹭鸶剪：那我们来比试一下吧！
Paper Heron: Show me what you've got.

？？？：谁在城门闹事？！
???: Who is responsible for this mayhem?

黄狗精：呜……呜……
Yellow Dog: *whimper*

一击将黄狗精击晕后，官吏模样的青年持刀转向骡上的鹭鸶剪。
A young man in an officer's uniform knocks the yellow dog out with a single strike. As it crumples to the ground, he turns his blade toward Paper Heron now seated on her mule.

？？？：你就是作乱城门的罪魁祸首？
???: Causing chaos at the city gate, are we? Looking for trouble?

鹭鸶剪：大人明察，非我也，狗也！
Paper Heron: Your most discerning lordship, I swear on all that is good. 'Twas he who started it.

？？？：区区黄狗精，岂须用你这么大阵仗。
???: Hmph. Was there really any need for all this?

那武官的腰牌就明晃晃地系在腰带之上，鹭鸶剪不免读出声来。
The officer's token hangs plainly and openly on his belt, tempting Paper Heron to begin reading its inscription aloud without thinking.

鹭鸶剪：直隶涣州府祝县太白巡检司，巡检，程和光……
Paper Heron: Patrol Bureau of Zhu County, Chief Constable, Chéng Héguāng.

程和光：正是在下。
Cheng Heguang: At your service.

程和光：杜六，杨武！你们一人安顿百姓，一人让道人解除咒法，并将其关押，我过会儿来审！
Cheng Heguang: Dù Liù, stay and maintain order. Yáng Wǔ, arrest this Daoist. Ensure she lifts the spell before you put her away. I will question her personally.

杜六&杨武：是！
Du Liu & Yang Wu: Understood!

术法的余韵尚在，城门处其他人的世界仍在一片昏冥中旋转。
The spell's force lingers in the air. The others at the gate remain dazed as the world spins.

杜六杨武只能从迷乱的人影中缓慢地清出一条路来。
Dù Liù and Yáng Wǔ push their way through the confused crowd.

平民Ⅱ：唉……唉……我这是到哪儿啦？天庭还是龙宫？
Civilian II: Aah. Where am I? Is this heaven?

平民Ⅲ：不对啊……怎么打开钱袋也看不见钱……我的眼睛瞎了？
Civilian III: Wait. What happened to the money in my purse? Did that dog curse my sight?

惠姑：唔……不是我干的……不是我……
Mayfly: Ah, don't look at me. I didn't do anything.

巡捕Ⅱ：黄……狗……精……别想跑……！
Constable II: Damned yellow dog! You won't get away from us!

一名昏了头的巡捕举着振气铃倒向了人群，浑然不觉黄狗精并不在此处。
A dazed constable holds the Reversion Bell as he stumbles into the crowd.

惠姑：——哎？
Mayfly: Eh?

在铃音的震慑中，惠姑的身影已然不再。
Under the bell's power, Mayfly's human form disappears.

眼前只有一株半枯的黄草。
In its place appears a wilting tuft of grass.

鹭鸶剪：不好！
Paper Heron: Oh, no!

芦草结：——她？！
Reed: Wait, she's a ...?

情急之下，芦草结喊出了声音。眼前的景象顿时雾气般散去。
Acting on pure instinct, Reed calls out, but the scene before her dissolves away like mist.

微风拂过发梢，祝县也已稍有秋日的凉意。
A light wind rustles her hair. Zhu County feels the first chill winds of autumn.

不知不觉间，她已走出了城门楼，回到了夜间的街道上。
Without realizing it, she has left the gate tower and found herself walking alone through the dark streets.

芦草结：风能长久地保留信息，这系结应该有不少年头了……我看到的是……惠姑的经历？
Reed: The wind can hold on to information for a long time, so I'm guessing that knot must've been here for ages. Then, that must have been Mayfly's memory?

芦草结：她竟然跟我一样，也是苇草……
Reed: Her true form was a tuft of reed, just like me.

芦草结：从周围的景色看，那时候是冬天……
Reed: It was already winter, though; she would've been running out of time.

她想起自己在笔记本上的涂画，三百多个格子已经划去三分之二。
She thinks of the calendar in her notebook. Over three hundred boxes, two-thirds crossed out.

芦草结：那个论坛上的人……会是惠姑吗？
Reed: Then, my informant from the forum ... Could it be her?

SU-04 一叶知秋 / Summer's Lease

编辑已经在床边默坐了许久。
Reed sits quietly by the bed.

每个角落都没有熟悉的蜘蛛朋友，她的胸针也始终不曾亮起。
No sign of her spider friend. No glow from the brooch on her chest.

她已经拿着胸针走遍了城内的大街小巷，但留给她的只有死一样的寂静。
She has walked every street in the city but never found an answer. It was all in vain.

芦草结：不行，联系不上编辑部……
Reed: Nope, wind's still giving me nothing.

几片枯黄的叶子自她的头上掉下，落在床褥之间。
A few dry leaves break off from her head, drifting toward her pillow.

芦草结：也许我应该先出县城，坐大巴去市区，询问空心木女士的意见后再折返回来……
Reed: Maybe I should leave so I can contact Ms. Verity and then decide if I want to head back.

芦草结：不……那个人太可疑了，空心木女士绝不会让我再继续调查了。
Reed: No. It's all too suspicious. She'd tell me to abort, for sure.

芦草结：所以我应该就此放弃，回到总部。如果我还有时间，就再筹备新的选题。
Reed: *sigh* Basically, I should give up and just go back to headquarters. I could pick another topic to work on if I still have time.

你还有多少时间？
How much time do you have left?

芦草结：我……还有时间吗？
Reed: Time. Hah. Like I've ever had that.

编辑自嘲地笑了笑。她捡起掉落在被间的草叶，将它轻轻展平。
The budding writer lets out a short laugh at her own expense as she picks up a fallen leaf from the bed and smooths it flat.

芦草结：冬天就要到了。
Reed: Winter's coming.

芦草结：到那时，我便该枯萎了。尽管明年又会有一株新的苇草，但那株草并不是我。
Reed: I'll have withered by then. Even if another reed'll sprout from my body next year, "I" will be gone for good.

芦草结：对于我们这样春生冬死的草本植物而言，这就是我们的命运。
Reed: The inevitable end of every ephemeral plant.

芦草结：惠姑……她后来怎样了呢？她逃过这样的命运了么？
Reed: Mayfly ... She was one of us. I wonder what happened to her. Did she find a way to keep on living?

芦草结：……不行。
Reed: Hrmph.

芦草结：我……不甘心。我不甘心就这样结束，这明明是我离答案最近的一次……！
Reed: I can't. I just can't accept that I'll die without finishing my article, especially when I'm, like, a single step away from finding a way to stay me.

草叶被认真地夹在了笔记本的纸页之间。
She places the blade of grass between the pages of her notebook.

芦草结：风的凝滞本就是异常事件。解开它，风就能恢复正常的流动。没有我，它也理应被其他神秘学家解开。
Reed: That's that. I just need to keep going. Besides, these knots are an anomaly that needs to be fixed anyway; why shouldn't I be the one to do it?

芦草结：不必去理会枯荣自任。我能靠自己的本事解开第一个系结，也能解开剩下的。
Reed: Alright, forget about whatever this OneWithFlow's trying. I'll just do my thing.

芦草结：我……必须完成我的选题。
Reed: I-I have to finish this article.

她合上笔记本，踏出了房门。
Reed closes her notebook and steps out the door.

意识再一次被狂风从躯体中抽出，这依旧让芦草结感到极大的不适。
Once more, the wind seems to pull at her, nearly tearing her mind straight out of her body. The gust leaves behind an uneasy feeling in her stomach.

强忍住这种感觉，她等待着预料中的下坠。
She bears the feeling and waits for the fall she knows is coming.

芦草结：……还会是惠姑吗？
Reed: Is this another of Mayfly's memories?

物伤其类的悲伤短暂升起，旋即被隐约耳熟的声音打断。
A brief sadness rises in her, then a faintly familiar voice cuts it off.

？？？：小程巡检？
???: Chief?

？？？：我能进来吗？
???: May I enter?

程和光：请。
Cheng Heguang: Please.

处理完城门处的骚乱后，杜六叩响了城门门军房的门。
After settling the disturbance, Dù Liù makes his way to the town's constabulary office and knocks at the door of his chief.

书案前，程和光正埋头研究着厚厚的案卷。
At the desk, Chéng Héguāng bends over a mess of documents.

杜六：小程巡检，那道人已经解除了咒法，百姓中有几名因黄狗精而受了惊吓，磕碰了几处，我已命人送去医治了。
Du Liu: Sir, the Daoist has lifted the spell. Several people in the crowd were injured by that yellow dog; we've sent them to get treatment.

杜六：城门关卡也已恢复秩序，平民正有序过关。
Du Liu: Order has been restored at the gate. Inspections are ongoing.

杜六：杨武将那道人和她的骡子押进了城门班房，等候您查问。
Du Liu: The Daoist and her mule are locked up. She's ready for interrogation. Yáng Wǔ is watching her.

程和光点点头，将目光从案卷中拔了出来。
The chief nods, barely looking up from his files.

程和光：好，你回岗吧，我马上就去杨武那边。
Cheng Heguang: Good. Return to your position. I will go to see her immediately.

杜六好奇地上前瞅了瞅程和光的手中之物，冲着密密麻麻的字抱怨。
Dù Liù looks down over the papers, letting out an unintended grumble as he realizes their meaning.

杜六：小程巡检，属下不懂，今年庙会的搜检真要这么严苛吗？
Du Liu: Ah. Forgive me, Chief, but isn't that someone else's job? I fail to see why we should bother investigating these animal carcasses. I know the Stilted Parade is about to begin, but—

程和光：“高跷巡神”岂是普通的庙会？
Cheng Heguang: You understand the importance of this for the people, do you not? We must leave no stone unturned.

杜六：即使它再重要，为了调查动物遗尸的案件，也有些过为已甚了。
Du Liu: Yes, but even so, it seems a waste of our men's time to look into a few dead animals?

杜六：更何况现在并无任何证据表明此事为精怪所为，兴许就是山上饿极的野兽干的呢？
Du Liu: There's no proof that they were killed by Yao. Perhaps it was some beasts in the mountain that chased them here.

杜六：而且即使就是“它们”作祟，我们也无需做出如此大的阵仗……毕竟，谁知这其中是否涉及“它们”自己的恩怨情仇。
Du Liu: And even if it was a Yao, there's no need to take it so seriously. It's best to leave them to their own affairs.

程和光：什么叫“它们”？
Cheng Heguang: "Their own affairs"?

程和光：无论是人是妖，只要有违反大明律令、威胁百姓安全之事，我们就当义不容辞。何必想这么多无关紧要之事？
Cheng Heguang: All residents of the Ming Empire, be they human or Yao, are bound under the same law, and it is our duty to uphold it.

程和光：你也知道，最近县里不太太平。我总觉得，这动物遗尸的案件与其他精怪犯下的案子有千丝万缕的联系。
Cheng Heguang: You know as well as I do that something is afoot here. Those carcasses are involved in all this. I can feel it.

程和光指了指手中的案卷。
He points at the file in his hand.

程和光：这是刚送来的案子，今早在城中春花巷内又发现了一具动物遗尸。
Cheng Heguang: This report just reached me. Another carcass was found in Chunhua Alley this morning.

程和光：与前几案相同，被发现时尸体面容灰白，肌肉失养，但肢体完整。在案发地的不远处，也再次出现了神秘游行队伍的目击报告。
Cheng Heguang: Like the others, it was intact, yet pale and dry. There were also sightings of the same mysterious parade near the scene.

程和光：散播长生流言的正是这支游行队伍，据我所知，已经有县民被他们蛊惑，去修行什么“长生之法”。
Cheng Heguang: They were spreading rumors about the Method of Longevity. They have already amassed a small following.

程和光：正值“高跷巡神”开办期间，厉守备早就嘱咐过我们，在此期间定要护县民周全，我们有什么理由不严查？
Cheng Heguang: And do not forget Commander Lì's orders: we must make sure the fair is without blemish. This risk is too large to ignore.

杜六：可是这几天兄弟们跑前跑后，轮流站岗，早就累得要命——
Du Liu: But, Chief Chéng, the men have been working for weeks without rest. They're exhausted. If we give them more work—

杜六还未讲完，门军房的门便再度被叩响。
Dù Liù doesn't have time to finish his complaint before another knock interrupts him.

巡捕Ⅰ：程巡检，杨武问您何时过去！
Constable I: Chief, Yáng Wǔ is expecting you.

程和光：我知道，我马上就去。
Cheng Heguang: Understood. I'll be there shortly.

抱怨尚未开始就被打断，杜六只得把满腔苦水都咽进肚里。
His subordinate decides to bite back his words.

杜六：那属下就先行……
Du Liu: I must go. Excuse me, Chief.

程和光：等一下！咳……
Cheng Heguang: Hold on! Hmm.

杜六站在原地，等待着程和光发话。
Dù Liù waits, already expecting his next words.

程和光：我……我知道最近因为城防的事情三班倒，大家都很疲乏。
Cheng Heguang: I, hmm, I know that everyone has been working hard of late, and I am sincerely grateful for their efforts.

程和光不熟练地搜肠刮肚着。
He stumbles to find the right words.

程和光：此事过后，我定会在县里最好的酒楼中……
Cheng Heguang: So, let them know, once the fair is over, I will take them to the finest restaurant in town.

程和光：宴请各位。
Cheng Heguang: My treat.

杜六：那属下代弟兄们谢过小程巡检了。不过小程巡检自己的俸禄应该就没多少，到时候……
Du Liu: Much appreciated. But I'm certain even a chief's salary couldn't cover such a meal.

杜六：我让弟兄们先喝三大碗井水再去，免得小程巡检难堪。
Du Liu: I'll have their bellies filled before we go. We wouldn't want to embarrass you, huh?

程和光：不必，此时鲈鱼正肥美，我与那酒楼的后厨相熟，自带食材的话，花销并不会太高。
Cheng Heguang: No need. The chef there is a friend. They won't charge me much if I bring the ingredients myself. Bass is in season.

杜六：如果是小程巡检自己钓的，那我便通知弟兄们空着肚子等了。
Du Liu: Oh, you're bringing bass? I'll tell the men to skip lunch then.

杜六：“涣州鲈鱼王”的名号，今年还没易主吗？当年那条28斤的鲈鱼可真叫人眼馋。
Du Liu: Still the record holder of the Fishing Competition, aren't you? Who else but Chéng could pull up a bass half his size?

程和光：不过是钓着玩玩，顺带补贴家用……好了，执勤期间，不宜聊太多无关话题。
Cheng Heguang: Please, Dù Liù, it's just a way to make some extra wen. Right, enough talk. Back to work.

杜六：得嘞！那属下告退。
Du Liu: Yes, Chief Chéng! I'll take my leave then.

杜六退了出去，程和光便又将精力投回到了案卷之中。
He leaves, and the young officer returns to his files.

目所能及处，一切景象又烟雾般消散。
The mist rises again, covering the scene before her and then dissolving away.

芦草结已经习惯了这片黑暗。她等待着眼前重新亮起旅馆那扇推开的窗户。
The darkness is familiar now. She waits for the inn's open window to return to her sight.

芦草结：并不是惠姑……这风结里有多少人的往事？
他们都是当年的当事人？
Reed: That wasn't Mayfly's memory. How many people are involved in this story? Are they somehow connected to each other?

？？？：别急，我帮你一把。
???: Perhaps this will make things clearer.

芦草结：……！
Reed: ...!

风从她的身边呼啸而过，被牵引着汇往未知的远处。
Wind screams past her, pulling her again toward some distant, unknown place.

她的思绪先下沉，蔓延出无数根系，扎根于泥土。随后，又被一首童谣托起。
Her thoughts sink first, spreading like roots digging into the earth. Then, a nursery rhyme lifts them up.

SU-05 获释 / Free at Last

童声：黑绒出，小儿苦，良田千里遍尸骨。
Child: When black grass creeps, the children cry, a thousand fields where dead ones lie.

童声：冬雷吼，乌云布，地裂千里鬼哀哭。
Child: When thunder roars and dark clouds curl, the earth splits wide, the spirits swirl.

鹭鸶剪：嗯？这是涣州的地方歌谣吗？
Paper Heron: Hmm? A local rhyme from Huanzhou, isn't it?

班房内，鹭鸶剪竖着耳朵，饶有兴味地听着远处街道上传来的隐约童声，骡子则悠然嚼着铺在班房中的茅草。
In the cell, Paper Heron listens with interest to the distant children's voices. Her mule chews straw on the floor, unconcerned with their present state of affairs.

一边的惠姑尽力地踮着脚扒在班房小小的窗口上，显然没有这种好心情。
Beside her, Mayfly strains on her tiptoes at the small cell window, her face a contortion of overlapping anxieties.

惠姑：他们抓了好多小精怪进来，我一直在数着。就咱们进来这会儿，都有五个了。
Mayfly: It's only been a few hours since we came in, and they've already captured another five Yao. We're doomed.

惠姑垂头丧气地转过身来，靠在班房的土墙上。
She turns dejectedly and leans against the cell's earthen wall.

沉默了一会儿后，口袋里一直珍藏着的物件被她狠狠地扔在了地上。
After a moment of brooding silence, she yanks the once-cherished object from her pocket and flings it to the ground.

惠姑：骗子！骗子！
Mayfly: Liar! You wretched, dirty liar!

惠姑：说什么不会被振气铃影响，一点用都没有！还那么贵！
Mayfly: That merchant swore his trinket could fool the Reversion Bell, but it didn't. I spent all I had on it.

惠姑：害得我被那黄狗精连累……！我踩……我把你踩碎……！骗子！
Mayfly: And that wretched yellow dog. If it hadn't made such a scene, I might have slipped right past. I hate you. I hate you all!

惠姑：呜……我真是笨到家了……
Mayfly: *sob* I'm such a fool.

鹭鸶剪：别急别急，也许等会儿就能被放出去了呢。
Paper Heron: Now, now. They'll release us soon. We only need to wait.

鹭鸶剪笑盈盈地看着生气的惠姑，又看了看地上被踩碎的草结护符。
Paper Heron smiles, looking first at the distraught Mayfly, then toward the trampled cloverleaf amulet on the floor.

鹭鸶剪：嗯……这护符倒是有用，只不过是最初级的隐身护符，不念咒掐诀的话，对付振气铃倒用处不大。
Paper Heron: And, for the record, your amulet is not a fake. Its power is merely too weak to silence the Reversion Bell without a spell. It could be that the merchant forgot to tell you.

鹭鸶剪：那人也不算真的骗你，兴许只是没说清楚。
Paper Heron: You're no fool. No one's to blame.

惠姑：你，你还替他讲话？我都已经……到这了……
Mayfly: A-Are you defending him? D-Don't you see how miserable I am?

鹭鸶剪：哎呀，早晚会出去的嘛。他们又不可能关我们一辈子。
Paper Heron: Now, now, we'll be just fine. They can't keep us locked away forever.

鹭鸶剪捡起破碎的草结护符，念念有词了几句，擦了擦灰，递给惠姑。
She picks up the amulet while murmuring a few words, then dusts it off, and hands it back to Mayfly.

鹭鸶剪：留着吧，万一以后有用呢。
Paper Heron: Here, take this. Might prove useful.

惠姑：我才不要这玩意儿！
Mayfly: Get that away from me!

鹭鸶剪：好吧，那我收着。你别生气啦，他们还不知道我用一捆稻草替了你，等我脱身后，你也就可以进城啦。
Paper Heron: All right, all right, no need to fear. Remember that spell I cast on you? Now they'll see you as just a bundle of hay. I'll pick you up and take you with me when I'm freed.

惠姑：唉……早知道……我就不该来……
Mayfly: *sigh* I never should have come here.

这安慰显然于事无补，惠姑头上的草饰都耷拉了下来。
The offer does little to lift her spirits. The grass ornament in her hair droops over, matching her defeated expression.

鹭鸶剪则是专注地看起了班房角落的石头，仿佛世间一切纷扰与她无关。
Paper Heron, by contrast, seems completely unbothered by their predicament. Instead, her eyes are fixed on a stone in the corner of her cell.

好一会儿后，她忽地惊呼起来。
A moment passes before she lets out a cry of delight.

鹭鸶剪：成了！
Paper Heron: And done!

惠姑：什、什么成了？
Mayfly: W-What?

鹭鸶剪略微移步，露出了班房角落的一块石头。
Paper Heron moves in a flourish, presenting the stone to her companion.

上面正刻着“我与惠姑到此一游”。
It now bears a carving that reads, "Mayfly and Paper Heron were here."

鹭鸶剪：在这里闲着也是闲着，不如留个纪念。你看，我刻得如何？
Paper Heron: Well, there isn't much else to do cooped up in here. How do you like it, eh?

惠姑看向那还留有碎屑的石砖，字迹的凹陷处正贴合鹭鸶剪指尖的宽度。
Mayfly looks at the stone brick still dusted with debris. The grooves of the carving match the width of Paper Heron's finger.

惠姑：你……用手刻的？
Mayfly: Did you carve that with your nails?

鹭鸶剪：云游时收集到的小法术，隔空刻字。只是力道不好控制，总显得不够美观。你有什么想刻的吗？
Paper Heron: Haha, no. Just a little trick I picked up on the road—carving with air. Not mastered yet, mind you. Not exactly fit for the emperor, haha. Anything else you'd have me add?

惠姑：你的术法……就用来做这些？
Mayfly: That's all? That's what you use your arcane skills for?

鹭鸶剪：嗯？稍等，是我疏忽了。其实这术法不只能刻字……
Paper Heron: Hm? Of course not. I'm capable of much more than this.

鹭鸶剪保持着俯身的姿势，右手掐诀，指尖缠绕着一股凌冽白气，指尖缓缓在空中滑动，砖石上便一点点勾勒出一株苇草。
Bent over, Paper Heron makes a gesture with her right hand. As she does, a line of sharp white Qi wraps around her finger. As she begins moving her finger through the air, the form of a reed plant etches itself into the stone.

鹭鸶剪：还能刻图呢！这样后来的人，也知道我们来过。
Paper Heron: See? It's you! Quite the way to mark the moment, eh?

惠姑脸上的神情很难称之为高兴。
It doesn't seem to ease her new friend's concerns.

惠姑：鹭鸶剪，你刚刚还讲拿稻草替了我……这下他们看了字和图样，不就全露馅了吗？
Mayfly: Heron, no! You turned me into a bundle of hay, remember? They'll know it was me.

鹭鸶剪：啊——！大意了，我现在就把它擦了——
Paper Heron: Ah! You're right. I'll undo it at once.

鹭鸶剪：本来还想着，这至少能留个一万年呢！——不好，这下可露了大馅了……
Paper Heron: For a moment, I thought that our names might be here for all to see for the next ten thousand years, not mere minutes.

惠姑：等一下……
Mayfly: Wait.

惠姑轻轻地摇了摇头，制止了鹭鸶剪的动作。
She stops Paper Heron's hand with a firm shake of her head.

惠姑：……留着吧。
Mayfly: Leave it.

鹭鸶剪：嗯？
Paper Heron: Hmm?

惠姑：就像你讲的，留个纪念吧。如果一万年后还有一个人，知道我曾来过……
Mayfly: It'll be a keepsake, like you said. If someone a thousand years from now see it and know I was here ...

惠姑：那……也不错。
Mayfly: Well, that wouldn't be so bad.

她的声音中有一股难以察觉的悲伤。
Her voice seems to echo as if coming from some hollow void within her.

鹭鸶剪若有所思地看着惠姑，最终还是微笑地点了点头，没有抹去那小小的法术痕迹。
Paper Heron studies her young friend. Thoughts flutter across her eyes until she nods and smiles.

鹭鸶剪：好好……反正你别再着急啦。
Paper Heron: Very well. Now stop your fretting.

远处传来一阵急促的脚步。
A set of hurried footsteps comes from afar.

鹭鸶剪：他们来了！你现在别出声，我把你藏起来——
Paper Heron: They're coming. Hush. I'll slip you into my sleeve.

鹭鸶剪催动咒诀，惠姑就变成了一张纸人，柔顺地飞进了她的袖口。
Paper Heron utters an incantation. In an instant, Mayfly transforms into a paper figure that she slips into her sleeve.

杨武：程巡检，那道人就关在此处。
Yang Wu: Chief Chéng, she's in there.

程和光与杨武打开了牢门，走到了鹭鸶剪身前。
The two constables open the cell door, barging inside before coming to a stop directly in front of Paper Heron.

杨武：你说你是道士？可有度牒？
Yang Wu: You claimed to be a Daoist. Where's your certificate?

鹭鸶剪：齐全的。
Paper Heron: Here.

接过了度牒，程和光眉头紧皱，审视的目光在度牒、鹭鸶剪和骡子三者中挪移着。
The chief takes her certificate and furrows his brow as he reads. He looks from the certificate to Paper Heron and then to the mule.

杨武：签发年月竟在洪武年间？那距今岂不是已有百年？！
Yang Wu: Issued in the Hongwu era? That's over 100 years ago!

程和光：修道之人，看上去年轻些也不奇怪。
Cheng Heguang: Daoists cultivate themselves for longevity. It's only natural she looks younger than she is.

杨武难以置信地看着鹭鸶剪，而程和光则更加严谨地比对起度牒的细节。
Yáng Wǔ stares at Paper Heron in wide-mouthed disbelief, but the chief has already moved on from those minor details.

程和光：那在城门处败露真身的草本精怪，与你是什么关系？
Cheng Heguang: What is your relationship with the plant spirit that was revealed at the gate?

鹭鸶剪：小道与她不熟，只是在城门处碰巧遇到……我都不知道她原来还是精怪呢。
Paper Heron: I have no relationship with her at all. We simply happened to be in line at the same time. I didn't even know she was a Yao.

程和光没有接话，只是抬眼看了看鹭鸶剪，便又开始审视起度牒。
He does not reply but glances up at Paper Heron, then back at the certificate.

鹭鸶剪：莫不是我这度牒上还需带上那笨骡子的名字？
Paper Heron: Oh! Do I need a certificate for my mule too?

程和光：你那骡子也入了教门吗？
Cheng Heguang: Is your mule a Daoist?

鹭鸶剪：没有的。
Paper Heron: No.

程和光：那就不用写。
Cheng Heguang: Then no.

杨武：……这都什么和什么啊？
Yang Wu: Heh. What kind of interrogation is this?

比对许久，程和光终于将度牒交还给了鹭鸶剪。
Completing his check with a resigned nod, Chéng Héguāng returns the certificate to Paper Heron.

程和光：度牒没有问题，可以走了，但你下次若再惹起事端，肯定不会让你走得如此轻易。
Cheng Heguang: Certificate's clear. You may go, but don't make any more trouble, or there will be consequences.

鹭鸶剪：小道向来遵纪守法……
Paper Heron: Not to worry, officer. I always keep to the straight and narrow.

确认鹭鸶剪没有问题后，程和光的注意力便不再放在她的身上。
He shifts his focus from the woman to the nearby cell.

程和光：那草木精怪呢？
Cheng Heguang: Where's the plant spirit?

杨武：在隔壁，显出原型后，她便一直没有再恢复人形，估计是想以此躲避牢狱之灾……
Yang Wu: In the next cell. Hasn't turned back to her human form yet. I think she's playing dead.

二人便这样走向下一间班房，鹭鸶剪则忙不迭地拽着骡子离开这个幽暗潮湿的地方。
As the two men walk over to the next cell, Paper Heron leads her mule out from the dark, damp place.

鹭鸶剪：好啦，你活动活动腿脚，看看有什么不舒服的地方没有？
Paper Heron: Here we are, free once more. Feeling alright?

寻了个没人的地方，纸人从鹭鸶剪的袖中飘出，落在地上，并在一阵烟雾中变回了惠姑。
Finding a quiet spot, the paper figure drifts from Paper Heron's sleeve and, in a puff of smoke, returns Mayfly to her familiar form.

鹭鸶剪：如何？我就说一定能将你也救出来。
Paper Heron: Didn't I say that all would work out just fine?

惠姑：嗯——嗯——
Mayfly: Hmm. Mmm.

惠姑：变成纸人的感觉可真怪……听不真切，看得模糊……还动不得……
Mayfly: It's not much fun being a piece of paper. I couldn't see or hear much of anything, and my body was so flat.

惠姑：但我听到什么……洪武年间……？
Mayfly: I think I heard something about the Hongwu era?

鹭鸶剪：嘿嘿，我那度牒，算是个古董……万幸，那巡检比看起来好糊弄……
Paper Heron: Haha, my Daoist certificate, long expired. Fortunate for us, the constable was too dull to notice.

鹭鸶剪：对了，你之前说要进城做什么来着？可还来得及？
Paper Heron: Tell me, what do you plan to do in town? I hope our delay has not brought you trouble.

惠姑：这个啊……嗯……啊，你肚子饿吗，鹭鸶剪？
Mayfly: Well, ah, oh right, are you hungry, Heron?

惠姑指了指不远处的摊位。街上人群已多了起来，摊主的招揽之声也更加卖力了。
She points to a nearby stall. The street has swelled with people, and as the crowd grows, the stall owners call out all the louder for attention.

热气蒸腾的笼屉旁，已有不少人翘首以盼，惠姑也自然地加入了队列。
A line has formed around a set of steaming bamboo baskets. Mayfly slips into the crowd of eager customers.

惠姑：唉，一天都没吃东西了，早知道就吃一口你的清白盏了……
Mayfly: *sigh* I haven't eaten since this morning. I should've had that clear soup.

摊主Ⅰ：你们要的桂花糯米糕蒸好了喂，热烘烘，甜滋滋——
Stall Owner I: Here's your sweet olive cake, fresh from the steamer.

惠姑：好，谢谢——诶，好香的桂花啊。
Mayfly: Thank you. *sniff* Smells divine.

惠姑迫不及待地咬下去，一股清甜软熟的香气四溢开来，她忍不住发出一句幸福的叹气。
She cannot wait and takes a bite. A soft, sweet scent fills the air, and a sigh of pure contentment follows.

惠姑：呼——真是，真是太好吃了……呜呜……
Mayfly: Mm, mm. It's ... It's so good.

鹭鸶剪：真有这么好吃？
Paper Heron: Really? It's only cake.

惠姑：很甜、很糯，很……总，总之，鹭鸶剪你也试试吧！
Mayfly: I can't help it. It's sweet, tender, chewy. You must try it.

惠姑笑着递给鹭鸶剪一块略有些烫手的桂花糯米糕，鹭鸶剪左看右看，最后轻轻放入口中。
She smiles and hands Paper Heron a sweet olive cake, still hot to the touch. Paper Heron looks it over, then delicately lifts it to her mouth.

惠姑：怎……怎么样？好吃吗？
Mayfly: So? So? Isn't it wonderful?

鹭鸶剪：唔，唔……口感很奇妙……
Paper Heron: Mmm. Hmm. The texture is quite remarkable.

鹭鸶剪努力地嚼着桂花糕，似乎正在寻找着那传说中的滋味。
She chews with effort, searching for the vaunted taste within.

鹭鸶剪：好像……
Paper Heron: Mmm. I think ...

惠姑：好像什么？
Mayfly: What? What??

她看着惠姑那幸福地嚼着桂花糕的模样，不自觉地模仿着对方，那桂花糕似乎也尝出了味道。
She watches Mayfly as she chews, each bite meeting waves of rapture, and attempts to mimic her delight. Somehow, the act of imitation seems to conjure the promised flavors.

鹭鸶剪：好像……还挺甜的，嗯，确实越吃越香甜啦！
Paper Heron: I think it's sweet, and it grows sweeter and sweeter the more I chew.

惠姑：我就说！
Mayfly: Right?

鹭鸶剪：好吃，好吃，我得再多吃几口，惠姑你也多吃点……
Paper Heron: Mmm. It's good, delicious. I must get some more. Mm. Here, eat up, Mayfly.

摊主Ⅰ：看你们风尘仆仆，应该也是慕名来参加这次庙会的吧。
Stall Owner I: You two must be visitors. Are you here for the fair?

鹭鸶剪：嗝……是啊，看今年的庙会办得特别大，特别好玩。
Paper Heron: *burp* That's right. Heard it would be quite the spectacle.

摊主Ⅰ：也是拜了那个“谣言”的福，今年我们这些做小本生意的也赚了不少钱。
Stall Owner I: It certainly will be. And thanks to that rumor, business is going great this year.

鹭鸶剪：只有今年？
Paper Heron: What makes this year so special, hm?

摊主Ⅰ：嗯……这几年，这个教那个教的，其实都在附近城里兴盛过，追求的都是长生成仙之类的。
Stall Owner I: Well, many religious sects have flourished in Zhu County recently, each one claiming to bring longevity to their followers. All just tall tales, of course.

摊主Ⅰ：不过，今年可不一般喽……客官，我也是听说的，您就当听个乐子。今年庙会本就办得隆重，大家都传，是因为有富商老爷求到真的仙人了。
Stall Owner I: Only this time is different. Well, it's hearsay. But many think the reason the fair is so busy this year is that one of the sponsors found a true immortal.

惠姑：这件事我也听过……我朋友的朋友的朋友的亲戚，早该在几年前就寿终正寝，但他今年却突然回家了，说自己在祝县受了仙人点拨，才活到现在。
Mayfly: I heard that too. My friend said her friend's grandfather, who'd been buried, suddenly came home alive, saying he was enlightened by an immortal in Zhu County.

摊主Ⅰ：据说呐，今晚的戏就是那群富商老爷给仙人办的“入世典仪”呢，那戏台的规模都比往常大个好几倍。
Stall Owner I: And they say tonight's opera is in fact an opening ceremony for the immortal's sect. They've even widened the stage.

鹭鸶剪：啊……这么厉害啊！
Paper Heron: Ah. Sounds impressive.

摊主Ⅰ：而且，这些捕风捉影暂且不说，你就说那些个官差，往年传啥他们都没什么反应，今年却如临大敌一般，我看啊，这事……
Stall Owner I: And not just that. Have you noticed the constables? I've never seen them so nervous. I'd say ...

鹭鸶剪：嗯——可是听来听去，全是听说和猜测，到现在都没个实影……眼不见为虚，倒不是很有意思。
Paper Heron: Hmm. But these are mere fancies. Is there nothing we can see with our own eyes?

摊主Ⅰ：想有意思？去看高跷巡神啊。
Stall Owner I: Certainly, the Stilted Parade.

惠姑：高跷巡神！
Mayfly: Oh, the Stilted Parade.

鹭鸶剪：就是你路上总说的那个？
Paper Heron: The event you mentioned on the way here, isn't it?

惠姑：对！听讲热闹得紧。在哪里能看呢？
Mayfly: Yes! I heard it's great fun. Where can we see it?

摊主Ⅰ：马上就来了。
Stall Owner I: Right behind you.

店主盖上了蒸笼，闪身走到了店铺之中，于门后消失了踪影。
The stall owner closes the steamer and slips back into the storefront.

街上不知何时失去了热闹的氛围，路人倏地都不见了，一股诡异的氛围如沉雾般从街头蔓延了过来。
It's only now that they realize how quiet the street had become. Not a soul in sight, until a strange, dense bank of perfumed air rolls past them.

惠姑：嗯？
Mayfly: Hmm?

SU-06 忧患实多 / Deadly Cure

天阴沉了下来，幽幽地有吟诵之声，惠姑好奇地向街道尽头望去。
The sky grows dim above them. A low, haunting chant drifts up into the air. Curious, Mayfly looks toward the end of the street.

惠姑：好像……有许多人过来了……
Mayfly: Oh, right, the parade's coming.

浩浩汤汤，人影幢幢，惠姑尽可能地探过身子去。
A crowded wave of people surges into view from the distance. Mayfly cranes her neck, straining to see.

吟咏之声：黑绒吞白骨，寒原鬼泣呜。
Chant: Withered grass devours bone. On icy plain the spirits moan.

吟咏之声：城覆仙人现，长生免祸殃。
Chant: When the city falls, the Immortal descends. Longevity granted, no death, no end.

宛如天神出游一般，吟诵之声远远传来，一队巨人踏着方步靠近着，细看才发现他们脚下踩着细长的高跷。
The unearthly parade advances; a line of towering figures leads its approach in long, otherworldly strides. It takes a moment to spot the stilts as they push against the fabric with each step.

惠姑：他们在唱什么？
Mayfly: What are they singing?

女子Ⅰ：黑绒吞白骨，寒原鬼泣呜。
Woman I: Withered grass devours bone. On icy plain the spirits moan.

惠姑：怎么……
Mayfly: What is ...

游行的队伍已至眼前，吟唱之声如天音般从惠姑的头顶灌了下去。
The parade is near. Their chanting pours over Mayfly like a flood of divine music.

扮神的演员Ⅰ：城覆仙人现，长生免祸殃。
"Immortal" I: When the city falls, the Immortal descends. Longevity granted, no death, no end.

众路人：城覆仙人现，长生免祸殃。
All: When the city falls, the Immortal descends. Longevity granted, no death, no end.

不知何时，一只狐妖和一名女子已来到了惠姑的身边，趴在她耳边厮磨着。
A fox and a woman have appeared over Mayfly's shoulder. Their hushed voices brushing against her ear.

女子Ⅰ：我们虽弱小，却也不能总叫人踩在头上。我们一只妖力量小，合起来难道还会小吗！
Woman I: We sit at the bottom of society, but still, we deserve dignity. One Yao's voice may not be heard, but what of a hundred or even a thousand more?

惠姑：你、你们是谁？想干什么？
Mayfly: W-Who are you? What do you want?

狐妖：我们都是妖，你也是。
Fox: Same as you, we are Yao.

狐妖：你难道不曾看见他们是如何驱赶、杀戮我们？这样的日子，你要忍到何时？
Fox: You've seen them bat us off, even kill us, haven't you? Will you continue to suffer in silence? Will you live on in fear?

女子Ⅰ：杀出去，我们一起杀出去，把同族救出来，去求那长生之法，再凌驾于人类之上！
Woman I: We need to fight. Fight for our lives! Save our people and claim the Method of Longevity for our own! Overthrow humans and rule the world!

狐妖：走啊，走吧！横竖都是死！拖他们一起死！
Fox: Come, join us! If we are doomed, then we will doom them with us!

惠姑：不、我、我……
Mayfly: No. I-I ...

惠姑本能地想向旁人寻求帮助，才发觉自己竟身处一片迷雾中。
She looks around, hoping to find help, only to realize she is surrounded by thick billows of scented fog.

女子Ⅰ：非我族类，其心必异。
Woman I: Those that are not with us are the enemy.

女子Ⅰ：他们可有怜惜你的命？你为何怜惜他们的？
Woman I: Did they ever show you mercy? Then, why hesitate?

白色的绒毛从她的鼻尖冒了出来，她看起来是只兔妖。
White fur sprouts from her nose, revealing the Yao to be a hare.

她的脚跺得如战鼓一般，其余精怪见了她的模样，面面相觑一阵后，竟有了加入的趋势。
Her feet begin to stamp like war drums. The other Yao watch, then look at one another. All of them feeling the pull to join in.

兔妖：仙人将授予我长生！
Hare: The Immortal will grant us longevity!

众精怪：仙人将授予我长生！
All Yao: The Immortal will grant us longevity!

精怪Ⅰ：不好！巡捕来了！
Yao I: Constables! Run!

惠姑：什么？
Mayfly: What?

游行的队伍突然如烟般消失在巷口，连同那吟唱的乐声一起，仿佛从未来过。
As they round the mouth of the alley, the parade vanishes as quickly as it appeared. The chanting music fades like smoke in the air.

鹭鸶剪：到这儿应该就没事了，你刚才被游行的队伍施了幻术之法，听不见我的声音。
Paper Heron: Mayfly? Can you hear me? You were caught in the parade's illusion. I had to lead you away.

惠姑：我……我没事了。但它们，它们都是追求长生的精怪……
Mayfly: I-I'm alright now. Those Yao—they're seeking longevity.

鹭鸶剪：是啊。
Paper Heron: Yes.

鹭鸶剪：可它们现在干的可不是追求长生，是在害人。
Paper Heron: But what they're doing is a risk to our entire community.

惠姑垂下头去，脸越涨越红。最后，她像是下定什么决心一样跺了跺脚。
Mayfly looks down, her face turning red. Finally deciding something, she stamps her foot.

惠姑：鹭鸶剪，谢谢你帮我进城。我这一路上受了你不少照顾，却一直在骗你……我……
Mayfly: Paper Heron, thank you for bringing me here. I owe you much, so I don't want to lie anymore. I ...

鹭鸶剪歪了歪头，真诚而略有些疑惑地看着眼前的女孩。
Paper Heron tilts her head, looking puzzled but relieved.

鹭鸶剪：有这回事吗？
Paper Heron: Lie about what?

惠姑：你也看到了，我的真身就是一株苇草，和它们一样的精怪。
Mayfly: You know my true form is a tuft of reed. I'm a Yao, just like the others in the parade.

惠姑：这番想方设法地进城，也是为了那个仙人授长生的传言。我先前不答，是有点羞于提及……希望你理解。
Mayfly: In truth, the reason I came all this way is to seek the Method of Longevity. I lied because, well, I feared you'd hate me. I'm sorry.

惠姑：但，但我并不想害人！我只是想自己活下去……活得……久一点……
Mayfly: But I don't want to hurt anyone. I just wanna live longer. Even a little would do.

鹭鸶剪：你别急，我并不介怀这些，倒是你……
Paper Heron: Hush. You'll hear no judgment from me. Only, I don't understand.

鹭鸶剪：县里查得这么严，你冒着这么大的风险也要来参加这个庙会，追求长生对你来说，这么重要？
Paper Heron: You risked a lifetime of confinement on a rumor. Is longevity really so important to you?

惠姑：……
Mayfly: ...

惠姑一时间收了声。片刻后，她垂下眼去。
She goes quiet for a moment, then looks down.

惠姑：这一路来，我们遇到的人……抑或妖，只要听到长生之法，多少都会提起一些兴趣。
Mayfly: Remember the travelers we met on the way here? Human or Yao, all sought the Method of Longevity.

惠姑：你却始终更好奇一些我们司空见惯的东西，不急不躁，好像那法门对你而言，还抵不上路边买的桂花糕。
Mayfly: But you're different. You care more for the small joys in life, like that sweet olive cake we shared.

惠姑：你又为何能不在乎长生呢？
Mayfly: It's almost as if you don't care about how long you'll live at all.

鹭鸶剪：我……
Paper Heron: Ah ...

鹭鸶剪：不是的，我只是想多看看，多尝尝。
Paper Heron: I'm not so unlike you. I suppose I'm just curious about everything.

鹭鸶剪：都进了城，也不忙这一时半刻的……而且这么纯正的桂花糕，别处还吃不到呢！
Paper Heron: We're already here. Why hurry? If we'd missed that cake, we'd have regretted it for the rest of our lives.

鹭鸶剪搔搔头，有些无措地解释着。
Paper Heron scratches her head as she tries to explain; words rest on her tongue, but they feel, like her, suddenly out of place.

惠姑：……
Mayfly: ...

惠姑：唉，你这人。
Mayfly: *sigh* You win.

她拍了拍裙面，叹了一口气。
She brushes her skirt and sighs.

惠姑：让你见笑了，别放在心上。我不该这样问你的。
Mayfly: Sorry, I shouldn't have been so suspicious of you.

惠姑：草木有灵，循灵而生。我们能习得术法，化为人形，但终究需得顺应大道，逃不过原定的命数。
Mayfly: Though we study arcanum and can take human shapes, we Yao are still just plants and animals. Even if we look like you, our lives are much shorter.

惠姑：像我这样的苇草，春生冬死，拢共不过活上一年。
Mayfly: Reeds like me sprout in spring and wither in winter. My entire life begins and ends in less than a year.

惠姑：虽然我追寻这长生之法像是病急乱投医，但……只要是医，也算有个念想。
Mayfly: I know it's foolish to risk so much on a rumor, but it's all I have.

惠姑：我也只是想要以后看到日落的时候，能当它是又有一天过去了，而不是……想到我的寿命又少一天了。
Mayfly: Do you know what I think when the sun sets? Not that the sky is lovely, but that I lost another day. I don't want to live in fear anymore.

鹭鸶剪：可是为了买那号称能骗过振气铃的护符，就几近耗尽了你全部身家吧。
Paper Heron: But you spent all you had on that amulet.

鹭鸶剪：万一这长生之法是个骗局，你岂不是会一无所有？
Paper Heron: What if the Method of Longevity proves false? You'll have nothing left.

惠姑低着头笑了笑，随后定定地望向鹭鸶剪。
Mayfly smiles, but she lets her eyes stay downcast for a moment before they rise to meet her own.

惠姑：长生之法的意义对你我来说是不一样的，对你来说是锦上添花，对我来说却性命攸关。
Mayfly: Longevity means much more to me than you, Heron. When the winter ends, you will see the spring, and I won't.

惠姑：这是能“鲤鱼跃龙门”的仙法，当然值得我倾尽所有。
Mayfly: If the Method is true, it will change everything. I have to take the chance, no matter the cost.

惠姑：而且，我的“所有”，其实也就是我的一条贱命罢了。
Mayfly: And as you said yourself, I have nothing left to lose.

鹭鸶剪看着惠姑的眼睛，晚霞映进了那双黑漆漆的眸子里，看起来似乎正燃烧着什么。
They share a long gaze. Paper Heron reads the dark eyes before her. They seem to burn like unsettled coal.

鹭鸶剪：……你——
Paper Heron: Mayfly ...

潇洒自由惯了的道人一时怔怔无语，正想说些什么，意外却突然袭来。
The usually free-spirited Daoist is, for a moment, speechless. She intends to speak, but then the unexpected strikes.

严肃的男声：守备！
Serious Male Voice: Commander!

男子的声音突然从拐角处传出，打断了鹭鸶剪。
The familiar voice comes from around the corner, seizing her train of thought.

鹭鸶剪：嗯？
Paper Heron: Hmm?

程和光：守备，属下有要事禀报。
Cheng Heguang: Commander, I come with an urgent report.

SU-07 各西东 / Separate Ways

鹭鸶剪：嘘，有人来啦，你再委屈一会儿！
Paper Heron: Shush! Someone's here. Get in my sleeve.

鹭鸶剪拍了拍骡屁股，那骡子哞叫两声，慢悠悠躲在一旁的草垛后面了。
Paper Heron gives the mule's rump a light slap. It brays as it ambles behind a nearby haystack.

接着，她贴身靠着墙，望向那两个巡捕模样的人。
She presses close to the wall and peers out at the two men. One familiar, the other unfamiliar and bearing greater authority.

程和光：厉守备。
Cheng Heguang: Commander Lì.

厉晦锋：这么急三火四地把我叫过来，什么事？
Li Huifeng: Such hurried words, Chéng. What's the matter?

程和光：属下得到线报，这里刚刚出现了一支奇怪的游行队伍，还带领在场的县民齐声吟诵怪异的口号。
Cheng Heguang: It's concerning an unusual parade that has been seen moving through the town. The marchers chanted strange words and even tempted townsfolk to join their ranks.

程和光：但巡捕到场之后，他们就离奇消失了。全县范围内，类似的案件已经发生过三起，这是第四起了。
Cheng Heguang: But they vanished as soon as our men arrived. This is the fourth such incident in as many weeks.

厉晦锋：然后？
Li Huifeng: Go on.

程和光：他们出现时，有时会在附近留下动物遗尸，我已命下属去搜寻了，兴许一会儿便能找到。
Cheng Heguang: Sometimes they leave animal carcasses in their wake. I've ordered a search. Our men may discover something soon.

程和光：这些动物尸体死相诡异，不像是被捕杀或自然死亡，更像是死于某种宗教仪式。
Cheng Heguang: These animals are unusual. They bear no marks of either hunting or natural death. It appears to be some sort of ritual slaughter.

程和光：正巧那游行队伍总在散播“长生之法”的流言，已有不少县民被其蛊惑，属下担心……
Cheng Heguang: They're the ones that have been spreading those rumors about the Method of Longevity. Many townsfolk have joined with them. I fear ...

厉晦锋：也就是说，你想抽调现在最吃紧的城防人力，去盘查一桩民间小教的装神弄鬼之事。
Li Huifeng: You would have me redirect men that already stretched thin to chase down a parade.

厉晦锋：而他们除了遗弃动物尸体外，还未有伤人传言。
Li Huifeng: Which, so far, has done little more than leave a few dead animals behind. Do I understand you correctly?

程和光：……
Cheng Heguang: ...

程和光耳尖通红，他似乎想说些什么，但最终只是嗫嚅了两下，什么也没说。
Chéng Héguāng's face turns red. He wants to say something, but the words come out in a fluster.

程和光：但属下认为，这桩案子和“高跷巡神”有莫大的——
Cheng Heguang: All of these events are linked together with the Stilted Parade, and—

厉晦锋：和光，你可还记得你在“高跷巡神”期间领的差事是什么？
Li Huifeng: Héguāng, what are the orders I've given you?

程和光：维护好县内的治安，严加盘诘，不许奸宄混入，让百姓们过个好节。
Cheng Heguang: To maintain order, keep criminals from the county, and to see our people enjoy the fair in safety.

厉晦锋：你觉得你做得如何？
Li Huifeng: And how do you judge your performance?

程和光：守备，属下一刻都未松懈过。
Cheng Heguang: I have done my utmost, Commander.

厉晦锋：但我听说，城门那边不太安分啊。
Li Huifeng: Yet there was a disturbance at the gate.

程和光：……属下无可辩驳。
Cheng Heguang: I cannot deny it.

厉晦锋：“高跷巡神”是万民同庆的盛会，百姓辛勤整年，就指着这些个节日来寄托来年的盼头。
Li Huifeng: The Stilted Parade is the most significant event of the year, an opportunity for people to laugh and be merry after a year of hard work.

厉晦锋：让他们放心玩乐，本就是我们这些巡捕的职责。
Li Huifeng: It's our duty to maintain peace so that they may enjoy the festival.

厉晦锋：这段时间，周围的百姓齐齐涌入祝县，巡防弹压的人力已吃紧万分。
Li Huifeng: But with all the visitors flooding into the county, we are already short on men.

厉晦锋：县内的捕头们因守夜巡街，已有三天轮班倒，连回家换身衣服的时间都没有。
Li Huifeng: You know well that they have been working day and night. Many haven't seen their own homes in days.

程和光：……我知道，守备。
Cheng Heguang: I know, Commander.

厉晦锋：那你为何不去疏解城门的压力，不去检修那庙会街的古桥——
Li Huifeng: No, you do not. While your men are out dealing with these visitors and all their other duties—

厉晦锋：却想抽出人手去调查那个所谓的谣言，只因为你捕风捉影的怀疑？
Li Huifeng: You come to ask that I direct them to another task based on groundless suspicions?

程和光：……属下知错。
Cheng Heguang: My apologies, Commander.

厉晦锋：唉，不必如此。和光，你是太心焦了。
Li Huifeng: *sigh* Raise your head. Listen. You are pushing yourself too hard, Héguāng.

程和光：……
Cheng Heguang: ...

程和光低头不答，原本严厉的守备见此，口气便放软了一点。
Noticing his protégé's dejected silence, the stern commander softens his tone, if only ever-so-slightly.

厉晦锋：这也不怪你。我知道，你比谁都更想立功。
Li Huifeng: I know how eager you are to prove yourself. Any man in your position would be.

厉晦锋：我是和你说过，因为你父亲的事，你未来的路不会好走，必须付出比其他人多十倍、百倍的努力。
Li Huifeng: And I know it was I who told you to work ten or a hundred times harder to earn your place, given your father's history.

厉晦锋：但你也不能太操之过急。
Li Huifeng: But true diligence must rest in stability. There are no shortcuts.

厉晦锋：这一路上，会有很多双眼睛盯着你。要想出人头地，洗刷耻辱，你得做到任何人都挑不出一个错处才行。
Li Huifeng: Many eyes are on you, Héguāng. If you truly wish to wash your family name of its dishonor, let them find no fault in you.

厉晦锋：既然你领了这差事，就先尽好本分。谁都是这样过来的。
Li Huifeng: Do your duty first, then take the next step. That is how things are done.

程和光：属下明白。
Cheng Heguang: I understand.

程和光仍是低头。厉晦锋想了想，清了清嗓子。
He keeps his face pointed down, averting his commander's stare. Lì Huìfēng thinks for a moment and clears his throat.

厉晦锋：咳，和光啊。由匪入兵，本是一件好事。你父亲会回去与匪类混迹，不代表你也会。
Li Huifeng: Ahem. Your father disgraced himself when he threw his lot in with those bandits, but that does not mean you will follow his path.

厉晦锋：有时一些闲话，不必太过在意。
Li Huifeng: You must not let the whispers of others shake your heart.

厉晦锋：当初把你招来时，我就看出，以你的脾性，稍加琢磨，便能成为一个还祝县清净的好巡检。
Li Huifeng: Do you remember why I recruited you? Because I saw a young man with the integrity and conviction to truly protect people.

厉晦锋：现在我仍这么想。
Li Huifeng: I still do.

厉晦锋拍了拍程和光的肩膀，随即将手背了回去。
Lì Huìfēng pats the young officer on the shoulder, then returns his hands stiffly behind his back.

厉晦锋：只要你不懈努力，有朝一日定能青云直上，洗刷你们程家的污名。
Li Huifeng: Héguāng, your future is bright. Work hard, and you will surely rise to the top, and your family name will be cleared.

程和光：……是。
Cheng Heguang: Understood.

厉晦锋：那我便走了，你好好想想吧。
Li Huifeng: I have other matters to attend to. Think carefully on my words.

程和光：守备慢走。
Cheng Heguang: I will, Commander.

从墙边望去，只见那年轻的巡检久久的立在墙边，如一尊木雕。
Watching from the wall, Paper Heron sees the young man standing motionless. For a moment, he seems so stiff that he could be a wood carving.

鹭鸶剪：不是都聊完了吗？他怎么还不走？
Paper Heron: The other one's left. What's he waiting for, hm?

程和光：……
Cheng Heguang: ...

程和光忽然抬起脚，狠狠地踢开了脚下的石子。
Suddenly, Chéng Héguāng lifts his foot and kicks a pebble away.

骡子：咴？！
Mule: Whinny?

程和光：谁？
Cheng Heguang: Who's there?

骡子：咴——？！
Mule: Whinny?

登时间，百枚树叶化作剑刃飞来，将骡子围了个大概。
Meeting the sound with calm and precise motion, he summons a hundred leaves that circle the mule; in that same instant, they take on a fearsome steel glint.

鹭鸶剪：啊哦！这可糟了。
Paper Heron: Uh-oh!

鹭鸶剪：你先走，惠姑，我不能丢下这烦人骡子不管。
Paper Heron: You go ahead, Mayfly. I can't leave that stupid mule behind.

鹭鸶剪左手拈起变成纸人的惠姑，右手掐了个解咒的诀。随后，她轻轻吹了一口气，纸人便飘向远方。
She picks up Mayfly's paper form with her left hand. With her right, she makes a gesture to break the incantation, then breathes a soft puff of air that sends her floating away.

看着纸人飘出巷外，鹭鸶剪便跳将上旁边的榆树顶，用叶子遮起了自己的身影。
Paper Heron watches as her friend drifts out of reach before leaping to the top of a nearby elm and hiding among the leaves.

街道上顿时只剩下了一人一骡。
Now only one man and one mule remain.

骡子：咴——
Mule: Bray—

程和光：哼……是那道人的骡子。
Cheng Heguang: Hmph. That Daoist must be around.

程和光：地上只有一串脚印断在了这里，人呢？
Cheng Heguang: But her trail ends here. Where did she go?

程和光看了看四周，装作要对那骡子发难，旁边的榆树顶忽然传来一丝波动的气息。
Chéng Héguāng looks around. He feigns an attack on the mule but stops mid-gesture as he catches a ripple of air from the elm tree above him.

眨眼间，鹭鸶剪便身处于榆树叶化作的叶刃阵中。
In a flash, Paper Heron stands amidst a newly formed ring of elm-leaf blades.

程和光：哪里跑！
Cheng Heguang: You won't get away!

鹭鸶剪：哎哟哟！这可失算了！
Paper Heron: Oops! Should've been more careful.

鹭鸶剪：呼、呼……官……官爷好脚力！
Paper Heron: Huff, huff. You surely can run, officer.

程和光：呵、呵……
Cheng Heguang: *panting*

程和光：你这偷听的邪道……着实难对付。
Cheng Heguang: Why were you eavesdropping, you conniving Daoist?

鹭鸶剪：官爷定是误会了什么，小道只想寻一个清净处——
Paper Heron: You must be mistaken, sir. I merely happened to be there.

程和光：上午扰乱城门秩序，下午就做了偷听的贼人，这世间哪有这么多凑巧？
Cheng Heguang: You happened to be there, did you? After making a scene at the gate this morning? Do you think me born yesterday?

鹭鸶剪：哎呀呀，这，现下跟你确实有些说不通……
Paper Heron: Ugh, is there any worth in explaining? You're being unreasonable.

程和光：那便跟我的刀说去——！
Cheng Heguang: You can explain in the interrogation room!

跃上屋顶的一瞬之间，鹭鸶剪迅速捡起一根粗细均匀的树枝，以抵挡来自身后的攻击。
Paper Heron jumps onto the roof and seizes a straight, even branch, blocking an attack from behind.

鹭鸶剪：诶诶诶，刀剑无眼！小心别伤着人了。
Paper Heron: Hey, hey, hey! Your blade's sharp! I might have been hurt!

程和光：少在这里装腔作势，你压根不怕我的刀，问心无愧的话就跟我回衙门！
Cheng Heguang: Hmph. My blade is no threat to you! If you have nothing to hide, stop this now and follow me to the Yamen!

鹭鸶剪：回衙门倒是无妨……但我有个不情之请。
Paper Heron: Very well, on one condition.

程和光：讲。
Cheng Heguang: What?

鹭鸶剪一听，眼睛便亮了亮，颇急切地开了口。
At that, Paper Heron's eyes light up as she launches into an eager explanation.

鹭鸶剪：我那骡子，自打上次踏过山溪崴了脚，就走不快了。
Paper Heron: My mule's been limping since it twisted its ankle in the mountain.

鹭鸶剪：看你轻功好不错，回头我跟你走了，能否教教我的骡子？我总嫌它慢了些。
Paper Heron: Could you teach it how to run? I think with a little training, you could make a champion out of it.

程和光：你！
Cheng Heguang: You ...

惊慌的声音：程巡检！程巡检！
Panicked Voice: Chief! Chief!

杨武：程巡检！城门那边出乱子了！辛苦您快些过来啊！
Yang Wu: There's another disturbance at the gate! Come, quickly!

鹭鸶剪：哦？
Paper Heron: Oh?

程和光惊异望去，杨武正站在街上抓耳挠腮，而再看向鹭鸶剪，她也停了下来，跟自己保持着几丈的距离。
Chéng Héguāng looks over in surprise to find Yáng Wǔ standing in the street, scratching his head, and then back to Paper Heron, who has stopped a short distance away.

鹭鸶剪：你瞧，不良方士另有其人。
Paper Heron: Told you I'm not the one you should be chasing.

程和光：又是城门，我看定是你的同伙作乱！
Cheng Heguang: The gate again! Your accomplices, no doubt!

程和光提气向鹭鸶剪追去，鹭鸶剪施施然地退后相同的距离。
He surges forward on a burst of Qi in pursuit of Paper Heron. Yet, with unhurried ease, she drifts back, maintaining her distance precisely.

程和光：可恨！
Cheng Heguang: Enough!

只见程和光挽了个刀花，整树树叶便化为利刃。
Chéng Héguāng spins his blade, and all the leaves on the tree become sharp edges.

嗡鸣声中，鹭鸶剪被这利刃结结实实钉在了墙上。
A humming noise fills the air as the sharp leaves pin Paper Heron against the wall.

鹭鸶剪：咦——
Paper Heron: Huh?

程和光：守备吩咐过，城门处断不能出什么乱子。
Cheng Heguang: I can't let another disturbance reach Commander Lì.

程和光：我且先把你拘在这里，等我平息骚乱，再将你的同伙与你一齐领回衙门。
Cheng Heguang: You stay here. I will take you and your accomplices to the Yamen on my return.

鹭鸶剪：官爷放心，小道我说话算话。
Paper Heron: Not to worry, officer. I'll stay right where I am.

鹭鸶剪：实在不放心，我那宝贝骡子还在这儿，你尽可以让别人看着，骡在我在。
Paper Heron: Take my mule if you mistrust me. You know I won't leave it behind.

鹭鸶剪朝底下那慢悠悠的骡子努了努嘴，程和光看了看，那骡子吭哧地叫了一声。
Paper Heron nods toward the limping mule below. He looks down to it. As if waiting for that cue, the mule brays out a greeting.

他再回头，看鹭鸶剪安静地不再挣扎，便冷哼一声，擒刀跃下了屋顶。
He looks back to Paper Heron, pinned yet completely serene. He snorts, sheaths his blade, and jumps down from the roof.

程和光：我懒与你作口舌之争！
Cheng Heguang: Hmph. There's no time to waste.

街道的冷清一角，惠姑正踮着脚四处张望。
In a quiet corner of the street, Mayfly stands on her tiptoes, peering around.

鹭鸶剪：你来啦。
Paper Heron: Hey, Mayfly.

惠姑小心翼翼地看着周围，即使空无一人，她还是踮着脚轻轻地跑了过来。
Finding no one, she darts forward still on her tiptoes.

惠姑：鹭鸶剪，我用了点小戏法把他引走啦。
Mayfly: Are you alright? I played a trick at the gate to distract him.

鹭鸶剪：多谢。
Paper Heron: Much appreciated.

鹭鸶剪：呼——
Paper Heron: *blow*

惠姑：你……这就把它们都弄掉啦？
Mayfly: Wow! You blew those off like dust.

鹭鸶剪：这有什么。
Paper Heron: It's not as hard as you imagine.

鹭鸶剪松了松筋骨，惠姑看着那些叮当落地的叶刃，眼中生起一丝欣羡。
Paper Heron stretches while Mayfly watches the leaf blades fall in a clatter. A hint of envy shines in her eyes.

惠姑：还好你没事……我就知道虽然你平时分不清东南西北，但关键时候自有神通。
Mayfly: I knew you'd work things out. Your mastery of arcanum is truly amazing, even if you lose your way sometimes.

惠姑：不像我，连应对振气铃都做不到……
Mayfly: I wish I could be like you.

惠姑：要是我哪天也能像你一样，能隐身掐诀，应对刀兵，畅快地游走天地就好了……
Mayfly: Wandering the world, fighting and casting spells, saving my friends from danger ...

鹭鸶剪：说的什么话。你看，你解了我的围，我也解了你的围，咱们现在不也很畅快吗？
Paper Heron: Nonsense! You just saved me from the clutches of the constables, didn't you? Our lives shine equally bright.

鹭鸶剪：如果你想学这些方术神通，我可以教你，只要你愿意学，可好？
Paper Heron: Ah, but I know what you mean. You want to learn some of my tricks, eh? I can teach you.

惠姑：唉……我不是指这个，就算我想学，时间也……
Mayfly: *sigh* No, that's not what I mean. Besides, there isn't time.

惠姑摇了摇头，及时止住了一个无法沟通的话题。
With a shake of her head, Mayfly swallows the words. They would have been pointless.

惠姑：不说这些有的没的了，鹭鸶剪，其实我要走啦。
Mayfly: Actually, Heron, I must say farewell.

鹭鸶剪：走？
Paper Heron: Farewell? Why?

惠姑：嗯……困在城门的时候，我本想报答一下你路上的照顾就走的。
Mayfly: Well, I'd planned this even before we entered town. Would've gone sooner if not for being caught.

鹭鸶剪：你又要去哪里，不是要学“长生之法”吗？
Paper Heron: But where will you go? I thought you were seeking the Method of Longevity.

惠姑：呃……我不去哪里，只是去找城里的同族，原本……嗯，我也是这么打算的。毕竟，我们草本精怪待在一起总是自在些。
Mayfly: I'm not leaving, just off to find some other herbaceous Yao. You know, plants of a leaf, same belief.

鹭鸶剪：好，我理解了。
Paper Heron: I understand.

鹭鸶剪点了点头。
She nods, but there's a strange tug of emotion within it.

惠姑：唉，虽然你道法高强，但我总觉得你哪里缺根弦。快要分别了，我反倒要担心你。
Mayfly: *sigh* But I worry for you already. For all your wonderful abilities, you're just so careless.

鹭鸶剪：不必不必，我看这里的人都挺好的，本事也好。
Paper Heron: Don't you worry about me. I'll be fine. Haven't met any rotten folk in this town thus far.

鹭鸶剪：有你，有好糊弄的巡检，还有那卖桂花糕的老板娘……嗯，游行的小妖也不错，只是不抱伤人之心便更好了。
Paper Heron: Let me see. There's you, that gullible constable, the cake seller, and the Yao from the parade. Well, I saw through their tricks. You see, I can take care of myself.

惠姑：哈哈，这些都是稀松平常的人和事啊……
Mayfly: Heh. You make it sound like a tale for the ages.

惠姑最后还想说什么，但看鹭鸶剪神色如常，便也不再多言。
She wants to say more, but at the sight of Paper Heron's calm composure, she stops herself.

惠姑：照，那……我们有缘再见吧。
Mayfly: Right. This is it then. Farewell.

鹭鸶剪：好，有缘再见。
Paper Heron: As it must be, farewell.

挥别之后，鹭鸶剪转身朝后走，打了个哨，那骡子便屁颠屁颠地朝她跑来。
Giving a wave goodbye, Paper Heron turns back with a whistle, and her mule trots behind her.

夕阳下，一人一骡的影子被照得又长又细。鹭鸶剪在路上稍微停了一下，从骡背挂袋里掏出了纸笔，写了什么，随后伸手往天上一抛。
In the sunset, their shadows stretch long and thin. Paper Heron stops on the road, takes some paper and a brush from her mule's pack. Before long, a slip of paper drifts into the wind behind her.

惠姑：唉，这人啊……
Mayfly: *sigh* I can't tell if she's a fool or a genius.

惠姑：等等，口袋里怎么鼓囊囊的，这，这是什么……
Mayfly: Hmm? What's this in my pocket?

惠姑急匆匆摸向口袋，掏出那不知何时被置入的物件。
She reaches into her pocket to find an object she doesn't remember putting there.

原来是此前被她踩碎的草结护符，现在被完整地还原，旁边还附赠了一张写满了歪扭字迹的纸条。
It's the same clover amulet she had trampled, now restored, and beside it, a hastily written note:

惠姑：“持护符念‘身藏真武，魂存通明’，后左手拇指掐中指，即可隐真身过振气铃，无需修炼亦可用。”
Mayfly: Hold the amulet and chant, "Hide my body behind Zhēnwǔ and my soul in Tongming Palace," then pinch your left thumb and middle finger. That will deceive the Reversion Bell. No cultivation needed.

惠姑：……
Mayfly: ...

惠姑：鹭……鹭鸶剪什么时候？
Mayfly: W-When did she ...?

橙黄而温暖的夕光洒满了祝县城内，在熙攘的人群中，牵着骡子的鹭鸶剪背对着惠姑，挥了挥手。
The warm orange light of sunset bathes Zhu County. Against the busy evening traffic, Paper Heron leads her mule, her back to Mayfly as she waves once again.

SU-08 仙人抚我顶 / The Longevity Ritual

在人声鼎沸的戏台周围，火红绯亮的鱼龙彩灯游曳于人群之中，宛若闹海一般。
Around the noisy opera stage, bright fish and dragon lanterns surge and dive amidst the crowd, as if breaching out of a living ocean.

庙会最热闹的时辰就要到了。
The festival is reaching its busiest hour.

惠姑：……唉。
Mayfly: *sigh*

惠姑：怎么办哇……大家都去哪里了？
Mayfly: Where should I go now? I'm all alone.

惠姑：脚也走累了，肚子也饿了……到处都是卖东西的小摊，我身上却没一个子儿。
Mayfly: So tired, so hungry. Not a wen to my name. Can't even buy myself a bun.

惠姑：同族也一个都没碰到，运气真差。
Mayfly: Where are they? Surely I'm not the only herbaceous Yao in town, am I?

面对着熙攘的人群，惠姑软软地倚到了牌坊的夹杆石上，索性就这么坐了下去。
Mayfly leans against a stone pillar at the Paifang and sits down as she looks out at the swirling crowd.

惠姑：找不到同族也没什么……我是一株草，草在哪里都能生根发芽，所以我不管怎么样都能有个落脚的地方……
Mayfly: Well, even if you find no one, you'll manage. You're a reed, after all. You can take root anywhere, and let the earth feed you.

惠姑：现在是什么时候了？
Mayfly: But I'd prefer food. What time is it now?

惠姑：早知道……就应该多吃几口糯米糕……现在也……也……
Mayfly: If I had known this would be so difficult, I'd have eaten more cakes while Heron was paying.

惠姑：也不会饿得跟肚子被人窝了一拳一样……
Mayfly: At least then I wouldn't be here listening to my stomach growl.

惠姑：要是我现在就会仙法就好了……就能像话本里说的那样潇洒快活，还有好喝的甘露……
Mayfly: *sigh* If only I were an immortal. I'd never go hungry again. I'll bet their elixirs must taste better than any river water.

惠姑：嗯？什么东西这么热闹？
Mayfly: Hm? Why are people gathering around here?

男童Ⅰ：娘！是打铁花！我不要小金鱼了，我要去看打铁花！
Boy I: Mama! It's the iron flower fireworks! Can I see? Can I see?

惠姑：转瞬即逝……
Mayfly: Fireworks, gone in a moment.

惠姑：可……真好看啊。
Mayfly: But so beautiful.

惠姑：要是我这辈子，也能……
Mayfly: If only my life had a moment like that, just one.

杜六：笑得这么灿烂，看什么呢。
Du Liu: Yáng Wǔ, what are you smiling about?

杨武：打铁花，好看！
Yang Wu: The iron flower fireworks. So beautiful!

程和光：杜六！杨武！马上带你们的人去戏台的哨点就位！
Cheng Heguang: Dù Liù, Yáng Wǔ! Get your men into position! Keep your eyes on the stage!

程和光：谣言中提到“仙人授长生”的地点本就是那戏台，你们须得打起十二分精神看好！
Cheng Heguang: This is where the immortal will supposedly arrive to grant longevity. If something happens, I need you all at the ready!

人群之外，程和光站在高处，面容凝重地审视着喜气洋洋的百姓们。
Chéng Héguāng stands on an elevated platform, looking down over the happy fairgoers with an unmatching expression, too dark and serious against the joyful night.

杜六：这才什么时辰啊——小程巡检，你怎么了？怎么感觉今天格外严肃。
Du Liu: But the opera doesn't start for a while yet. What's wrong, Chief? You're looking more serious than ever.

杨武：下午，有个女道士从他手里跑了。
Yang Wu: A Daoist gave him the slip this afternoon.

杜六：唉？倒是还没听说过有谁能在小程巡检的手底下逃脱的。
Du Liu: What? Who could escape Chief Chéng's leaf blades?

杨武：在城门公然使用妖法的那个嫌犯，也没抓着。
Yang Wu: It was the lady who cast a spell at the gate, remember? Best keep an eye out for her.

杜六：这两件，到底是你负责的，还是小程巡检负责的？
Du Liu: Are these orders from you or Chief Chéng?

杨武：你这人，我好心告诉你事情的原委，你怎么还损我呢？
Yang Wu: You asked the question, I answered. No need to be snide.

程和光：聊够了吗？那道人使着奇怪的妖法，我从未见过，让她逃脱确实是我的失误。
Cheng Heguang: Enough. That Daoist possessed strange arcane skills, the likes of which I have never seen. I take the blame for her escape.

程和光：在这个节点，县内冒出来这么一个形迹可疑的邪道……此事必然有诈！诸位不可松懈！
Cheng Heguang: Her arrival coinciding with this mysterious sect is no coincidence. She's scheming something. Stay sharp!

杜六：你知道吗？小程巡检之前有一张弓，有一天早上断掉了，断之前还喊出一句话来，全府的人都听见了。
Du Liu: You ever wonder why the chief's sword is never blunt? I figure it's because he's always yelling at it.

杨武：喊的什么？
Yang Wu: What are you talking about?

杜六：不可松懈！不可松懈！
Du Liu: "Stay sharp! Stay sharp!"

杨武：噗……
Yang Wu: Pfft.

程和光：杜六！
Cheng Heguang: Dù Liù!

杜六：是！小程巡检！
Du Liu: Yes, Chief!

程和光板着脸，耳朵尖却红了。
Their chief holds a stern face, but his cheeks betray him with a flush of red.

程和光：没有发生过这样的事情。
Cheng Heguang: I wasn't talking to my sword.

杜六：是！小程巡检！
Du Liu: Right, of course, Chief!

杨武：杜六在府内传播谣言，属于知法犯法。
Yang Wu: Tsk tsk, can't believe you're spreading rumors like that.

杨武：程巡检，你该罚他掌嘴才是。
Yang Wu: I'd say that warrants a caning. Allow me to carry out the sentence.

程和光咬了咬牙，按刀背过身去。
Their chief grits his teeth, places a hand on his blade, and turns his back.

程和光：快戌时了，尽快到哨点就位！要是放跑了可疑人员，我再数罪并罚！
Cheng Heguang: The opera will begin soon. I need everyone in position. No more jokes. If any suspect gets away, you'll face more than a caning.

杜六&杨武：是！
Du Liu & Yang Wu: Understood!

程和光：剩下的人，跟我走，都给我打起精神来！务必要护参加“高跷巡神”的百姓们周全，也不许放跑一个贼人！
Cheng Heguang: Follow me, and keep your eyes and ears peeled! We must safeguard the civilians and apprehend any offenders!

众人：是！
Constables: Yes, Chief!

夜幕降临，点点花灯缀于河面之上，秉烛的乌篷船也多了起来。
Night falls. Lanterns dot the river. More black-awning boats appear, each one festooned with candles.

男童Ⅰ：娘……蜡烛上有小人在跳舞。
Boy I: Mama, look! There's a little man dancing on the candle.

古代妇女Ⅰ：你看错啦，那是烛火在跳动呢。
Ancient Woman I: Don't be silly. That's just the candlelight flickering.

小贩Ⅱ：投壶！讨个彩头喔！小姑娘，来试试？
Vendor II: Come and play pitch-pot! Young lady, dare to try your luck?

惠姑：我……
Mayfly: I ...

杨武：清道了，清道了！
Yang Wu: Make way! Make way!

杨武：把这块都让出来，一会儿看戏的时候人都得从这儿走。
Yang Wu: Make way, please! We need to clear a path for the audience.

小贩Ⅱ：好嘞，官爷。
Vendor II: Of course, officer.

惠姑：要开始唱戏了吗？
Mayfly: Is the opera about to begin?

杨武：是啊，小姑娘，等到戌时戏就开场了。
Yang Wu: Yes, in just a few minutes.

嬉笑之声传来，一伙男男女女相簇拥着路过了杨武。
Laughter and chatter close in as a group of men and women pass Yáng Wǔ.

惠姑：是在茶摊遇到的那些人……
Mayfly: Those are the Yao I met at the cake stall.

兔妖：来呀～
Hare: Come join us!

洋溢着欢愉的精怪队伍从惠姑面前走过，如走马灯般似乎没有尽头。
A parade of joyful Yao passes before Mayfly. They spin around until they seem like a carousel with her in the center, a parade with no beginning and no end.

惠姑：我……
Mayfly: I ...

在惠姑愣神之际，人群突然拥挤了起来，惠姑只觉自己如同被山洪席卷而去。
Entranced by the sight, the procession sweeps Mayfly off her feet, carrying her away as if caught in the current of a flooding river.

惠姑：呃唔——
Mayfly: Ugh!

杨武：干什么！不要拥挤！喂！那边的！维持秩序！
Yang Wu: Hey! No pushing! Over there! Keep the peace, or we'll keep it for you!

惠姑：呵……呵……
Mayfly: Ugh! Eh ...

惠姑回头望去，骚乱已平息，她自己却如浮木般被冲到了万里之外。
Mayfly looks back. She's been carried far only to be left in a strange place, sticking out like driftwood after a receding tide.

惠姑：嗯？我……怎么被挤到戏台这里了？
Mayfly: The-The stage? How did I—?

乐曲紧锣密鼓地奏着，戏曲演员踩着碎步上场亮相了。
The music rises fast and loud. An opera singer steps onto the stage with quick steps.

台上之人一开口，戏腔绵长悠扬，台下不禁噤声。
The singer's melodious voice captures the crowd in a sudden rapture.

惠姑：是《邯郸记》！
Mayfly: This is Legends of Handan!

唱腔悠悠然飘到了戏台的另一端，那边正站着程和光和手下一群人，盯梢着这戏台周围的一举一动。
The singing reaches the far end of the stage, where Chéng Héguāng and his men stand eyeing the proceedings suspiciously.

程和光：早知道有“仙人授长生”的谣言，竟然还安排唱这出！
Cheng Heguang: Legends of Handan? How could they choose this of all operas with these rumors going around?

杜六：小程巡检知道这戏的内容？
