Du Liu: What's it about, Chief?

程和光盯着那戏台，眼中全是不加掩饰的不满。
Chéng's hard stare conveys his disdain even before his words confirm it.

程和光：……这戏名叫《邯郸记》，是讲吕洞宾引导一个书生入梦，那书生梦中经历官场沉浮后顿悟，梦醒后便随吕洞宾修道去了。
Cheng Heguang: It tells the story of a scholar who was guided into a dream by the immortal Lǚ Dòngbīn. There, he experienced life as an official in the imperial system; he found enlightenment once he awoke and became Lǚ's apprentice to pursue longevity.

杜六：难怪这八仙都来劝人学仙，原来是这个意思。
Du Liu: Hah. No wonder you're so shook up over it.

惠姑：看……看不到……
Mayfly: I, eugh, I can't see.

惠姑极力在人群中踮脚，想望到台上的光景。好在声音不会被眼前的人群阻碍。
Mayfly stands on her tiptoes, unable to see the stage over the crowd. But though she can't make out the scene, the song, at least, breaks through.

惠姑：我可听过千百遍了。
Mayfly: I must've watched this opera a hundred times.

惠姑：只是，戏子们一直拿着那烛台干嘛？
Mayfly: But I've never seen them use candles before. Did they change the story?

惠姑痴痴地望着戏台，现在那里是这庙会中最热闹的地方，汇聚着人们的喜悦与向往。
She finds her way to the front of the stage and looks up, captivated at the performance. It pulls the joy and hope of the crowd up like spun silk that gives warmth and color to the night sky.

戏台周围，无数蜡烛被点燃。跳跃的烛光明灭摇晃着，将人们微暗模糊的身影打在墙上，似求似拜。
Countless candles ring the stage. Their flickering flames throw dim, dancing shadows on the walls, shadows that seem to sway and bob like a procession of monks in prayer.

惠姑：好温暖的烛火……
Mayfly: It's so warm.

狐妖：哎哟～好美的东西～
Fox: Goodness, how beautiful!

兔妖：真叫人看得入迷了。
Hare: I can't keep myself from staring.

烛火仿佛跳出了蜡做的供台，朝人们开了金口。
The flames leap out from their wax altars, speaking in a divine and wordless tongue to the people below.

惠姑：这是什么时候点起来的？它们一直就在这里吗？
Mayfly: Hold on. When did they light these candles?

惠姑：烛火……在说些什么……？
Mayfly: The flames, they're whispering something.

点点烛火在夜幕下摇曳，忽亮忽暗，引得人挪不开眼。
The small lights sway beneath the night sky, alternating between bright and dim. They become a hypnotic flow that those watching cannot turn away from.

烛火们嬉笑怒骂，念着不甚清楚的口号，宣泄着千百年来朝生暮死的苦楚。
The flickering lights seem to laugh, to scold, and then to chant unclear words, venting the pain of their brief lives through the ages.

惠姑：啊，我听清了！它们在说……
Mayfly: Yes, I can hear them. They're saying ...

狐妖：要我长生，要我成仙……
Fox: Grant us longevity.

兔妖：要我长生，要我成仙……！
Hare: Grant us longevity.

惠姑：戏台……什么时候如此近了？
Mayfly: Wait. When did I get this close?

人群的熙攘之声消散，惠姑抬头望着台上之人。
A hush falls over the crowd. Mayfly looks up at the figure on the stage.

烛火盈盈，心随影动，这戏台仿佛是专门为诚心者而设。
The warm light shimmers. Hearts beat in time with the swaying shadows. This stage feels as if it were instead a refuge, a bastion of light and song calling out to those who might approach it.

夜幕笼罩下，百人的仰望里树起了百个戏台。
Under the cover of night, under the gaze of many hundreds of eyes, a hundredfold stages rise.

程和光：杜六！杨武！你们去哪儿？！
Cheng Heguang: Dù Liù! Yáng Wǔ! Where are you?

程和光：不好！这烛火里有能迷惑人心的妖法！别看！
Cheng Heguang: Ah. They're using the candlelight to conjure illusions! Avert your eyes!

蓬山好看春只要有神仙分：世上人不学仙真是蠢
惠姑: 世上人不学仙真是蠢。
Only those given the chance to cultivate their lives may enjoy the everlasting spring of Penglai.: Only a fool would give up such a chance.
Mayfly: Only a fool would give up such a chance.

鹭鸶剪：你想获得长生吗？
Paper Heron: Do you wish to become immortal?

惠姑：嗯？
Mayfly: Hmm?

惠姑：鹭……鸶剪……？
Mayfly: He-Heron?

鹭鸶剪：天地含精，万物化生，日月并明，与我偕终。
Paper Heron: Heaven and earth bear the essence which forms all life. I shall live as long as the sun and the moon shine.

SU-09 故事尽头 / The End ...?

烛火的光焰逐渐隐没，房间内的电灯映亮了芦草结的眼睛。
The candlelight fades and is soon replaced by the steady glow of modern incandescent bulbs.

她下意识地摸了摸头顶，只有草叶静静地扫过她的指尖。
Reed touches her head unconsciously, feeling blades of grass brush against her fingertips.

芦草结：……所以，惠姑真的求到了长生。
Reed: So, Mayfly was given the Method of Longevity. Just like she wanted.

芦草结：鹭鸶剪就是传说里那位仙人……
Reed: And that means that Paper Heron was the legendary immortal.

或许是因为刚才的触碰，又一片草叶飘落下来。
As if a reminder, another blade of grass tumbles down at her touch.

芦草结：我……
Reed: I ...

芦草结：不管这些是不是真的，我必须抓紧时间留下线索！
Reed: Well, true or not, I better get this down before I forget any details.

随手将草叶揣进口袋，编辑胡乱地翻出纸笔，快速地写下一行行记录。
She tucks the grass into her pocket and practically leaps toward her paper and pen.

芦草结：“东方戏剧的独特旋律和烛光将现场氛围推向高点，当仙人的手指落下，无论参与者是否对此抱有怀疑——”
Reed: "The distinctive melodies of Eastern opera, combined with the magical glow of candlelight, brought the atmosphere to its peak. When the immortal moved her fingers, the audience, including those who had doubts about longevity ..."

芦草结：“他们都开始倾向于相信世上真的有永生的奇迹，尤其是身为一年生草本植物精怪的当事人惠姑。”
Reed: "... naturally came to believe in this miracle, including Mayfly, a herbaceous Yao whose life was about to end only a few months later."

芦草结：“根据当地居民的叙述，以及笔者的亲身经历，可以在此做出一个大胆的推测。”
Reed: "Based on accounts from local residents and my own experience, I feel I can make a bold assumption."

芦草结：“仙人鹭鸶剪为惠姑授了长生之法，延续了她的寿命。而后，出于某种缘由，沉睡在祝县地下。”
Reed: "After the opera was over, Paper Heron, the legendary immortal, taught the Method of Longevity to Mayfly to extend her life. Then, for some reason, she fell into a deep sleep beneath Zhu County."

不知过去多久，窗外已经响起了鸟鸣。街面上也渐渐热闹起来。
The passage of time goes unnoticed as her pen glides from page to page. The sound of scribbling accompanied first by the silence of night, then gentle birdsong, and finally the bustle of a waking city.

芦草结：呼，又是新的一天了。
Reed: *stretch* Another day.

笔记本上的方格又被划去一个。
One more square in her calendar is crossed out.

往常，编辑会在这些记录旁边补充上详细的备注。但今天，她犹豫片刻，收起了笔。
Usually, she would leave a detailed journal of her day, a record for her next iteration. But today, she lets her pen rest.

芦草结：也许这次，不需要下一个“我”来重新记住这一切……
Reed: Maybe I won't need to leave a note for the next "me" this time.

清早，小店的主人例行拉开白铁皮的卷帘门。
As the morning progresses, the storekeeper pulls up the shop's rolling shutters.

门外除了晨风和空荡的马路，意外还有一位等待已久的客人。
Waiting outside, aside from the morning breeze, is a familiar face.

老板娘：来啦。今天起这么早啊！
Storekeeper: You're up early today. Did you get enough sleep?

老板娘：对了，昨晚忙忘了，少找你三块六，等等啊，我把门口扫了就……
Storekeeper: Oh, and I was so busy last night, I forgot to give you your change. Hold on. Let me unlock the door first.

话音还没落，编辑已经在屏幕前坐好。
Before she can even finish her words, Reed has returned to her glowing screen.

芦草结：没关系，我的报道马上就能完成了！我赶时间呢，少睡一会儿不要紧。
Reed: Sleep, shmeep, my article's almost finished. All I really need is a computer.

芦草结：噢，抱歉，忘记问了——我现在可以用电脑了吗？
Reed: Oh. Sorry, I got a little overexcited. I meant, would it be possible to use one?

老板娘：你这丫头，性子这么急。行，你自己会鼓捣就好，我忙我的去啦。
Storekeeper: I can see that, haha. Go ahead. You can use that one. You know how to turn it on.

芦草结深吸一口气，在键盘上敲下思索了一整夜的词句。
Reed takes a deep breath before typing the words she spent the night planning.

热心的店主从不同寻常的操作声中觉察出了不对劲。
The odd pace of the typing draws the storekeeper's attention.

老板娘：你鼠标怎么按得这么急？是不是网卡了？
Storekeeper: Are you trying to put a hole in my mouse, or is the network down?

芦草结：……什么？
Reed: Huh?

芦草结：没有没有……电脑很好。
Reed: Oh, no, the network's fine.

她才意识到自己的整条手臂都因为高频率的点触而阵阵发麻。
It's only then that she notices that her whole arm has gone numb from the speed of her typing.

芦草结：对了，姨姨，有没有其他人来你这里上过网？
Reed: Has anyone else come by recently?

老板娘：最近只有你，位置我都给你留着的。放心啦。
Storekeeper: No, you're the only one. But I'll keep a spot open for you. Don't you worry.

芦草结：谢谢您！
Reed: Oh, thank you!

键盘声飞快地响起。

她不再快速刷新，只是瞪大了眼睛盯着显像管上每一个肉眼可见的三色荧光粉单元。
The frantic typing resumes as soon as their conversation ends.

芦草结：……！
芦草结：梅树……？我记得城中有梅树的只有……

芦草结在天光下重新打量着眼前绿意盎然的中心公园和旁边正在火热施工的楼盘。
In the daylight, Reed returns to reassess the leafy central park and the bustling construction site nearby.

巨幅的广告牌如昨夜般昂然站立在那里，升仙上府的打印字体在日照下反射着微光。
The words "Immortal Residence" decorating the impressive billboard gleam down at her in the sunlight.

对比之下，公园中那棵半死不活的梅树显得有些黯然失色。
Far beneath it, the half-dead Mei tree that lies in the middle of the park looks dull by comparison.

开发商：你是……记者？昨天不是说过了吗，不用来了，过来也是白跑！
Property Developer: Another journalist? I already told the other ones we're not open for interviews.

或许是她在附近张望太久，旁边的中年男子忍不住开口了。
It seems she's spent too much time staring as a middle-aged man approaches in a huff.

开发商：不管你们是什么杂志，我们不接受采访！同志，你回去吧。
Property Developer: I don't care who you write for. Get out of here, will you?

芦草结：噢，不采访！我就——我就在附近看看。
Reed: Oh! No, no, I'm not here for interviews. I'm just having a look around.

芦草结：昨天有人来？是看着和我差不多的人吗？
Reed: So, someone came around here then? Someone who looked like me?

开发商：你再问也问不出什么，不是闹鬼！现代社会，不兴这一套，什么影子，都是看错了！
Property Developer: I'm not answering any questions! My building isn't haunted, and that's that!

芦草结：你是说……
Reed: Not haunted? You mean ...

没等芦草结接着开口，一个声音就吸引了所有人的注意。
Before Reed can ask anything more, a new voice draws away their attention.

办事员：经理、经理……真出事了！
Employee: Sir! We've got a problem!

跑得气喘吁吁的年轻人打断了他们的对话。
A young man, breathless from running, cuts her questioning short.

开发商：你才出事了，会不会说话！
Property Developer: What, and you want to hand it over to me?

办事员：经理，那个张教授他讲……
Employee: It-It's Professor Zhāng. He said he—

经理猛地拽了一下他的胳膊，客气地同芦草结打了个招呼，走到了旁边。
The property developer pulls his arm, gives a polite nod to Reed, and walks aside.

半分钟后，芦草结听到了一句脏话。
Half a minute later, Reed hears shouting.

开发商：我去你的，什么叫那些人是被怪物吃了？
Property Developer: Would you listen to yourself? What do you mean they were eaten by monsters?

办事员：张教授说他们在古籍上查到的……咱们能不能不管他？
Employee: Professor Zhāng said he found this in an ancient book. Should we just ignore him?

开发商：狗屁古籍，我神仙府的招牌都打出去了，你现在说他们是被吃了，我房子还卖不卖了？！
Property Developer: Damn him and his book! I go and call it the "Immortal Residence," and then it turns out people died here? If this gets out, I'll never sell the place!

开发商的嗓音随着情绪激动渐趋高亢，随风而来的只言片语引起了芦草结的注意。
The developer's voice rises, and Reed catches pieces of their argument on the wind.

办事员：他还把那个古籍复印了一份给我……他开口就要十万，不然就寄给报社。经理，你要不要看看？
Employee: He gave us a copy of the book. Said he'd send one to the press unless he receives 100,000 yuan today. Do you want to look at it?

开发商：我看个屁！
Property Developer: F**k him!

趁着他们争执的工夫，芦草结悄悄地走向公园入口。
While they argue, Reed slips away toward the entrance of the park.

她满心期待地打量着那棵梅树，它干枯的枝上缀着不少花苞。
Full of hope, she looks up at the Mei tree. Its dry branches hold many buds.

树下，一头骡子安静地啃着新铺的草皮。
Under the tree, a mule chews on fresh green grass.

芦草结：……？
Reed: ...?

芦草结：“枯荣自任”……？
Reed: OneWithFlow?

编辑试探地唤了它一句。
She calls out to the mule, not entirely convinced by her own conclusion.

骡子：咴。
Mule: Whinny.

骡子受了惊，转身要逃。芦草结注意到它身上的披挂。她不久前曾在别处见过。
The mule, startled, turns to flee. Reed immediately takes notice of the familiar pack, one she knows she's seen before.

芦草结：鹭鸶剪进城时就带着你！
Reed: You traveled with Paper Heron wherever she went!

芦草结：等等——
Reed: Wait.

一阵风猛然吹来，树叶的沙沙声甚至盖过了骡子的蹄音。
A strong wind blows. The rustling leaves drown out the mule's trotting hooves.

灰白的纸页不偏不倚，恰好落在她身前半步。
A pale page falls a half step before her.

芦草结：其时日月同天，地裂陷人，自梅花教门，隙长数里……
Reed: At the time, the sun and moon hung together in the sky. The earth split in two at the gate of the School of Mei, opening a rift miles long that swallowed souls.

芦草结：令尹使人发之，往往空有衣冠及草木花鸟，鲜见尸首……
Reed: When the governor had it investigated, they couldn't find a single human dead or alive, only clothes, dead plants, and animals.

芦草结：时人多以为……地龙噬人？
Reed: Many believed the phenomenon was caused by the earth dragon?

芦草结：……！！！
Reed: ...!!!

令她惊讶的不仅仅是这些记载。
It's not just the records that surprise her.

纸页落下的地方，风在半空中打着旋儿。为她指示出一个精确的坐标。
Where the page fell, the wind spins in midair, leading her to a precise spot.

一个系结。
Another Wind Knot.

芦草结：空有衣冠……地龙噬人……
Reed: Only clothes, dead plants, and animals ... The earth dragon ...

芦草结：难道那些精怪……没有成仙？
Reed: No way. Then the Yao didn't really become immortal?

SU-10 乐土 / To "Heaven"

烛火盈盈，台上踱步如风。
On stage, footsteps move with a light, quick pace.

你想获得长生吗？
Do you wish to become immortal?

惠姑抬头，眼前却是空无一物。
Mayfly looks up but sees nothing before her.

你想获得长生吗？
Do you wish to become immortal?

惠姑：世上人不学仙真是蠢。
Mayfly: Only a fool would give up such a chance.

惠姑：嗯？这是哪里？
Mayfly: Hm? Where am I?

惠姑从床上坐了起来，打量着四周。
Mayfly sits up from a comfy bed and looks around.

惠姑：嘿！
Mayfly: Eh!

惠姑：这里好生气派……
Mayfly: This place is so luxurious.

飞身下床，惠姑好奇地在房内四处踱步。
She jumps to the floor and walks around the room, curious about her new surroundings.

惠姑：好柔软的床，被子也很暖和……
Mayfly: The bed's soft, and this blanket's so light and warm.

惠姑：我做了个好奇怪的梦，但是睡得又特别足！
Mayfly: What a strange dream I had, but, my, do I feel rested?

惠姑：吸——呼——神清气爽！入秋以后一直都没什么精神，可今天我却觉得自己可以……
Mayfly: *deep breath* I'm brimming with energy! I haven't felt this good since autumn. With strength like this flowing through me—

惠姑：可以插一亩地的秧！
Mayfly: I could till a whole field all on my own!

惠姑：说不定，那个跟我差不多高的大花瓶也举得起来！
Mayfly: That vase is almost as big as me, but I bet I could lift it.

说着，惠姑便走向放置在房间角落的花瓶，跃跃欲试地比画着它的高度和直径。
She finds herself standing in front of the vase in the corner, excitedly stretching out her hands to measure its height and width.

？？？：惠姑，你醒了？
???: Hello, Mayfly.

惠姑：您……您是？咦？
Mayfly: Who-Who's that? Wait.

惠姑：鹭鸶剪？
Mayfly: Paper Heron?

？？？：刚才我与鹭鸶剪在门外谈些事情，听到房间内有响动，便想应该是你终于醒了。
???: We were chatting outside your room when we heard your voice. I'm glad to see that you are doing well.

？？？：你现在身处梅花教内，想必一定有很多疑问。无妨，我们慢慢来。
???: I know what you wish to ask. You are in the School of Mei.

身着白衣的夫人微笑着点点头，继续向惠姑介绍。
The lady smiles and nods as she explains further.

？？？：我是梅花教的掌门，大家都称我任仙子，你也这么跟着叫便好。
???: And I am its founder. They call me Master Rén, or Rén the Immortal.

惠姑：任仙子……
Mayfly: Rén the Immortal.

惠姑：难道您、您就是那个“仙人”！
Mayfly: Th-Then, you must be the immortal everyone's been talking about?

惠姑：请仙人授我长生之法！
Mayfly: Please, Master, teach me the Method of Longevity!

任仙子：呵呵……又是一个初见而不知真貌的小家伙。
Master Ren: Hah hah. Another young soul looking too far ahead to see the truth before them.

任仙子：你要找的人就在此处，可并不是我。当年，我也是承了她的恩，才习得这长生之法的。
Master Ren: The immortal you seek is standing right in front of you, but it isn't me. In fact, I was one of her students.

惠姑：……诶？
Mayfly: What?

惠姑的目光在任仙子和鹭鸶剪之间游移，然后试探性地落在了鹭鸶剪身上。
Mayfly shifts her focus between Master Rén and Paper Heron before resting on the more comfortably familiar face.

任仙子不语，也笑着看向鹭鸶剪。
Saying nothing, Master Rén smiles and follows Mayfly's gaze to Paper Heron.

惠姑：鹭鸶剪——？！你是说鹭鸶剪她才是仙人？！
Mayfly: Heron? You mean, she's the immortal?!

鹭鸶剪搅着碗里的甜汤，里面的白砂糖因为饱和而沉了底。
Paper Heron stirs the sweet soup in her bowl. The white sugar has sunk to the bottom.

鹭鸶剪：可以不用这个词称呼我吗？听了只觉得身上有蚂蚁在爬。
Paper Heron: I'd prefer if you wouldn't call me that, Mayfly. Makes me feel as though I'm covered in ants.

惠姑：这到底是怎么回事？
Mayfly: But how can that be?

任仙子：你还记得昨晚的事吗？
Master Ren: Do you recall the evening passed?

惠姑：昨晚……在戏台上，我……
Mayfly: Last night, I was pushed out on the stage, and then ...

任仙子：是了，昨晚鹭鸶剪在戏台上为你以剑抚顶，做了仪式，之后你就睡得十分之香甜。
Master Ren: Precisely. It was then that Paper Heron held the longevity ritual for you. You fell into a deep slumber for the rest of the night.

任仙子：你现在感觉如何？
Master Ren: How do you feel now?

惠姑：倒是觉得神清气爽，也有力气了不少……我已然长生了？
Mayfly: I feel refreshed, energetic, alive. Then, I've gained longevity already?

任仙子：不，你只是跨进了长生的门槛。
Master Ren: No. This is but the first step.

任仙子：鹭鸶剪初步扭转了你体内的气蕴，使其运行更接近天道，符合继续修行的条件。
Master Ren: Master Heron altered the flowing pattern of your Qi to imitate that of the Way, laying the foundation for true longevity cultivation.

任仙子：要想真正获得长生，还需在梅花教内用特定的法子继续修行，这法门我会慢慢教与你们的。
Master Ren: But this alone will not extend your life. To achieve true longevity, one must cultivate it through the method of our school. Worry not. I will be your guide.

惠姑：这样啊，等、等一下……
Mayfly: I see. No, wait.

惠姑疑惑地掰起了手指头。
Mayfly looks puzzled; she counts her fingers, as if attempting to follow the logic to its conclusion.

惠姑：也就是说……鹭鸶剪是任仙子的师父……是梅花教的师祖……
Mayfly: Paper Heron, if you're Master Rén's master and the founder of the School of Mei ...

惠姑：那你明明什么都知道……一路上还跟我装傻充愣……
Mayfly: Then you knew all along? You were just pretending?

惠姑：好啊，原来我也被你骗了，这下我……我不会再内疚啦！
Mayfly: Th-Then, you lied too! You know, I felt so guilty about leaving you behind!

鹭鸶剪：我没有故意要瞒你啦……原先我也不知你是来找任仙子的。
Paper Heron: I didn't deceive you. I had no inkling that it was Rén that you sought.

鹭鸶剪：我本不知庙会的安排，后来才晓得任仙子本来要在戏台上传法，我一时兴起便替了她。
Paper Heron: I only learned of her ritual on the stage at the last instant. I took her place as its officiator as a bit of fun.

鹭鸶剪：怎么样，昨晚我厉害吧？你是不是都没意识到戏台上的人变成我了？
Paper Heron: But I looked quite splendid up there, don't you think? Didn't you notice it was me?

想到高兴之处，鹭鸶剪美滋滋地舀了一口甜汤放进嘴里。
At this pleasant thought, Paper Heron spoons some of the sweet soup into her mouth.

惠姑：……
Mayfly: ...

惠姑：那……那日临别时，我口袋中的护符和纸条，也是你通过这法子放的？
Mayfly: So it was you who slipped the amulet and the note into my pocket.

鹭鸶剪：嗯，这法子我很久没使过了，正好这趟出来，不就得着几个机会了嘛。
Paper Heron: Of course. I hadn't cast that spell for some time, so I thought I'd seize the opportunity to give it a spin.

鹭鸶剪：别苦着脸呀，惠姑，你知道吗，昨天演出的效果可好了！现在有好多小妖怪都在外面排着队要学。
Paper Heron: Ah, why the glum look, eh? Our performance was a great success. Yao have joined the school in spadefuls.

惠姑：学也是学长生之法，不是你这乱七八糟的……
Mayfly: They're here for the Method, not your magic tricks.

惠姑：……啊不，不成，怎么能对仙人这样说——
Mayfly: Ah, scythe me down. You're the immortal! How could I say such a thing?

惠姑还没说完，便被门外一阵急匆匆的脚步声打断。
Before Mayfly can finish, hurried steps outside cut her off.

惠姑：咦……？
Mayfly: Hm?

那脚步声到了门口，倏地停了下来，紧接着一阵窃窃私语和衣裳摩挲之声传来。
The footsteps stop at the door, followed by whispers and the rustle of clothes.

突然，门口露出一只矮胖的小刺猬、一只头上长草的山药精，紧接着是一只灰鼠精、一只鼩鼱精，后面还有一群排成长队、乌泱泱的小精怪们……
Suddenly, a short, plump hedgehog and a yam with a leafy head peek out from behind the door. Then a gray rat, a shrew, and behind them, a whole parade of other Yao.

喧闹的小妖：仙人！听说您在此处，我们冒昧来看您……和新来的小师妹了！
Noisy Yao: Immortal! Please, forgive our intrusion. We're here to see you and our new schoolmate.

害羞的小妖：师……师祖，晚辈不才，您见面给我们带的那些贵重法器，晚辈没……没有好报答的回礼，若您不嫌弃……
Shy Yao: Grandmaster, our greatest thanks for these artifacts. We've brought a token of our gratitude. Though it's not so valuable, I hope it will suffice.

鹭鸶剪：哎哟，这有什么。咱们都是同脉传人，这是我头次来教门看你们，也是应该的。
Paper Heron: Oh, think nothing of it. Consider it a gift from your grandmaster.

喧闹的小妖：仙……啊呸呸，师祖客气了，昨夜您表演完那招后，咱们好多人都说想学呢！
Noisy Yao: Thank you, Immor—Uh, Grandmaster. Erm, if it's not too much trouble, could you teach us the spell you used on the stage last night?

惠姑：……
Mayfly: ...

鹭鸶剪摆摆手，脸上的表情却是很受用。
Paper Heron waves their praise away with her hand, but the smile behind that waving hand reveals her joy.

鹭鸶剪：这有何难！回头我教你们就是，你们还想学什么？
Paper Heron: Sure, it's not so difficult. Just say what more you want to learn, and I shall teach you.

涌入的精怪们和鹭鸶剪正热闹地攀谈着，惠姑看着被围成一圈的鹭鸶剪，摇了摇头。
The Yao pour in, talking excitedly with Paper Heron. Mayfly watches as her friend-turned-grandmaster enters the circle and shakes her head.

任仙子：咳咳！
Master Ren: Ahem!

几声清响，任仙子用咳嗽打断了这场热闹的师门相聚。
A few clear coughs cut the clamoring voices short.

任仙子：好了，别闹你们师祖了，如此嬉笑，成何体统？该修炼的便回去修炼，其他人各自回位。
Master Ren: Now, now, students. You ought to show respect in the presence of the grandmaster. Enough playfulness. You must all return to your cultivation.

害羞的小妖：可……可我听说师祖多年未踏足我们梅花教，昨夜才第一次到来……大家，大家都想多跟师祖说说话……
Shy Yao: But I hear this is the first time the grandmaster has visited our school in many years. We only wanna talk to her.

鹭鸶剪：我也很想和大家多聊聊。
Paper Heron: And talk we shall.

任仙子微笑了一下。
Master Rén smiles.

任仙子：你们师祖将在教门内停留多日，到时有什么问题，尽管问便是了。
Master Ren: The grandmaster will be with us for many days. There will be plenty of time.

任仙子：只是怕你们现在打扰到新进门的师妹，惠姑，你说是不是？
Master Ren: For now, we ought to consider our newest schoolmate. You need some time to settle in, isn't that so, Mayfly?

惠姑：诶……
Mayfly: Err ...

任仙子：你刚刚得法，身体正是需要适应的时候。
Master Ren: You have just received the ritual. Your body needs time to adapt.

任仙子：你们这些做师兄师姐的，带惠姑多走动走动，了解下咱们教门的环境，如何？
Master Ren: Students, will you show Mayfly around our school? A little bit of activity should do her good.

鹭鸶剪：哦，对！是得多活动活动！
Paper Heron: Ah, right. Best to get some exercise.

喧闹的小妖：师父说得是，咱们确实冒昧了些。
Noisy Yao: Whatever you say, Master.

喧闹的小妖：你叫惠姑是吧？其实咱们也给你带了一点礼……嘿，刚刚只管围着师祖转，差点忘了！
Noisy Yao: Mayfly, is it? We brought you a gift too. Sorry, we got carried away after seeing the grandmaster.

这只小妖拿出了早已准备好的数盒药材、几笼糕点放在桌上，份量看着并不轻。
The Yao bring out several boxes of herbs and steamers filled with cakes, all prepared in advance—a substantial offering.

惠姑：啊……谢谢你们的好意！我……我也觉得身体里有股劲儿，十分想出去跑跑跳跳。
Mayfly: That's alright, and thank you for the gift. I feel so full of energy now. I'd love to look around.

鹭鸶剪：前庭那边还挺好玩的，惠姑你可叫它们带你过去看看，等回来再拆礼也不迟。
Paper Heron: You should spend some time getting to know the other students. Your gift can wait.

惠姑：照，那我们先走一步，不打搅二位大人了。
Mayfly: Alright then. I can save it for later.

惠姑拍了拍裙面，便随着小妖们一同离开了厢房，不久后，庭院内便传来了梅花教弟子的惊呼。
Mayfly pats her skirt and leaves with the Yao. Soon, she enters a busy courtyard bustling with the voices of other students of the School of Mei.

喧闹的小妖：师妹！那可是千斤大鼎，举不得啊——
Noisy Yao: Stop it, Mayfly! That cauldron's too heavy! You could hurt yourself.

任仙子：呵呵……想当初我刚获得长生之时，也是这般，不知力该往何处使了。
Master Ren: Heh heh. I was just like her back then. Didn't know what to do with my newfound strength.

鹭鸶剪从碗里舀了一大口甜汤，随后便把碗放在了桌子上。
Paper Heron lifts another spoonful of her sweet soup to her lips and then sets the bowl down.

任仙子：你那“五感退化”的毛病，有好些吗？
Master Ren: So, have you retrieved your five senses?

鹭鸶剪：嗯——嗯——
Paper Heron: Hmm. Mmm.

任仙子点点头，等待鹭鸶剪把嘴里的东西咽下去。
Master Rén nods and waits for Paper Heron to swallow.

鹭鸶剪：还是那样子，这次回来，连“清白盏”的味道都尝不出来了……还是聊聊正事吧！
Paper Heron: No, it's become worse. Even clear soup is practically tasteless to me now. But enough about that; we have more important things to discuss.

鹭鸶剪：近日我夜中起卦望气，险道兽揽诸已醒了五六分，我来的路上也看到了不少异象预兆。
Paper Heron: My divinations suggest that Lǎnzhū is waking. I have observed many omens along the road.

鹭鸶剪：冬天千鸟北徙，枯草变黑……用不了多久，它便会完全苏醒了。
Paper Heron: Birds migrating north, withered grass blackening. Ere long, Lǎnzhū will awaken.

鹭鸶剪：揽诸与其他险道兽有异，它脱离了侲子的管束，在涣州一带兴风作浪，引发地震。
Paper Heron: Unlike other Xiǎndào Beasts, Lǎnzhū is not under Zhènzǐ's control. The quake it wrought brought great suffering to the Huanzhou region.

鹭鸶剪：曾经，我白马派以“金丹术”与其缠斗百年，能做的也仅是将其堵塞的气穴打通，使其再次陷入沉睡。
Paper Heron: The White Horse School once fought it, and I among them, yet we could only force it into a long slumber.

鹭鸶剪：后有了祖师得大道所赐的两把长生剑，才让普通弟子也有了运转阴阳之气、安抚揽诸之力。
Paper Heron: Until the Way bestowed on us two Swords of Longevity, allowing ordinary students to control the Qi of Yin and Yang in order to pacify Lǎnzhū.

鹭鸶剪：但现在……
Paper Heron: But then ...

鹭鸶剪停了停。
She pauses.

任仙子：我知晓你的意思。
Master Ren: You need not say more.

任仙子在空中划了一个法阵，那法阵金光萦绕了一阵后便退却，显出一把通体莹白的剑来。
Master Rén draws an array in the air. It glows gold for a moment, then fades as a white sword appears.

鹭鸶剪沉重地望着这把剑，空中的长生剑发出温润莹莹的白光，一如既往。
Paper Heron stares intently at the sword. It floats in the air, radiating with a soft white glow.

鹭鸶剪：如今，长生剑只余一把。
Paper Heron: Now, only one sword remains.

鹭鸶剪：白马派亦已不存于世。
Paper Heron: And the White Horse School is no more.

她紧握着剑柄，双手略有些颤抖。
Her hands shake as she grips it, as if she were holding it too tightly.

任仙子：……不必担心，自从你手中接过长生剑后，我便开始考虑镇压揽诸。
Master Ren: You needn't worry. Since the moment you passed the sword to me, I have been making preparations to face Lǎnzhū.

任仙子：我知揽诸一旦苏醒，定有天崩地裂、乾坤失序、日月同天之象。
Master Ren: I know the consequences if I fail. The earth will split, and beneath the dual sun and moon, disaster and disorder will reign.

任仙子：若镇压失败，不只是祝县，整个涣州都将分崩离析，百姓将面临灭顶之灾。
Master Ren: Zhu County, all of Huanzhou, will shatter, causing untold devastation.

任仙子：于是我便创立梅花教，好广集天下群侠之力量。
Master Ren: That is why I founded the School of Mei to gather strength in numbers.

任仙子：这几十年间，我已做好了万全的打算，既有长生剑作倚靠，又列了“镇殃大阵”以作后手，万无一失。
Master Ren: Though I wield the last Sword of Longevity, if it should fail, I have prepared a Quelling Array. But I will need their strength to help me activate it.

鹭鸶剪：哦？
Paper Heron: Oh?

任仙子：你很惊讶？
Master Ren: Do I surprise you?

鹭鸶剪环视厢房，轻轻地叹了一口气。
Paper Heron looks around the room and answers with a sigh.

鹭鸶剪：不，只是感慨那年今日，你还是梅花树下的一名小妖……如今已是一方教派的掌门了。
Paper Heron: Ah, no. It's just ... You were but a little Yao when we first met beneath that tree. Look how you've grown.

任仙子：呵呵……对你来说数旬光阴并无区别，但对我们这些寿命不过几轮圆月的小妖就不是了。
Master Ren: Heh heh. A Yao's life is shorter than most. We must make every day count.

任仙子：人生苦短。既然你将此事托付于我，我定将全力以赴。
Master Ren: You entrusted this task to me, and I will do all that I must to finish it.

任仙子：镇压之事不会出纰漏，这是为了梅花教，更是为了天下人。
Master Ren: I will allow nothing to get in my way. Not only for the sake of the school, but for the sake of everyone in this land.

看着任仙子的微笑，鹭鸶剪一怔，随后摇头一笑。
She sees Rén's smile. Paper Heron pauses, then offers an affirming smile to her old student.

鹭鸶剪：看来我是多虑了，你的考量比我周全许多。不过我要提醒，好生护着你的徒儿们，别让白马派灭门一事再度重演。
Paper Heron: You are more prepared than I could ever hope to be. But mind your students well. I should not like to see your school meet the same fate as mine, eh?

鹭鸶剪：我会在祝县待到镇压结束，危难之时我也会出手。
Paper Heron: I will stay here until the task is done. And intervene if need be.

任仙子郑重地点点头。
Master Rén replies with a solemn nod.

任仙子：当初梅树下，你授我长生，赐我长生剑，才有了今天的我与梅花教。
Master Ren: Grandmaster, you gave me a second life and the Sword of Longevity. I owe my life to you.

任仙子：在此事上，我与梅花教必将全力以赴，定不负你的赐剑之恩，也不负你师门未竟的遗命。你放心。
Master Ren: I swear I will complete the suppression, no matter the cost. For you and for your school.

SU-11 境遇 / Dilemma

阴暗的班房中，时不时传来幽幽的吟诵之声。
In the dim cell, low chants rise and fall over and over until it almost feels like a natural phenomenon, like the howling of the wind.

巡捕Ⅰ：程巡检，这段时间捕获的闹事精怪都关在这里。
Constable I: Chief, all the Yao we've arrested are here.

随着门发出悠长的吱嘎声，精怪们停了下来，在各自的牢狱中齐齐望着于门后出现的三人。
A cell door creaks open slowly. The other Yao stop and look out from their cells at the three who enter.

程和光：……
Cheng Heguang: ...

程和光：呵，我到今天才知道“鹰瞵鹗视”到底是个什么意思。
Cheng Heguang: Hmph. This must be the true meaning of being "watched like a hawk."

程和光：你出去吧，我让苦主问几句就走。
Cheng Heguang: You may leave. I will have the victim identify the culprit.

巡捕Ⅰ：是。
Constable I: Understood.

进了这尽是精怪的班房，程和光身边的平民男子畏惧地瑟缩至程和光身边。
The cell is packed with Yao. Afraid, a man presses himself fearfully against Chéng Héguāng.

程和光握了握腰间的长刀，扭头示意男子莫慌，便稳步踏下台阶。
Chéng grips his blade and tells the man not to be afraid, as he takes the first bold step toward them.

程和光：你们应当认得我。
Cheng Heguang: I trust there's no need to introduce myself.

鸟妖：程巡检，我们自然认识，毕竟要从你那城门进来，实在是费了我们不少工夫，哈哈哈哈……
Bird: Of course, Chief Chéng. After all, it took us all quite some effort to sneak past you, hahahahaha.

鸟妖：这可不是说程巡检玩忽职守的意思，是您管理的城门实在是连只苍蝇都难飞进来呀。
Bird: Let no one say that you neglected your duties. In fact, you did such a sterling job that not even a fly could buzz through that gate.

鸟妖：可惜我飞得比苍蝇要高得多。
Bird: A pity for you that I soar much higher than a fly! Ahahahahahaha!

众妖哄笑起来，程和光提刀震了一下牢门。
The Yao all laugh, leading Chéng Héguāng to raise his blade and strike it against the cell door.

程和光：肃静！
Cheng Heguang: Quiet!

程和光：你看看，这里面是否有诱拐你家人的那只精怪？可得瞧仔细了。
Cheng Heguang: Look over them. See if you can identify the one that abducted your family.

即使有牢门阻隔，男子仍被精怪环绕，他左躲右躲都不是，只差没顶个竹篓将自己扣进去。
Even with the cell door between them, the man feels surrounded by Yao; he dodges fruitlessly left then right as if to avoid their gaze.

他瑟缩着从眼角瞄着被囚的精怪，瞧上一眼都要缓上三缓。
He peeks at the jailed Yao from the corner of his eye. But each glance makes him all the more concerned.

祝县县民Ⅰ：没有……
County Resident I: I-I don't see them.

鸟妖：程巡检真有种知县的范儿了，嘶——但我记得按照大明律法，区区巡检没有审讯的权力。
Bird: My, my, should I call you County Magistrate Chéng now? If I recall correctly, it falls outside of the duties of mere constables to interrogate suspects.

隔着牢门，鸟妖尽可能近地凑到了程和光的面前。
Through the bars, a bird-like Yao leans toward Chéng Héguāng.

鸟妖：您莫不是借机找我们讨那“长生”的法子来的？
Bird: Could it be that you are using this opportunity to learn the Method of Longevity for yourself? Haha!

程和光：鼓唇弄舌。我来这里确实与“长生之法”有关，但不是为了与你们同流合污。
Cheng Heguang: Enough of your twittering, bird. I am investigating this rumor on behalf of the people, not for myself.

程和光：我虽非知县，照例问询的权力还是有的，我迟早将你们查个清楚！
Cheng Heguang: Nor is this a formal interrogation. I am within my rights to question any one of you.

鸟妖：嘻嘻……我之前不是说了吗，程巡检可审不了我们，我们不说，您又能如何？
Bird: Heh heh. And if I don't tell you a thing, what then, Chief Chéng?

鸟妖：巡检为何总与我们过不去？整个祝县，就您让我们提心吊胆。
Bird: Must you really be so harsh on us? Every Yao in Zhu County is scared to death of you.

鸟妖：予您黄金万两，予您长命百岁……
Bird: But I know that you're not all that cruel-hearted. Could you be persuaded to let us go?

鸟妖一边说着，一边将两只手伸出牢门，一手金条，一手符箓，交替着在程和光面前轮舞。
As she speaks, she puts both hands through the bars. One holds a gold bar, the other a charm. She waves them before Chéng Héguāng.

鸟妖：您留我们一条生路，尽早放了我们可好？
Bird: I can offer you both wealth and health.

程和光：妖言惑众！别以为能拿这拙劣的谎话骗我。
Cheng Heguang: Fiend! I will not allow you to deceive me.

程和光以刀背拂开鸟妖的手，惊得她向后蹦了一丈，绷着身子望了程和光一阵，才缓缓地走了回来。
Chéng Héguāng pushes her hands aside with the back of his blade. She jumps back, staring at him tensely, then approaches once more.

鸟妖：巡检如此针对我们，不过是觉得长生之法是假的。
Bird: You think it deception merely because you believe the Method of Longevity to be a false rumor.

鸟妖：若我说，这不是谣言，程巡检又该如何看待呢？你猜我如今几岁了？
Bird: But what if I tell you, it's true, hm? Take a guess at how old I am.

程和光：我不必做这样的猜测，你本是精怪，就算千岁又如何。
Cheng Heguang: There's no need to guess. It is said that Yao can live over a thousand years.

鸟妖：错了，天行有常，命数已定。我们精怪只是假托大道，化作人形，寿命却不改，普通麻雀活多久，我便活多久。
Bird: Whoever told you that knew nothing. Our lives are scarcely longer than our true forms. My own kind live and die within the age of a sparrow. Nothing more.

程和光眼里闪过一丝惊讶，示意鸟妖继续说下去。
Surprise flashes in Chéng Héguāng's eyes. He motions for her to continue.

鸟妖：我们只是想通过别的法子活得久一点，程巡检，你何故为难我们？
Bird: We only want a little more time in this world, Chief Chéng. Why must you stand in our way?

程和光：好让你们继续谋财害命，为祸人间？
Cheng Heguang: Then should I simply allow you and your people to kill, steal, and bring chaos?

鸟妖：我们？
Bird: Me and my people?

鸟妖愣了一下，便开怀大笑起来。
She is stunned for a moment, then responds with a burst of laughter.

鸟妖：哈哈哈哈……我懂了。
Bird: Hahahaha ... I see.

鸟妖：程巡检，是以为我们精怪全无好人。
Bird: You believe the Yao to be evil.

程和光：不，是你们这些散播流言的精怪绝非好人。
Cheng Heguang: No, not universally. Yet it is Yao like you who spread these dangerous rumors in the county.

听闻此言，鸟妖突然止了笑意，缩起脖子，全身的羽毛簌簌抖起。
The Yao stops laughing, her neck jerking in as her feathers rise and puff out.

也不顾栅门的阻挡，她暴怒着冲向程和光。
Filled with rage, she storms toward Chéng Héguāng, ignoring the bars.

鸟妖：你这废物！我们从来都没有害过任何一个人！只是想活下去！
Bird: It is no rumor, fool! Even if it were, what harm have we ever brought for speaking it alone? All our kind desire is to live!

鸟妖：我什么都没有做！放我出去！我等不起了！
Bird: I've done nothing wrong! Release me! Every moment is precious!

程和光：即使你与诱拐之事无关，你也是妖言惑众之人，你被拘在这里，并不冤屈。
Cheng Heguang: You may not have taken part in these abductions, but the rumors you spread surely enticed the ones that did. I will not release you.

鸟妖：你这样对我们……梅花教不会放过你的。
Bird: Fine, continue in your blindness, but the School of Mei will bring justice to us all.

鸟妖发了狠，在牢中扑腾起翅膀来，砖墙上尽是抓痕。
The Yao turns fierce, beating her wings in the cell. Claw marks cover the walls.

程和光：梅花教，便是你们那教派的名字？
Cheng Heguang: The School of Mei. That's the name of your sect, is it?

鸟妖不愿再说更多，只是一味地泄愤。程和光阻隔在鸟妖与惊恐的平民男子之间，护着他离开了班房。
Her anger has become an incomprehensible mash of threats and insults. Chéng Héguāng stands between her and the scared man, leading him away.

衙门书房，平民男子颤抖着坐在木椅之上。
In the Yamen's study, the man sits shaking on a wooden chair.

程和光：喝点茶水，压压惊。
Cheng Heguang: Calm down. Have some tea.

祝县县民Ⅰ：好……好……
County Resident I: Th-Thank you.

男子接过茶水，啜饮几口，便放了下去。
He takes the tea, sips a few times, then sets it down.

程和光：无须惊慌，它们现在被关在牢中，不会再随意出来害人了。
Cheng Heguang: No need to worry; our cells are quite unbreakable.

程和光：关于诱拐你家人的那只精怪，你可还能想起什么来？
Cheng Heguang: So, what more do you know of the Yao that abducted your family?

祝县县民Ⅰ：我只知道它们口口声声说是要长生……
County Resident I: It was jabbering on about "longevity." That's all I know.

程和光：害人不浅。
Cheng Heguang: This rumor is a true menace to society.

祝县县民Ⅰ：程巡检……求求你，我只能靠你了……帮我把我爹找回来吧！
County Resident I: Please, Chief Chéng, please find my father. You're my only hope.

男子抓住程和光的衣襟，几欲下跪，程和光只好拢住他的臂肘，将他托起身。
He grabs the front of Chéng Héguāng's clothes as if to kneel. But the chief constable catches him by the arms and lifts him to his feet.

程和光：不必如此，这本就是我分内之事。
Cheng Heguang: Please, sir. I am merely fulfilling my duty.

程和光：我答应你，一定会查明真相。
Cheng Heguang: I will find the truth. This I swear.

祝县县民Ⅰ：谢谢……
County Resident I: Thank you.

程和光：你在这里歇歇再回去吧，切勿过于劳神，伤及身体。
Cheng Heguang: Rest a while. Best not to overwork yourself.

程和光：来人！
Cheng Heguang: Guard!

巡捕Ⅰ：程巡检。
Constable I: Chief.

程和光：照顾好这位报案人，我要去旁听“高跷巡神案”的审理。
Cheng Heguang: Take care of the good man. I must deliver my report on the events at the opera.

巡捕Ⅰ：是。
Constable I: Understood.

程和光拍了拍男子的肩，走出门去。
Chéng Héguāng pats the poor man's shoulder as they walk out.

一缕风随着他的动作越过门槛，散往远处。
A breeze follows him past the door and scatters far away.

衙署大堂内，一场临时汇报正在进行。
In the great hall, a report on the case is being given to the gathered court.

主簿：……女道士以剑相抚一名村姑的头顶，女子现出原形，枯黄的根茎重新变为青绿色。
Registrar: The female Daoist raised her sword above a woman's head, revealing the latter's true form to be that of a herbaceous entity and shifting her withered leaves into a verdant green.

主簿：随后，她对台下众人称可赐人长生，听到此话，场下的精怪与百姓失神一般涌上戏台。
Registrar: The Daoist then proclaimed the ability to bestow longevity upon any who joined her school. This declaration incited the crowd to a frenzy as they stampeded the stage.

主簿：……之后，仙人与村姑不知所踪。我们抓捕了部分精怪，并救治了十数位在踩踏中受伤的百姓。
Registrar: Later, the Daoist vanished from the scene together with the herbaceous entity. Several Yao present were detained, and the injured were escorted to the nearest clinic for treatment.

主簿：综上所述，这应该是在“高跷巡神”的戏台上由烛火妖法引起的意外。
Registrar: In summary, the stampede has been determined to be an unforeseen incident arising from the female Daoist's use of arcane skills.

汇报结束，条陈被重新折起，呈递到知县手中。
With the report concluded, the paper is folded once more and then handed over to the county magistrate.

知县：哼，意外？“高跷巡神”出事后，到处都有那长生之法的谣传。
County Magistrate: "Unforeseen incident"? Your lack of foresight has seen this longevity rumor spread to every corner of the county!

知县：精怪疯了一样往城里挤，东坊报邻里失踪，西坊报妖书妖言，我这桌案几天之内就垒了堪比几个月的本子！
County Magistrate: Yao are flooding our lands in droves! Never in my life have I received so many reports of missing persons and acts of sedition!

知县：这就是你们干的好事！
County Magistrate: Make no mistake. This is the result of your errors!

知县将条陈揉成一团，直直砸到主簿身上，而堂下的人只是把腰弓得更低了。
The magistrate crumples the paper and throws it at the registrar. In response, the man bows even lower.

知县：唉，我知道你们是指望不上了。
County Magistrate: *sigh* We were foolish to put our faith in you.

知县：厉守备，我借调你来管城防，如今……你说怎么办？
County Magistrate: Commander Lì, you are in charge of our defenses. Tell me, how should we proceed?

一旁伫立的男人沉吟片刻，缓缓开口。
Lì Huìfēng had been standing nearby; he pauses, considering the details for a moment, before speaking out in a measured tone.

厉晦锋：非常时期当用非常之法。
Li Huifeng: In these desperate times, I can see only one solution.

厉晦锋：官兵吏员分为两班，昼夜盘查，力争三日内肃清所有混入城中的精怪。
Li Huifeng: I would divide all constables into two shifts and have them sweep the entire county. We will locate and apprehend all Yao hiding among the populace over the next three days.

知县：甚好，甚好！都听到了吗！谁若是偷奸耍滑，休怪本县不留情面！
County Magistrate: Very good! Do you hear that? All departments will cooperate with Commander Lì! And if I hear of any misconduct, I will show no mercy!

众人唯唯诺诺，抱揖称是。
The others hasten to agree as they bow with clasped hands.

程和光几欲开口，如今寻到机会，赶忙上前一步。
Chéng Héguāng has been wanting to speak. Seeing his chance, he seizes it and steps forward.

程和光：属下以为，精怪之外，梅花教也需严加盘查！
Cheng Heguang: Honorable Magistrate, I believe we also ought to consider investigating the School of Mei.

其余吏员偷偷抬眼，看向这粒被筛落的黄豆。
The other clerks sneak sneering glances toward him, like a discolored bean sifted from the pile.

知县：你？哦……我对你有印象……你是……程巡检，对吧？
County Magistrate: And you are? Wait, I believe I recall, Chief Chéng, is it?

知县：梅花教？可是那活跃于县内的小教？
County Magistrate: And this School of Mei? A minor religious sect, yes?

程和光：是。秉知县，属下正追查动物遗尸的案件，庭审前才顺藤摸瓜寻到了梅花教，还未来得及写到案卷之上。
Cheng Heguang: Yes. Please forgive me. After the report was submitted, I discovered a connection between the sect and the animal carcasses found on the streets.

程和光：已有涉事精怪承认，那神秘游行队伍是梅花教在背后指使，而长生谣言和动物遗尸与这支游行队伍又有颇多联系。
Cheng Heguang: While in custody, a suspect admitted that the School of Mei was behind the mysterious parade connected to both the rumors and the drained carcasses.

程和光：因此，“戏台授长生”的闹剧极有可能也是出自梅花教的手笔。精怪是叶，梅花教才是根。
Cheng Heguang: I believe this opera was another part of their scheme. If the Yao are the fruit, the School of Mei is the root.

官吏们收回目光，忍不住窃窃私语。
The others look away and whisper.

县丞：这就是那个程巡检？次次都抢着出头的那个？
Deputy Magistrate: And who are you to speak? Some upstart boy desperate to clear his family name?

主簿：对，就是他。上个月捕盗还和咱们衙门抢功劳，争得面红耳赤。
Registrar: That's him alright. Just last month, he was ranting about some thief-catching scheme; the argument could be heard from the streets.

县丞：去岁考核，咱们原本报了无事太平，他抓了几个逃兵，非要年前交上去。
Deputy Magistrate: Do you remember last year? This boy nigh on knocked the doors down, insisting we include those deserters he caught in our update to the Imperial Court.

县丞：你是不知道，当时知县老爷脸都黑了……只想着向上爬，一点处世之道也不会。
Deputy Magistrate: Hard to believe the magistrate allowed him to leave with his head. It seems he hasn't any sense for his position or his shame.

主簿：他那背景你也知道，急着摇尾巴表忠心呗……
Registrar: The son of a bandit turncoat. No wonder he barks like a dog, demanding praise for his every deed.

主簿：要我看，贼就是贼，终究是上不了台面……
Registrar: He's fooling himself if he thinks he can wash himself clean of his family's past.

程和光对这些低语置若罔闻，只是如松柏一样扎在原地。
Chéng Héguāng ignores their whispers and stands tall and firm as a noble pine.

知县：厉守备……你看此事……
County Magistrate: Commander Lì, thoughts on this matter?

众人安静了下来，厉晦锋干咳几声，开口说道。
As all else goes quiet, Lì Huìfēng clears his throat and speaks.

厉晦锋：不论如何，都不可放任精怪在县内胡作非为，将其驱逐，维护县内治安才是重中之重。
Li Huifeng: Ahem. I hold to what I've said before; the Yao pose a serious danger to the people. Our priority must be to expel them from the county.

厉晦锋：知县觉得如何？
Li Huifeng: What would you have us do, Your Honor?

知县：这事便交付给守备了，大家散了吧。
County Magistrate: The matter is handed to Commander Lì. Dismissed.

众人：是！
Constables: Understood.

程和光：可梅花教一事……
Cheng Heguang: But the School of Mei ...

眼看众人就要这么散去，程和光着了急，他四下寻找，仅剩厉晦锋还在廊下等他。
The others seem prepared to leave, but Chéng Héguāng looks around anxiously, until finding the familiar shape of his commander waiting under the eaves.

程和光：厉守备！
Cheng Heguang: Commander Lì!

厉晦锋：和光，你过来一下。
Li Huifeng: Come here, Héguāng.

厉晦锋快步走出大堂，程和光不得不后面小步疾走。
Lì Huìfēng walks from the hall in long, quick strides, forcing his subordinate to hurry to keep pace.

厉晦锋：和光，你难道就一刻也等不得？
Li Huifeng: Are you really so desperate for glory that you forget the chain of command?

厉晦锋：你这样不管不顾，如何能破得了案子？
Li Huifeng: How do you aim to win trust if you refuse to pay respect to your betters?

程和光：守备，我知道我不该隔越奏事。
Cheng Heguang: I apologize, Commander.

程和光：可那梅花教的事，我已经从精怪口中得知确切线索！此时不查，更待何时？
Cheng Heguang: But this is a promising lead. If we don't act now, we may miss our chance.

厉晦锋转过身来，语气是前所未有的严厉。
Lì Huìfēng turns, his voice sterner than ever.

厉晦锋：你有线索，难道就你有线索？
Li Huifeng: Do you think you're the only one with a lead on this case?

厉晦锋：你区区一个巡检都能知道，其他人能不知道？你能查到，其他人能查不到？
Li Huifeng: That no one else can do as you have done? Not even those with greater power and resources?

厉晦锋：你自持正义，便光明磊落袒露线索。可并非人人都是如此。若他人堂上听去，暗中通风。你还能有线索吗？
Li Huifeng: Is that why you announced your intentions for all to hear? Your heart may be pure, but others have their own designs. If your words reach the wrong ears, do you think they will sit and do nothing about it?

程和光徒劳地张开了嘴，他本做好了挨一顿批评的准备。
Chéng Héguāng's tongue twists. He had prepared for a scolding, not this.

程和光：守备的意思是……
Cheng Heguang: Commander, you mean ...

厉晦锋：继续追查精怪，不要打草惊蛇。
Li Huifeng: Keep digging, but do not draw any further attention.

厉晦锋：今天的事到此为止。这些话，当我没有说过。
Li Huifeng: That's all for today. And if your actions are brought to light, I will tell them I denied your request, understood?

程和光：……是，守备！
Cheng Heguang: Yes, Commander!

少年人领略行礼，身姿重新变得挺拔。
He bows deeply, then straightens his posture.

程和光：守备的教诲，我定会牢记于心。
Cheng Heguang: I will learn from your wise words.

SU-12 梦中天台 / Castle in the Sky

bg图

任仙子：来吧，惠姑。正式修行前，我先带你熟悉一下教门。
Master Ren: Come, Mayfly. You ought to familiarize yourself with our school before you begin.

惠姑：照……
Mayfly: Yes, Master.

惠姑从房门探出身来，好奇地看向前庭。
Mayfly peeks out from behind the door, watching the others in the front courtyard.

惠姑：这才卯时，大家就开始修炼啦……
Mayfly: It's still early in the morning, but everyone's already up and busy.

任仙子：是啊，你很快也会成为它们中的一员的。
Master Ren: It is. Soon, you will be practicing alongside them.

看见惠姑，有不少已经面熟的小精怪向她点头致意。
The many Yao she has come to know nod to her in greeting.

任仙子：这边是厢房，是弟子们日常起居的场所，你以后也会一直住在这里。有些人你可能已经面熟了。
Master Ren: The students live in the side house here, as will you. I believe you've met some of them already.

灵巧的耗子：吱吱！
Quick Mouse: *squeak*

惠姑：呀——咦？为什么在墙上装一半的竹筒？刚才有耗子钻进去了……
Mayfly: I see, ah! There's a mouse climbing up on that bamboo by the wall.

任仙子：那是你的一位师兄，他好用真身行走。
Master Ren: Heh. Don't be alarmed by Brother Mouse. He has taken to staying in his true form most of the day.

惠姑：师、师兄好！
Mayfly: F-Forgive me, Brother.

任仙子：他已经走了。梅花教是属于精怪们的教门，在这里我们不强制大家化为人形，如果你想的话，作为一根苇草生活在这里也是可行的。
Master Ren: I'm sure he does not mind. The School of Mei is one of the few refuges for Yao in this region. Our students are free to live in whatever form they wish. You may even choose to live as a reed, if that is what you desire.

惠姑：作为一根苇草……吗……
Mayfly: Live in my true form. But I ...

任仙子：物各有性，径自分殊，得道的办法不止一种。
Master Ren: One must learn to find fulfillment in their true nature; only then may one discern their path to the Way. It will make sense in time.

惠姑：唔……
Mayfly: Hmm.

任仙子：走吧，我带你去前庭。
Master Ren: Come. Let us speak further in the front courtyard.

惠姑：仙子，这一路上我一直听见奏乐之声，可是我怎么都找不着是在哪里传来的。
Mayfly: Master, where is that music coming from? I keep hearing it, but I don't see anyone playing.

任仙子：少安毋躁，很快你就能见到他们。
Master Ren: You won't have need of that haste much longer, Sister Mayfly.

任仙子：此处是前庭，不论是修炼还是偷闲，大家平日聚在这里多些。
Master Ren: This is the front courtyard, where students may gather to train or rest as they like.

惠姑：可是现在这里好像一个人都没有。
Mayfly: But no one's here.

任仙子：这边。
Master Ren: This way.

江南的园林讲究巧妙的遮掩，月洞门之后再走过三两弯小径，又是别有一番洞天。
The gardens of this land excel at artful concealment. Past the moon gate, after a few winding paths, a hidden world opens up to her.

乌顶的檐压着洁白的厢房围成了一个正方形，碎砂石铺成的地上，汉白玉制成的长方形石砖被摆成了一个八卦阵的形状。
Black eaves press down upon white rooms that enclose a square. The ground is paved with gravel, into which white marble tiles are set, forming a Bagua array.

一群白衣弟子正站在八卦阵之上，齐奏着肃穆的道乐。
Students in white stand atop it, playing solemn Daoist music together.

山药精：小师妹好！
Yam: There she is, the new student!

刺猬精：师妹……身子可好点了？
Hedgehog: Sister Mayfly, are you feeling better?

鹭鸶剪也早就等在这里，众多弟子不时会瞅向这边。
Paper Heron waits here too. The students occasionally steal small glances at her.

她环视周围，见此地聚集人数众多，时不时便向弟子们点点头，见到惠姑也打了声招呼。
She looks around, nodding to the students as she meets their eyes and greeting Mayfly in particular.

惠姑：各位……在这里做什么呢？
Mayfly: Hello, everyone, what are you all doing here?

众妖：任仙子！
All Yao: Master Rén is here too!

众妖：请任仙子为我们传道授业！
All Yao: Greetings, Master! We humbly request your guidance this day!

任仙子：好，好。
Master Ren: It's good to see you all. Please, be seated.

众人散开，绕着任仙子围成了一个圈儿坐下。其中一位女性精怪亲切地拉过惠姑，让她在自己身边坐了下来。
The crowd spreads out and sits in a ring around Master Rén. A female Yao pulls Mayfly in to sit beside her.

任仙子：今日有新的弟子加入，我们便先温故，简单复习一下长生之法的根基，然后再知新。
Master Ren: Revision always offers new insight. And with a new student among us today, let us begin by reviewing the stages of the Method of Longevity.

任仙子：修行长生之法的阶段如下，分别为“调气”“存元”和“易筋”……
Master Ren: To master this art, one must attain three stages: the regulation of Qi, concentration and visualization, and the cultivation of the body.

任仙子：调气，是指练习呼吸和吐纳，具体的姿势和吐纳方式需根据你们个人的体质而定。
Master Ren: In the first stage, we focus on the rhythm of the breath. Each of you must find the pace which best suits your constitution and nature.

任仙子：存元，则是需要你们在高度入静的情况下，将意念集中于神内或身外，易筋，便是……
Master Ren: Once you reach a state of meditation, we will work to concentrate the mind on an object, opening ourselves to the stimuli of the divine, as for the cultivation of the body.

听到这里，鹭鸶剪打断了任仙子。
Hearing this, Paper Heron interrupts Master Rén.

鹭鸶剪：这不大好。
Paper Heron: That wouldn't be for the best.

任仙子：怎么了？
Master Ren: Whatever do you mean, Master?

鹭鸶剪：你这开口非根非基，徒儿们练功岂不是如空中楼阁？从头讲会更好些。
Paper Heron: Your students are getting ahead of themselves. Teach them the basics first, eh? A pavilion is not built from the roof down.

任仙子：长生之法渊源已久，从头讲的话，那便涵盖整个白马派的历史了。
Master Ren: If I am to cover every foundational detail, I would have to start from before the White Horse School was even founded.

任仙子：我虽能算作白马派的传人，却从未真实在教门中修习过……还是由你来为大家讲述会更好些。
Master Ren: Unfortunately, I never walked its halls. All that I know, I learned from you. Would you do us the honor, Grandmaster?

任仙子：若弟子们能因此了解功法传承之脉络，也算幸事一桩。
Master Ren: The students would be most grateful to hear it from your lips.

鹭鸶剪环视一圈，见众弟子都对自己的讲解翘首以盼，门派生机盎然，当下心中一阵宽慰。
Paper Heron looks around. The students wait eagerly for her words. The School of Mei seems to be thriving on the high morale of its students, and her heart is warmed by it.

鹭鸶剪：倒是好久没跟人讲过这些了……好，今日便由我来！
Paper Heron: It has been quite some time since I last spoke of my old school, but I'd be happy to.

鹭鸶剪轻提脚跟，纵身跃进圈中，开始为众人讲解。
She lifts her heels and leaps gracefully into the ring before launching into her story.

鹭鸶剪：“长生之法”最早可以追溯到上古时期，但从白马派听起也算开了个好头。
Paper Heron: The very first attempts at achieving longevity can be traced back to ancient times, but it's enough to start with the founding of the White Horse School, eh?

鹭鸶剪：白马派始于晚唐，师祖因注重道法传承，便前往各地搜集经法残章。
Paper Heron: It first took shape in the late Tang Dynasty, as our founding master traveled the land collecting many rare and lost scriptures in hopes of preserving the Daoist arts for future generations.

鹭鸶剪：在研读残卷的过程中，他融会贯通，从中研究出了一套可炼养阴阳之气，从而延年益寿的心法。
Paper Heron: From those arts, he developed a method to balance Yin and Yang, and through it, discovered the secret to a long life.

鹭鸶剪：师祖将其命名为“金丹术”，而此术便成为了我们“白马派”的根基。
Paper Heron: He named it The Practice of Inner Alchemy, and it later became the foundation of the White Horse School.

鹭鸶剪：“金丹术”修炼过程是这样的，你们听好。
Paper Heron: Now, to perform it properly, you must work through these stages in order. Listen closely.

鹭鸶剪：第一步，“人能常清静，天地悉皆归。”你们需得放下世情，去寻求内心的沉静，以此得以揣摩天道的意义。
Paper Heron: The scripture says, "When one's mind is tranquil and free of distracting thoughts, all things between heaven and earth will become one with it." So, the first step is to set aside worldly concerns and seek stillness from within, for only then can one perceive the presence of the Way.

鹭鸶剪：第二步，感受自己体内的“气”，“人之生，气之聚也。聚则为生，散则为死。”
Paper Heron: Step two is about finding your Qi. "Life is born of the accumulation of Qi. When Qi gathers, we live; when it disperses, we perish."

鹭鸶剪：“气”便是我们修身养性，从而延年益寿的关键，我们需要通过漫长的摸索来认识自己体内的“气”，熟知它的流转。
Paper Heron: Without Qi, we can neither strengthen our bodies nor nourish our spirits, and so we cannot prolong our lives. We must spend years learning its workings, until it becomes as familiar to us as our own hands.

鹭鸶剪：第三步，你们需融会贯通，要学会引导自身的“气”，改变其本来的运转方式，使之融入天道。
Paper Heron: The third step is to use your understanding of Qi to work its flow, guiding it until it moves in harmony with the Way.

鹭鸶剪：而接下来这步是重中之重，你们需得让体内的“气”和身体慢慢磨合，切不可急躁。
Paper Heron: This step is the most crucial—when your body attunes itself to your Qi and allows you to retain it. This may take some time, but it must not be rushed.

鹭鸶剪：“道炁不居人身，人身则空，人身既空，何得久生？”
Paper Heron: "Without the Qi within, the body stands hollow. And if hollow, how may life endure in it?"

鹭鸶剪：你们需日复一日，持之以恒地潜心修行，磨炼自己的肉体凡胎，使它与体内的“气”和谐共存。
Paper Heron: This takes real devotion. You must practice daily until your body is ready to harmonize with the flow of Qi.

鹭鸶剪：“保气则得道，得道则长存”说的便是这个道理。
Paper Heron: "To retain Qi is to attain the Way; one who has attained the Way may long endure," so the scripture says.

鹭鸶剪：但这磨合的过程漫长且凶险，稍有不慎，修炼者便会走火入魔，更甚者则会神形俱灭。
Paper Heron: But the path is long and perilous. Stray from it, and both body and spirit may be annihilated.

鹭鸶剪：快的话，这个磨合的过程一般会持续个几十年，慢的话……修炼了上百年的人我也是见过。
Paper Heron: At best, it is a process of decades; at worst, well, I've seen some wait hundreds of years.

刺猬精：师、师祖……
Hedgehog: But, Grandmaster ...

鹭鸶剪：嗯，你说。
Paper Heron: Yes? Speak your mind.

刺猬精：您说……这个过程……要经历个几十年，甚至上百年吗？
Hedgehog: Do you really mean it will take a few decades for us to master this method?

鹭鸶剪：这便是长生，越是静心修炼，不问外界，越是能凝神聚气，形神俱妙。
Paper Heron: To walk the path of longevity is no small feat. But the calmer your mind, the clearer your vision, and the quicker you will progress.

刺猬精：可是……我的寿命也不过数载而已，如何能经历这么久的时间呢？按照师祖所说，岂不是只有长生之人才能修得长生之法了？
Hedgehog: But how can I devote myself to a method that takes decades to master when I only have a few years to live? And if what you say is true, wouldn't only the long-lived be able to achieve longevity?

鹭鸶剪：这……
Paper Heron: Ah!

鹭鸶剪沉吟半晌，踱步至艮卦之上。
She pauses, composing her thoughts for a long while, then walks over to the Gen trigram.

鹭鸶剪：并非如此。有道是，“为学日益，为道日损。损之又损，以至于无为。无为而无不为。”
Paper Heron: Not entirely. The scripture says, "In the pursuit of worldly knowledge, one gains daily. In the pursuit of the Way, one loses daily. Less and less is done, until nothing is done. When nothing is done, nothing is left undone."

鹭鸶剪：你们莫陷入执念，活好当下，自然会有你们的机缘出现。
Paper Heron: Don't get so hung up on the path ahead. Nothing stays fixed forever. Live in the moment, and new opportunities will arise.

刺猬精：难道要我什么都不做吗……
Hedgehog: So we'll just do nothing at all?

鹭鸶剪：也不对。无为而无不为，并非是要你什么都不做，而是要做你该做的命内事。
Paper Heron: Not exactly. It isn't nothing but rather "non-action." We let go of all deliberate effort, attending to your purposes, doing only that which is yours to do.

听了鹭鸶剪一席话，底下的小妖们纷纷面面相觑。一只精怪按捺不住自己的性子，突然冲出人群。
Hearing her words, the Yao look at each other. One of them cannot hold back their frustration and rushes up in front of her.

獾子精：这是什么话！
Badger: That's absurd!

獾子精：我们本来寿命相比你们仙人的就要短，我们该做的命内事岂不就是乖乖等着寿命耗尽？
Badger: If that's how it is, what are we to do? Sit around and wait for death to come? Our lives are much shorter than yours, you know!

山药精：诶诶，獾兄别着急，万一师祖……
Yam: Now, now, Brother Badger. The grandmaster didn't mean ...

突然冲出的小妖并未听从同门的劝阻，继续发问。
Undeterred by the gentle redirection, the Yao continues its questions anyway.

獾子精：到底什么才是命内事？我投入梅花教，算不算命内事？
Badger: "That which is yours to do." What's that supposed to mean? Is this "what's mine to do"?

刺猬精：师祖，我们……我们来投奔梅花教，也不是想坐着等死啊……
Hedgehog: Grandmaster, none of us would be here if we had been content with the time we were given.

鹭鸶剪：这……
Paper Heron: Ah ...

鹭鸶剪一时语塞，发现这个问题似乎从一开始就错位了。
Paper Heron is speechless. She sees now the crux of the issue; they have been led astray from the very beginning.

眼见不服之声越来越大，众妖的情绪也越来越激动，鹭鸶剪站在人群中手足无措，惠姑亦不知如何是好。
The doubting voices grow louder. The Yao become agitated. Paper Heron stands silent above them, lost. Mayfly struggles in her seat, not knowing who to agree with.

任仙子：好了！
Master Ren: Alright, everyone.

一声清亮的高喊传出，如同石子落入水面，众妖瞬间安静了下来。
A clear, loud call rings out like a stone dropped in water. The Yao immediately fall silent.

獾子精：师父……
Badger: Master.

任仙子踱步至圈内，站到了鹭鸶剪的旁边。
Master Rén walks into the ring and stands beside her teacher.

任仙子：师祖肆意潇洒惯了，为人处世自有她的一番道理在，却并不一定就是天理。
Master Ren: Each of us approaches the Way differently, for we are all guided by our own nature. The grandmaster speaks only from her own experience.

任仙子：你们听了能有启发是最好，也不必因这番话徒增烦恼，只需先记在心里，日后说不定会有顿悟的时候。
Master Ren: If her words help you, hold them. If they muddle you, do not be troubled. You may understand them in the time to come.

山药精：谨遵任仙子教诲。
Yam: Yes, Master.

任仙子：师祖远道而来实在疲乏，还得陪你们胡闹，还是让她歇歇吧。
Master Ren: It's been a long day, and the grandmaster has traveled far. Please, leave her to rest.

鹭鸶剪看了看任仙子，又看了看被安抚好的精怪们，随后不自然地点了点头，坐到了圈外的石凳上。
Paper Heron looks at her former student and then at the calmed Yao. With a stiff nod, she resigns herself to a stone stool outside the ring.

惠姑：鹭……鹭鸶剪，你还好吗？
Mayfly: Heron, are you alright?

惠姑轻轻走了过来，坐在了稍显不安的鹭鸶剪身旁。
She walks over and sits by Paper Heron, whose serene facade now seems ever so subtly broken.

鹭鸶剪：我还好，只是看样子，我……似乎说错了话。
Paper Heron: I'm fine. Should've chosen my words with more care, though.

惠姑：那个……
Mayfly: Well ...

惠姑不知道说什么好，一时之间，周围的蝉鸣和鸟叫逐渐显得刺耳了起来。
For a moment, the cicada chirps and bird calls sound unusually sharp.

鹭鸶剪低着头，惠姑看不到她的表情。
Paper Heron looks down, hiding her face.

鹭鸶剪：我本以为……本以为大家都会很乐意学这法子的，明明从前……
Paper Heron: I thought they'd be interested. Back in my time ...

一句小声的咕嚷从惠姑耳边传来，声音细微得几乎听不见。
The words are a faint whisper, so light she barely hears them.

惠姑：什么？
Mayfly: What do you mean?

鹭鸶剪：……没什么，你们继续跟着任仙子修炼吧。
Paper Heron: Nothing. Just forget what I've said and follow your master's teachings.

鹭鸶剪：也许……也许她找到了更好的，更贴近天道的法门呢……
Paper Heron: Perhaps she's found a better way.

任仙子：……关于师祖提到的第三步，便是“易筋”，即让肉身与体内的“气”慢慢融汇，最终浑然一体。
Master Ren: The third step the grandmaster spoke of is what we call the "cultivation of the body." Through practice, your body will work with your Qi until they are one.

任仙子：“易筋”原需数十年，甚至为期百年的修炼，但梅花教的“长生之法”无需特意练习“易筋”，而更注重于“调气”和“存元”……
Master Ren: Mastering this may take decades, even hundreds of years, but here in the School of Mei, we needn't dwell on that step. Instead, we focus on the regulation of Qi, and concentration and visualization.

鹭鸶剪：……
Paper Heron: ...

鹭鸶剪若有所思地望着正在讲解的任仙子，表情逐渐凝重起来。
She looks over to Master Rén as she continues her lesson and resolves herself to what must be done.

鹭鸶剪：“无需特意练习易筋”？
Paper Heron: "We needn't dwell on that step"?

SU-13 直如弦 / Unbending Will

烟尘

巡捕Ⅱ：让道让道！执行公务！
Constable II: Move! Constables on duty. Make way!

日已西斜，巡捕们却握弓佩刀，气势汹汹地穿越街道。
The sun sets in the west. Meanwhile, constables armed with bows and blades march through the streets.

百姓们好奇地望着这一条藏青色的长龙，相视过后寒暄几句，也不知巡捕们是要去向何方。
Like a long, cobalt dragon, they pass by as people watch curiously and whisper to each other, wondering at their destination.

长龙之首处，两名巡捕紧赶慢赶地追着带头的青年。
Two constables hurry to reach the young man leading the grim-faced parade.

杨武：程巡检，那苇草精就像钻进了石头缝里，根本找不着一点踪迹。
Yang Wu: Chief, there's no trace of that reed girl anywhere. She's disappeared.

程和光：我知道了。先抓别的，私下留心着她。
Cheng Heguang: I see. Stay sharp and keep an eye out for her. We can't allow any more Yao to escape.

杜六：西门的巡捕又抓住了两个，过来问巡检是否要去看看。
Du Liu: News from the west gate: two more Yao have been captured. Do you want to question them yourself like last time?

程和光：知道了，过会儿就去。
Cheng Heguang: I'll be there shortly.

杨武：对了，程巡检，我们这是要去——
Yang Wu: We've been walking for a while now. Where are you leading us?

杨武还欲说些什么，程和光却已经举起右手，示意后面跟随的巡捕停下脚步。
Yáng Wǔ still wants to speak, but their chief raises his right hand, signaling the marching constables behind to stop.

程和光：到了！
Cheng Heguang: This is it!

面前的府邸位于街道尽处，门扉紧闭，难以窥探。然而，若有若无的唱诵声固执地从砖缝里飘出。
The house before them lies at the street's end. Its doors are tightly shut, but chanting voices escape out through the cracks.

？？？：黑绒吞白骨，寒原鬼泣呜……城覆仙人现，长生免祸殃……
???: Withered grass devours bone. On icy plain the spirits moan. When the city falls, the Immortal descends. Longevity granted, no death, no end.

？？？：一气归元，长生可望。命本可改，道只传人！莫待他朝，永驻仙乡！
???: All returns to origin. Longevity draws near. Stars will shift only when the true path appears. Depart from this strange world, and find peace in the immortal realm.

程和光：哼，果然和线报一样，有精怪聚众修炼！
Cheng Heguang: Hmph. The source was right. Yao are gathering here.

程和光对着门扉握拳，而后猛地抬起。
Chéng Héguāng clenches his fist toward the door, then lifts it in a sharp upward motion.

化为金属的门闩应声而落。
The metal bolt falls with a clang.

程和光：走！
Cheng Heguang: Move in!

庭院
震动

程和光抽刀撞开府门，众巡捕紧跟着涌入这四四方方的小庭院内，不停晃动手中的振气铃。
He draws his blade and throws the door open. The constables pour into the small square courtyard, ringing their Reversion Bells.

程和光：巡检司抓贼！闲杂人等退避！
Cheng Heguang: Patrol constables! Civilians, stay back!

富商巨贾Ⅰ：你们是谁？！
Prominent Local Merchant I: By whose order are you here? Who gave you the right?

程和光：区区小妖，装模作样。
Cheng Heguang: Hmph, quite the posture for a wanted suspect.

程和光：巡检司办案，统统拿下！
Cheng Heguang: You're all under arrest. Seize them!

富商巨贾Ⅱ：大胆！小小巡检司，知不知道我们都是谁——
Prominent Local Merchant II: This is outrageous! You jumped-up toll collector! How dare you lay your hands on us!

富商巨贾Ⅱ：吵死了！
Prominent Local Merchant II: Urgh! What on earth is that noise?

富商巨贾Ⅰ：别摇了！别摇了！
Prominent Local Merchant I: That's enough! I said enough! Stop!

振气铃响彻屋檐。人们捂住耳朵，但却没有长出尾巴，或是化为树皮。
The bells ring under the eaves. Those inside cover their ears, but no tails grow, and no bark forms to cover their skin.

程和光：……不是妖怪？
Cheng Heguang: They're not Yao?

程和光诧异地站定，这些人穿着华贵的绫罗绸缎，更像是达官贵人，而非预想中的精怪流民。
The young chief constable is struck still, grappling with the unexpected outcome. These people dressed in fine silks are wealthy merchants, not Yao cultists.

门外，稍有资历的巡捕们正小心翼翼地窥视着。只有些刚来报到的新人还拼命地摇着振气铃。
From outside, older, wiser constables peek in, while the newer, oblivious recruits continue to ring their bells as ordered.

程和光：都先停下！
Cheng Heguang: Stop the bells!

巡捕们停下摇铃，程和光将人群左右扫视一遍，而后将刀收入鞘内。
The constables stop, and Chéng Héguāng looks over the crowd before sheathing his blade.

程和光：我奉命调查扰乱“高跷巡神”的教门精怪，相关之人一律严拿究办。
Cheng Heguang: I am Chief Constable Chéng, acting under orders to investigate the Yao involved in the Stilted Parade. I have been instructed to bring them to justice without delay.

程和光：你们刚刚所唱的，正是精怪教门在“高跷巡神”前后宣扬的长生妖法。如有得罪，还请莫怪。
Cheng Heguang: The verses you were reciting are identical to those the Yao chanted at the parade. If I am mistaken, I humbly ask for your forgiveness in advance.

富商巨贾Ⅱ：你的意思是，我们是修炼妖术的妖怪？
Prominent Local Merchant II: Can you believe this petulant boy? He thought we were Yao gathering for some evil ritual!

富商巨贾Ⅱ：岂有此理，你可知道这叫诬告！
Prominent Local Merchant II: Watch yourself, "Chief Constable." Slandering a respected merchant like myself could get you in serious trouble!

程和光：律法面前不分贵贱，我也是依律行事，还请各位大人理解，和我回衙门一趟，将事情解释清楚。
Cheng Heguang: All are equal before the law. I only act in accordance with it. I ask your presence at the Yamen, so please, gentlemen, come with us.

程和光：若各位大人念诵的并非教门经文，下官自会赔礼道歉。
Cheng Heguang: Should you be proven innocent, I will offer my deepest apologies.

富商巨贾Ⅲ：好大的口气，你可知我们是谁？
Prominent Local Merchant III: Do you know who you're speaking to, boy?

富商巨贾Ⅲ：把你的上司叫出来，我倒要听听他下的是什么令——
Prominent Local Merchant III: I won't leave this house unless your superior comes and explains everything in person!

程和光：这——
Cheng Heguang: I ...

气氛如千钧沉重，巡捕们面面相觑，谁都不敢开这个口。
The air feels heavy as lead. The constables look at each other, no one daring to speak.

若不是门外传来那道声音，这场对峙还不知何时才能收场。
For a moment, the standstill feels as if it might go on forever, until the tension is at last cut by a voice from outside.

厉晦锋：——这是个误会。
Li Huifeng: Gentlemen, I'm afraid there's been a misunderstanding.

程和光：……守备？
Cheng Heguang: Sir?

巡捕们让出道路。厉晦锋疾步走入院内，身后还跟着一位身穿锦缎的发福中年男子。
The constables part respectfully as Lì Huìfēng marches into the courtyard, followed by a plump middle-aged man in brocade.

厉晦锋：各位大人只是来此唱诵经典，修身养性。
Li Huifeng: Those honorable gentlemen are simply studying the classics and cultivating their minds.

厉晦锋：与“高跷巡神”的风波绝无相关，妖怪妖法更是无稽之谈。
Li Huifeng: It has nothing to do with the turmoil on the streets, nor with the Yao's evil deeds.

富商巨贾Ⅳ：厉守备所言极是！这是张真人手抄的三卷经典，念诵可使人神智通明，绝非什么长生妖法。
Prominent Local Merchant IV: You speak the truth, Commander. These classics the gentlemen were reciting are scriptures transcribed by His Eminence Zhāng himself! They serve only to enlighten the mind.

富商巨贾Ⅳ：定是这位巡检急于捉妖，被奸诈精怪哄骗，这才不慎冲撞了各位大人，是吧，厉守备？
Prominent Local Merchant IV: But no doubt our young Chief Constable here only intended to perform his duties and perhaps leaped to judgment. Is that so, Commander?

厉晦锋：幸好您派人来及时相告，场面才没有弄得更加难堪，我之后一定会严厉斥责他。和光，给各位大人说声不是。
Li Huifeng: I thank you for your understanding and your timely message, else this could have been an even greater humiliation. Héguāng, apologize to the honorable gentlemen.

程和光却未接话，只是定定看着那男子手中的经文书卷。
Chéng Héguāng remains silent and stares at the scripture scroll in the man's hand.

厉晦锋：——程和光！你还不知错？
Li Huifeng: Chéng Héguāng! Do you not hear me?

程和光：……是卑职鲁莽了，请各位大人海涵。
Cheng Heguang: I acted thoughtlessly. For that I am sorry, Your Excellencies.

厉晦锋：你这是什么态度？回衙门领六十大板！
Li Huifeng: Do you think that an acceptable apology? When we return to the Yamen, you'll suffer sixty strokes for your insolence!

富商巨贾Ⅳ：唉，厉守备，这是何必？程巡检想必也只是急于捉妖。年轻人嘛，血气方刚，莽撞些也正常——
Prominent Local Merchant IV: Please, no need to be so harsh, Commander. I'm certain the chief acted with the best intentions. Young men often rush to judgment. We've all done the same.

厉晦锋和这中年男人一唱一和，气氛已然缓和了不少。
Speaking back and forth, Lì Huìfēng and the middle-aged merchant ease the tension at last.

院内的几人交换了一个眼神，地位最高的那个终于松口了。
A look passes among those in the courtyard. The obvious leader among them speaks.

富商巨贾Ⅰ：念在没出什么事，这次我们就不计较了。
Prominent Local Merchant I: No real harm has been done to us; do not punish him for doing his duty.

富商巨贾Ⅱ：厉晦锋，管好你的手下！
Prominent Local Merchant II: Just be sure to keep your officers in line, Lì!

厉晦锋：是是，我们这便离开。
Li Huifeng: Of course. Your generosity is greatly appreciated, gentlemen. We shall take our leave.

厉晦锋并未多说什么，只是领着众人离开了庭院。
Lì Huìfēng says no more and signals for the constables to leave the courtyard.

巡捕们耷拉着脸回到县衙，如同烂布沿街拖了十里。
A wounded cobalt dragon retreats back to its cave in the form of a slow and dreary procession of downcast faces.

不断有人用埋怨的眼神看向程和光。尤以跟得最近的杜六和杨武为最。
Lì Huìfēng stands ahead, unconcerned with the sour faces of the lower ranks behind him.

程和光：……
Cheng Heguang: ...

碍于厉晦锋在场，巡捕们也不敢多话，只是作鸟兽状散向饭堂。
With their commander present, the constables dare not even speak as they pass through the doors of the Yamen and file away to the mess hall.

唯有程和光还直挺挺地站在原处。
Only Chéng Héguāng remains by the entrance, struggling to hold his head high. The result is something stiff and strange but proud.

厉晦锋：不去吃饭，是有话要说？
Li Huifeng: Why are you standing there like a statue? It's time to eat.

程和光：属下在等自己的六十大板。
Cheng Heguang: I'm awaiting my sixty strokes.

厉晦锋放下了手中的案卷，眼神复杂地看了一眼程和光。
Lì Huìfēng puts down the case file and looks at him with a complex expression.

厉晦锋：并没有这六十大板。你回去吧。
Li Huifeng: *sigh* There won't be any coming. Now, go eat.

程和光依然分毫未动。
But he still does not move.

程和光：既然没有这六十大板，那属下还想问一事。
Cheng Heguang: If you've elected to spare me, then allow me a question, Commander.

程和光：和守备一起进来的男子，他手中的经文典籍从何而来，为何上面有梅树和玉剑的八卦阵图案？
Cheng Heguang: The man who came with you had a scroll in his hand. Where did it come from? There's a Bagua array on it, formed by a Mei tree and a jade sword.

厉晦锋：既然没有这六十大板，这便不是你该过问的。
Li Huifeng: Héguāng, if I spare you the punishment, you ought to at least do me the courtesy of sparing me the questions.

程和光：那属下便站在这里等着领六十大板。
Cheng Heguang: Then I would rather take the punishment.

晚风吹过冷清的衙门大堂，让案前的烛光闪烁了几分。
The evening wind blows through the hall, and the candlelight flickers in response.

厉晦锋：你知道你今晚得罪的是谁吗？
Li Huifeng: Do you really have no inkling of who you offended tonight?

程和光：属下不知。
Cheng Heguang: I do not.

厉晦锋：陈氏，本地乡绅，一代出了三个进士；陆总兵，更是在此地世袭武职；李家更不必说，你于祝县生长，也该听过他们的名号。
Li Huifeng: The Chén family, respected gentry with three Imperial Scholars in only a few decades. Lord Lù, a corps leader, his family have served in the military for generations. And the Lǐs—I needn't remind you who they are.

程和光：属下本是兵贼出身，门楣低微，自然不知。
Cheng Heguang: I am but the son of bandits. I don't know any of these high lords.

厉晦锋：那你现在该知了。
Li Huifeng: Now you know.

厉晦锋不再看向程和光，只是翻阅手中的案卷。
Lì Huìfēng looks away and reads from the case file.

程和光：那手持经文的男子，也是其中一门显贵？
Cheng Heguang: The man with the scroll—is he of noble birth, too?

厉晦锋不答。
He does not receive an answer.

程和光：你不让我查梅花教，并非惧怕打草惊蛇，而是因为你早就知道？
Cheng Heguang: Am I right to assume that you've kept me from investigating the School of Mei, not because you feared I might alarm them, but because you are aware of the school's prestigious background?

厉晦锋仍是不答。
The words are pointed but do not break his commander's grim silence.

程和光：你早就知道，城中混乱根结在梅花教，但他们有权贵撑腰，所以只是抓些流散精怪，做些表面功夫——
Cheng Heguang: You know they're responsible for the turmoil in the county, yet you permit these men to walk free, allowing the common Yao to take the fall—

厉晦锋：闹够了没有——？！
Li Huifeng: Enough!

厉晦锋猛然站起，将手中的案卷摔到地上。
Lì Huìfēng rises with an expression as fiery as a lit rocket as he throws the files to the ground.

厉晦锋：你知道今天还能站在这里，靠的是谁吗？！
Li Huifeng: Are you so naive? Do you truly have no clue as to why you were spared today?

程和光：……靠的是守备和那持经文男子的关系。
Cheng Heguang: Because of your connection to the man with the scroll.

厉晦锋：你也知道！
Li Huifeng: Then you do have some inkling of what's going on!

厉晦锋：你这几日捉妖有功，我本打算事后向陆总兵推荐你——可你今天却跑去抓他的亲戚。这让我怎么开口？！
Li Huifeng: You did well capturing those Yao, and I had planned to speak highly of you before Lord Lù. But after your actions today—storming into a civilian's home, attempting to arrest all present—how can I possibly recommend you!?

厉晦锋：还是说，你已经忘了你曾经发的誓，甘愿永远带着你父亲留下的污点？！
Li Huifeng: Have you forsaken your vow and decided to live in your father's disgrace forever?

程和光：……属下不曾忘却！
Cheng Heguang: I would never!

程和光咬了咬牙，但并未退让。
He grits his teeth but does not give an inch.

程和光：可是守备，我追查梅花教，并不仅是为了立功升级。只是想避免酿成大祸！
Cheng Heguang: But Commander, this is more important than my name. This is for the safety of the townspeople!

厉晦锋：好！不愧是祝县的好巡检。那我想问问，梅花教造成了什么危害，触犯了哪条刑律？
Li Huifeng: Alright. Then tell me exactly what harm the School of Mei has done and what crime you accuse them of.

程和光：正如我之前汇报，诸多煽动蛊惑之举该坐师巫邪术一条——
Cheng Heguang: As my prior report states, they are practicing sorcery and other forbidden arts.

厉晦锋：那游行的确假降邪神，扶鸾祷圣，可抓着了游行的人，可有画押口供？
Li Huifeng: They fabricated the descent of a deity at the parade, yes. But have you caught any of the offenders from that day?

程和光：……此无实证。
Cheng Heguang: Not yet.

厉晦锋：那可抓到了梅花教的人，或收缴了什么妖书？
Li Huifeng: And has any member of the school actually committed a crime? Or have you found some scripture that proves their evil intention?

程和光：……
Cheng Heguang: ...

程和光：亦无实证。
Cheng Heguang: I have not.

厉晦锋：这也无实证，那也无实证，你要如何说服我——说服知县老爷为了你得罪那些府衙官员？
Li Huifeng: So you have nothing. You wish me to convince the magistrate to act against the School of Mei, risking the anger of officials and high lords based on nothing? Hm?

厉晦锋：他们会说，梅花教不过是个民间修身养性的教派，游行只是幻术。妖怪愚笨，才信了什么长生。
Li Huifeng: The school will claim that they were only teaching the methods to strengthen the body and enrich the mind, and that the Yao were foolish and greedy to think their practices could grant longevity.

厉晦锋：而为了一个谣言冲撞上级，只会显得我们捉妖不力，推卸责任。
Li Huifeng: We cannot act on hearsay and rumors, especially when it may anger the high lords!

程和光：我暂时没有物证，反驳不了守备的话。
Cheng Heguang: You're right. I lack the evidence to refute your words.

程和光：但我可以避开官员，先盯梢别院。三日内，定能抓出切实线索！
Cheng Heguang: But if it is the lords that worry you, I will investigate in secret. Three days is all I need. I will find the proof.

厉晦锋：不必了。
Li Huifeng: Enough.

一阵风吹入堂内，将桌案上的纸张带得簌簌作响。
Another cold blast of wind sweeps through the hall, rustling the papers on his desk.

厉晦锋拿镇纸将案卷压平，坐回木椅。
Lì Huìfēng uses a paperweight to smooth the files and sits back into his chair.

厉晦锋：回去休息吧。
Li Huifeng: Go now. Get some rest.

厉晦锋：你手下的人我会调给张捕头，他对城里更熟悉。以后，你就负责支援吧。
Li Huifeng: Your men are to be placed under Captain Zhāng; he knows the county well. You will remain, but only as his backup.

程和光：——为什么？！
Cheng Heguang: Why? I've done nothing wrong!

厉晦锋：——你还是不知道。
Li Huifeng: *sigh* Then you've not listened to a word I've said.

炉里的水烧开了，咕噜噜地喷着盖子。厉晦锋并不理会。
The water in the pot boils, the lid rattles, the steam whistles, and Lì Huìfēng pays it no attention.

热气逐渐填满程和光的视野，在眼前晃动不止。
Steam fills Chéng Héguāng's sight.

水就要溢出来了。
The pot at last boils over.

程和光：守备！
Cheng Heguang: Commander!

程和光：难道一定要等梅花教害死了人才重视吗！
Cheng Heguang: Must the people's blood be spilled before we act?

厉晦锋：注意你说话的分寸！
Li Huifeng: Watch your tongue!

案上的茶碗里，激起了一丝微弱的涟漪。
In the tea bowl on the desk, weak ripples form.

程和光：……
Cheng Heguang: ...

年轻人在堂前久久立着，直到热气和呵斥一并散去。
The young man stands solid, silent for a long time, rooted like a tree as the steam fades from him.

良久，他才终于挪动生根的脚步。
At last, he breaks the roots and turns.

程和光：……守备的意思我明白了。
Cheng Heguang: Perhaps I have not listened, Commander.

程和光：告辞。
Cheng Heguang: Goodnight.

深夜时分，凉月如水。
The cool moon shines like a lantern over a dark lake.

程和光放下手中的书卷，疲惫地揉了揉脖颈。
Chéng Héguāng puts down a book and rubs his tired neck.

程和光：已不早了。
Cheng Heguang: *sigh* It's getting late.

他借烛火引燃了斜搭在桌腿上焦黑的火把，举着这点光明步入了夜色中。
He lights a blackened torch with a candle, holding the light as he steps into the dark.

程和光：仲尼曰：“君子中庸，小人反中庸。”
Cheng Heguang: Zhòngní said, "One of virtue follows the course of the Mean; one of cunning turns from it."

程和光：“君子之中庸也，君子而时中。小人之反中庸也，小人而无忌惮也。”
Cheng Heguang: "Following the Mean, the virtuous acts in due measure. Turning from the Mean, the cunning moves without restraint."

程和光站在门口处思索着什么。
He stops at the door, deep in thought.

程和光：不早了，但也不算晚。
Cheng Heguang: Fortunately, it's still not too late.

不远处忽然传来野猫的叫声。
A street cat cries out nearby.

切图

程和光：嗯……？那是……
Cheng Heguang: Hm? That's ...

更夫：走水啦！！走水啦！！！
Night Watch: Fire! Fire!

一名县民慌张地奔走着，他身后是熊熊火光。
A man runs in panic. Behind him, plumes of smoke leap and billow into the sky.

更夫：是程巡检家——！程巡检家走水啦！！
Night Watch: There's a fire at Chief Constable Chéng's house!

SU-14 未烧尾 / A Sow's Ear

厢房内，几名小精怪正围着惠姑摘刚从山上采下来的药材。
Inside the room, a few Yao gather around Mayfly, helping her trim the fresh herbs she picked from the mountains.

山药精：惠姑，你记住上山的路没？以后有空的时候你就上山采采药，还能锻炼身体呢。
Yam: Now that you know the path, you can go up the hill at your leisure and gather the elixir ingredients yourself. A little walk in the forest will do you good.

惠姑：我懂得修炼“长生之法”搭配药石进度会更快些，只是……看着这些草药，你不会觉得瘆得慌吗？
Mayfly: Thank you. I know the elixir helps with the practices, but isn't it a little unsettling, harvesting these herbs like this?

山药精：这有什么，它们还未成精，也不算作我们的同类，惠姑你大可放心。
Yam: What's the matter? They're only plants, too young to form any spirit yet. It's not as if you're cutting down one of your own.

鹭鸶剪：惠姑……！咳咳，我来看看你现在如何了？
Paper Heron: Mayfly! Oh, uh, I mean Sister Mayfly, I thought that I should come check on you. See how you're getting on.

惠姑：哎哟，窗户封了，我才知道你还是个不敲门的主。
Mayfly: Look at that. Someone finally discovered the door. Though not much of a knocker, are you?

山药精：师祖。
Yam: Good day, Grandmaster.

鹭鸶剪朝小妖点了点头，随后便围着惠姑转了一圈，左看右看。
Paper Heron nods to the Yao, then walks around Mayfly, looking left and right.

惠姑：有话你就说，别这样，看得我心里毛毛的……
Mayfly: What? What is it? You're giving me the withers.

鹭鸶剪：……你按照任仙子的法子练了也有几日了，身体怎么样？没出什么事吧？
Paper Heron: You've followed Rén's teachings for a few days now, hm? How do you feel?

惠姑：鹭鸶剪，你都问了我好几日，好几遍啦。
Mayfly: Heron, you've asked me this a few times already.

惠姑：不仅昨日无事，今日也无事！最近更是觉得神清气爽，上山下河的，连身体都轻松了许多。
Mayfly: I'm well, just as I was yesterday and the day before that. My strength's improving. I feel light and full of energy, even after a long day in the mountains.

鹭鸶剪背着手，又围着惠姑转了两圈，随后轻轻点了点头。
Paper Heron puts her hands behind her back and circles Mayfly two more times, nodding each time.

鹭鸶剪：这种效果倒是好的……你确定近日身子没有任何异样？
Paper Heron: That's good. That's good then. Are you certain everything's fine? Nothing feels strange at all?

惠姑：当然！
Mayfly: Absolutely!

惠姑仿若做保证般拍了拍胸脯，向鹭鸶剪展示自己的身体无碍。
Mayfly pats her chest as if to prove her health.

惠姑：怎么，你好像巴不得我出点什么岔子。
Mayfly: Why do you keep asking? Is something troubling you?

鹭鸶剪：无事自然是最好，只是……我问你，任仙子的功法，你练着觉得有奇怪之处吗？
Paper Heron: Nothing makes me happier than seeing you well. But may I ask have you felt anything out of place while practicing Rén's methods?

惠姑：奇怪？哪里奇怪？你看，我已经学到第二阶段了，“存元”。
Mayfly: Out of place? I don't know. But I've moved on to the second stage, "concentration and visualization."

惠姑摆了个打坐的样子，手掐了个诀。
She sits in a meditation pose and makes a hand gesture to cast an incantation.

惠姑：任仙子讲，“存元”便是在高度入静之时，将意念集中于神内或身外的神灵，念念不忘，以至长生不死。
Mayfly: Master Rén said that to meditate, I must sit in silence, concentrating my mind on an object and visualizing the inner deities until I find their presence. With consistent practice, the path to longevity will reveal itself.

惠姑：而祝县那棵梅花树乃千年神树，冥冥有灵，是十分不错的寄情对象。
Mayfly: That Mei tree nearby really is an ideal object to focus on. It seems to have been there for over a thousand years. Maybe it really does have a connection to the spiritual world.

鹭鸶剪：任仙子是这么教你们的？
Paper Heron: Are those her words?

惠姑：对啊，我现在是日思夜想，有时做梦还能梦到那棵梅花树呢。
Mayfly: Her exact words! I meditate about that tree day and night. I even see it in my dreams sometimes.

惠姑：仙子真是好人，我听小妖们说，仙子还会用长生剑帮它们修炼，说是……
Mayfly: And Master Rén has been most generous. She even helps the other students using the power of her sword. How did she explain it?

惠姑：嗯——说是会用长生剑帮它们疏通“气穴”，这样能修炼得更快一些。
Mayfly: Something like using the sword to clear the blockage in their body, freeing the flow of Qi, so they can advance more quickly with their training.

惠姑：当初我可吓死了，以为要用剑在身上捅几个窟窿，但实际上，仙子只是在我头顶轻轻一扫……就像当初你给我“授长生”时那样。
Mayfly: The first time I saw it, I almost thought she was about to poke a few holes in me. But instead, she just swiped it above my head, just like you did at the parade.

惠姑：而且啊……我还让山药精偷偷教我第三阶段的功法，我学得可好了！
Mayfly: I even asked Brother Yam to teach me something from the third stage. You should see how well I can do it already.

惠姑：第一式，拂肺式……面北而立，两足分开同肩宽……
Mayfly: Posture one, "Breeze in the Lungs." Face north, feet spread as wide as the shoulders.

惠姑一边念诀，一边在鹭鸶剪面前展示起她新学的长生之法。
She chants the words and shows Paper Heron what she has learned.

惠姑：任仙子讲，我们需得在这个阶段磨炼筋骨，使肉体适应“气”的变化，才能“脱胎换骨”，达到真正的长生。
Mayfly: Master Rén told us that we must cultivate our body to align with the movement of Qi. Only then can our mortal flesh be prepared for longevity.

惠姑：第三阶段啊，练它两个月就差不多了。
Mayfly: She said the cultivation would take about two months.

鹭鸶剪：两个月……这也是任仙子说的？
Paper Heron: Two months? Those were her words?

惠姑：对啊。
Mayfly: That's right.

听完惠姑所说，鹭鸶剪脸色似有动容，一股难以察觉的严肃之色凝聚在她的眉间，仿佛若有所思。
Hearing Mayfly's words, Paper Heron's face changes. A hint of sternness cuts across her brow.

小蝶虫：呵……呵……
Butterfly: *panting*

小蝶虫气喘吁吁地跑进屋内，手舞足蹈地，像是有什么话急着跟大家说。
Butterfly bursts in, panting and waving his hands.

小蝶虫：太好啦！那个姓程的巡检遭报应啦！！！
Butterfly: Wonderful news! Karma finally came for that heartless Chief Constable Chéng!

鹭鸶剪：姓程的巡检……？
Paper Heron: Chéng?

闻言，其他的精怪也都凑了过来。
Hearing this, the other Yao gather around.

刺猬精：就是那个守在城门……天天试图抓我们的家伙？
Hedgehog: You mean that grumpy, self-righteous constable that's been hunting us night and day?

山药精：我有亲戚落在他手里，听说他审讯的手段残酷至极，会把精怪的毛发一根一根地拔下来……
Yam: I heard that he's been interrogating Yao, plucking his captive's hairs one by one.

小蝶虫：呼……就是他，这家伙真是坏透了！
Butterfly: Yes, that's him. What a pig! No offense to pigs!

小蝶虫：听说他家本是盗匪，杀敌有功入了军籍，不料贼就是贼，过了三代，就原形毕露了！
Butterfly: I guess brutality must run in his blood. His family used to be bandits until they worked their way into the military. Not that they lasted long as soldiers. His own father turned out to be a crook!

小蝶虫：他急着和他爹划清界限，立功晋升，就拿我们当垫脚石，无所不用其极。真不是什么好东西！
Butterfly: He cut ties with his father to keep his post. But I don't believe it. If he's willing to throw us all behind bars just to make himself look good, then he's just as bad as the rest of them!

山药精：真可恨呐……你说他遭到报应是怎么回事？快快细说！
Yam: I'll bet he's rotten to the core. But what do you mean by "karma came for him"? Ah, tell us what happened.

小蝶虫等的就是这句话。他眉飞色舞，将程和光家中走水一事说得绘声绘色。
Butterfly seizes the moment with excitement as he proceeds to describe the fire at the chief constable's home.

惠姑：鹭鸶剪，这个巡检是不是和我们打过交道的那个……
Mayfly: Isn't that the man we met at the gate?

鹭鸶剪：……嗯。
Paper Heron: I believe so.

鹭鸶剪未置一词，只是听着众妖喧哗。
Her response is quick and muted, intending not to interrupt the clamor of the Yao.

惠姑：不过……我们就只是想多活几天而已，也没做什么坏事，他们为什么一定要这么为难我们呢……
Mayfly: I just don't understand why he hates us so much. We haven't hurt anyone. We just want to spread the Method of Longevity.

刺猬精：倒也不稀罕……本来就活得长的人怎么舍得让我们学长生之法呢……
Hedgehog: Hardly a surprise. Those with long lives seldom care for the short-lived.

场面突然冷了下来，众妖你看看我，我看看你。
The words bring a harsh chill to the air as the other Yao look at each other and then to Paper Heron.

山药精：你说什么呢，师祖还在这里呢……
Yam: Hedgehog! The grandmaster is still here.

鹭鸶剪：无妨，你们爱说什么就说什么。
Paper Heron: Please, speak your mind. It is every creature's right.

场面一时冷寂，直到小蝶虫忽地想起了什么，崇拜般地开口。
Her words do little to break the sudden chill until Butterfly steers things back on topic.

小蝶虫：——对了，这姓程的还冲撞过师祖！
Butterfly: Oh! I nearly forgot that awful chief had nearly locked up our grandmaster!

小蝶虫：师祖，该不会是您偷偷出手的吧？
Butterfly: Grandmaster, did you start the fire to avenge us?

鹭鸶剪：哈哈……那倒不是，但若有必要，也可以说是我做的。
Paper Heron: Haha. No, I didn't. Though if anyone questions you on the matter, you may give them my name.

小蝶虫：师祖……
Butterfly: Grandmaster ...

众妖听闻，都纷纷崇拜地望向鹭鸶剪。
Hearing this, all the Yao look at Paper Heron with awe.

小蝶虫：有师祖这般的真仙人给我们撑腰，能加入梅花教，真是三生有幸啊！
Butterfly: It is a great honor to study under an avenging hero like you.

小蝶虫：师祖受小的一拜！！！
Butterfly: Please accept our humblest gratitude.

山药精：师祖受小的一拜！！！
Yam: Please accept our humblest gratitude.

鹭鸶剪：这……
Paper Heron: Aha ...

鹭鸶剪哭笑不得，但场面早已不受控制。
Their undeserved praise lands somewhere between funny and vexing, yet she can't help but realize the situation is growing beyond her control.

山药精：师祖如此关爱弟子！咱们更得勤加修炼，早日修得长生，将教门发扬光大！
Yam: The grandmaster has taken our interests to heart, and we must repay her with our greatest effort. We must achieve longevity and spread the school's name.

众妖：早日修得长生！将教门发扬光大！
All Yao: Achieve longevity! Spread the school's name!

众妖在厢房内喧哗，惠姑一时之间觉得头晕脑胀，眼前似有无数小黑虫在翻飞。
The room has become a hubbub of cheers and excitement. But Mayfly does not seem to be participating. She stares up blankly, spots dancing in her vision like fireflies at dusk.

惠姑：呃，等等……我，怎么……
Mayfly: Huh, I ... What's going on?

山药精：惠姑？你怎么了？
Yam: Mayfly? Are you alright?

须臾之间，惠姑突然感到天旋地转。
In a moment, Mayfly feels the world spin beneath her feet.

倒下

鹭鸶剪：……！
Paper Heron: ...!

在天旋地转的世界里，惠姑看到鹭鸶剪的身影正朝自己倾斜而来，随后便是一片黑暗。
As she tumbles, she sees Paper Heron glide toward her. Then all goes dark.

第二日的太阳照常升起，衙门的巡捕们却有了新谈资。
The next day's sun rises as usual, but the Yamen's constables have a new topic to discuss.

巡捕Ⅰ：喂，听说了没。昨天咱们放走的那些大官，今天好像都发病了？
Constable I: Did you hear? Those gentlemen we met yesterday have all fallen ill.

巡捕Ⅰ：听说他们突发热疾，有的忽然在家中昏倒，还有的穿里衣跑到大街上乱叫，引来不少人。
Constable I: It seems they've all been taken by a strange fever. Some fainted in an instant, while others went running and yelling on the streets in their undergarments. It was chaos.

巡捕Ⅰ：看来程巡检还是没抓错人，那长生功法还是练不得。
Constable I: The chief was right. Whatever they were doing must have been dangerous.

巡捕Ⅱ：但我听说他们请了个方士，喝喝符水就好了。
Constable II: But I heard they hired a Daoist who cured them with nothing but water and a pinch of talisman ashes.

巡捕Ⅰ：呔，他们倒是好得轻松，巡检的房子都被那些贼人烧光了！
Constable I: Hmph. Well, that was easy. Shame the chief wasn't so lucky. To think a man could lose his home simply for doing his duty!

巡捕Ⅱ：现在还不清楚失火原委吧？
Constable II: Well, we don't know what caused the fire, do we?

巡捕Ⅰ：除了那些妖贼还能有谁？巡检那天的行为你也看到了。说不准就是查到了点儿什么，才会被杀人灭口。
Constable I: What else could it be? You were there. I think the chief found something important, and now they're desperate to get rid of him.

巡捕Ⅱ：好险好险，幸好我昨天没有跟着冲进去……
Constable II: I'm just glad I was on guard duty.

一个影子挡在了二人面前，二人瞬间噤了声，但程和光没有停留，而是径直走入衙门大堂。
A shadow passes before the two men. They're struck silent with fear. But Chéng Héguāng does not even seem to notice them as he walks straight into the Yamen hall.

大堂

高堂之上，厉晦锋正望着衙上挂着的牌匾。
From his high seat, Lì Huìfēng looks at a plaque on the wall.

厉晦锋：和光，你家昨夜走水了？
