Li Huifeng: Héguāng, I understand it was your house that caught fire last night.

程和光：是。
Cheng Heguang: It was.

厉晦锋：人没事就好。
Li Huifeng: It's a great relief to see you unharmed.

厉晦锋：出了这么大的事，我准你几日假，你回家收拾收拾，也歇息一下。
Li Huifeng: But I'm sorry for your loss. Take a few days. Find another place to stay and get some rest, will you?

程和光：我正要和守备禀报此事。
Cheng Heguang: Much appreciated, Commander. That is precisely why I came.

程和光作了一揖，随后便像连珠炮一样倒出了陈辞。
Chéng Héguāng bows and then pours out his prepared words. It's clear immediately that he's had little rest.

程和光：当时我正在家中读案卷，被野猫叫声惊扰，及时注意到贼人身影，方才幸免于难。只是我寡不敌众，只能眼睁睁看着房屋被烧毁。
Cheng Heguang: I was up late reviewing some case files. As it happened, the arsonists startled a cat as they approached. I was able to spy them from my window. Though I couldn't stop them in time.

程和光：它们皆为精怪所化，所作所为，无非是为打击报复。
Cheng Heguang: They were all Yao. I'm quite certain of it, as retaliation for the arrests I've made.

程和光：我尚有能力自保，但县民呢？梅花教今日敢在城内纵火，刺杀官员。明日便敢在城内抢夺财物，攻击百姓。
Cheng Heguang: Commander Lì, if I, a trained officer, couldn't protect my home from their schemes, what hope do the ordinary townspeople have?

程和光：我必须彻查此案，把他们绳之以法！谁庇护他们谁就是同党！
Cheng Heguang: Please, permit me to bring them to justice and anyone else who shields them!

厉晦锋：你——
Li Huifeng: You—

程和光：请守备放心，我理解县里到处都需要人手。没有明确线索之前我会自己查，不会调动部署。
Cheng Heguang: I know the Yamen is short-staffed. I won't ask for anyone's help until I have solid evidence.

程和光：属下告辞！
Cheng Heguang: Now, I must take my leave. Good day, Commander!

未等到厉晦锋再开口，程和光已经转身离去。
He does not wait for Lì Huìfēng to say more and turns to leave.

脊兽下的檐铃被寒风催动，晃出一声悠长的脆响。
High above them, the Yamen's bell is stirred by the wind, ringing out a long, clear note.

SU-15 公无渡河 / Into the Fire

早饭刚过，惠姑的床前便围着几名精怪。
After breakfast, several Yao gather around Mayfly's bed.

山药精：惠姑，你睡了一天啦。
Yam: Mayfly, you were out for the whole day!

刺猬精：惠姑，听阿山说你晕倒了，我带了些甜糕来看看你，等你醒了便能吃上了……
Hedgehog: Brother Yam told me you were unwell, so I brought some sweet cakes. I thought you might like something to eat after your fall.

惠姑：嗯……
Mayfly: Hmm. Thank you.

惠姑还不太清醒，有些疲惫地应着声。
Still half-asleep, Mayfly responds in a weak voice.

鹭鸶剪：惠姑，我又来了！
Paper Heron: Mayfly, it's me again.

快速脚步声

鹭鸶剪：我给你带了点补气的黄芪、党参……放心，都是未成精的草木，不是精怪。
Paper Heron: I've brought herbs to replenish your Qi. Don't worry. I checked. All cut from plants. No Yao were harmed.

山药精：师祖好！
Yam: Greetings, Grandmaster!

看到鹭鸶剪，精怪们纷纷热切地向她问好。鹭鸶剪一一点头回礼，随后轻轻地将一堆药材放在桌上。
The Yao greet her enthusiastically. She nods to each of them in turn, then sets a bundle of herbs on the table.

鹭鸶剪：大家不必多礼，自在些便好……只是我有些话要和惠姑说，你们可以行个方便吗？
Paper Heron: Ah, no need for those formalities, please. Would you give Mayfly and me a moment in private?

山药精：那是自然！我们这就离开！
Yam: Of course. We'll leave you two alone.

山药精：愣着干什么，师祖都发话了，快走啊！
Yam: Don't you hear the grandmaster? Come on, let's go.

众精怪你推着我，我推着你。不出一会儿，厢房里便只剩下了鹭鸶剪和惠姑两人。
The Yao nudge each other out of the room. Before long, only Paper Heron and Mayfly remain.

惠姑：鹭鸶剪……？
Mayfly: Paper Heron?

惠姑也意识到了今日的异样之处。她扭过头去，看见鹭鸶剪的表情是未曾见过的凝重。
She senses something unusual about the moment and turns her head to find Paper Heron wearing a dour expression.

鹭鸶剪：惠姑。我来这里就是想告诉你，别再练任仙子的功法了。
Paper Heron: Mayfly, you must stop practicing Rén's method.

惠姑：……为什么？
Mayfly: Why?

鹭鸶剪：你没有感觉吗？除了会昏厥外，你时而会心火亢盛，气冲如奔豚，时而会头晕目眩，脚底如软泥。
Paper Heron: Your Qi is too unstable. At times, it surges like a boar, and at others, it falters. Haven't you noticed?

惠姑：我……
Mayfly: I ...

鹭鸶剪：都有，对吧？你之所以会晕倒，是因为你身上的“气”出现了亏空。
Paper Heron: You know I'm right, don't you? Your fall before was a warning. Your Qi is in decline.

惠姑：可……我确实也觉得近日身体轻快了不少，就连头脑也清晰了许多……
Mayfly: But I've felt so much more energetic lately. Even my mind feels clearer than before.

鹭鸶剪：因为“调气”本就是休养生息之法，只是“调气”的话自然会强身健体。
Paper Heron: Yes. You have learned a great deal about how to control your Qi. You'd be in great shape, if that were all you were practicing.

鹭鸶剪：但“存元”需要你将体内的“气”与天道调和，若是你的身体不够强健，如何承载与天道相近的“气”？
Paper Heron: For you to advance further, your Qi must align with the Way, and your body must be strong enough to carry it.

鹭鸶剪：因此你“存元”越深，对身体的负担就会越大，长此以往，自会亏空。
Paper Heron: But if you're too weak, your Qi can become too great a burden. It could consume you.

鹭鸶剪：而我们白马派的功法，注重的是磨炼身体，以身载“气”，因此会在“易筋”这一步耗费很长时间。
Paper Heron: In the White Horse School, we always ensured our physique was strong enough to handle each step along the path.

鹭鸶剪：任仙子跳过了这最难的一步，加上“长生剑”的加持，这才使得你们这些本来没时间练功的小妖怪也有可能练成长生之法。
Paper Heron: But Rén is moving too fast, pushing you forward with the power of the Longevity Sword. It's possible you may still succeed in the end, but ...

鹭鸶剪：……但这极其微弱的可能性，是以你的全部为代价，无论是你的肉身，还是你原本的“气”。
Paper Heron: You're risking both body and spirit for a tiny possibility.

鹭鸶剪：再练下去，你怕是会直接形体坏灭……暂且别练了，先好生休养。
Paper Heron: You could end up with nothing. Your body destroyed, your spirit extinguished. You need to stop and allow your body to recover.

惠姑：休养……？养几日？三天？三周？三个月？
Mayfly: For how long? Days? Weeks? Months?

鹭鸶剪：以你现在的身体状况……休养两个月再继续修炼为佳。
Paper Heron: Given your condition, I'd say two months before you resume any training.

惠姑：……两个月？
Mayfly: Two months?

惠姑：你知道我的寿命还剩多久吗？冬天就要到了，我等不了那么久。
Mayfly: Do you realize how little time I have? Winter's coming. I can't wait that long.

鹭鸶剪：……我知道。
Paper Heron: I know.

鹭鸶剪：但你再修下去，恐怕连两个月都撑不到。
Paper Heron: But if you continue in this fashion, I fear you may not live to see the winter.

鹭鸶剪：我不能眼睁睁看着你落到这般地步，也不想看到其他小妖如此……这并非天道。
Paper Heron: I can't stand by and watch you destroy yourself. Not just you. All the Yao. This isn't the right path for any of you.

惠姑：鹭鸶剪……
Mayfly: Heron ...

惠姑：我想知道，两个月……不，一年在你心里，是不是眨眨眼就过去了？
Mayfly: I know, to you, two months may seem like nothing. I suppose it may seem like years pass by you in the blink of an eye, don't they?

鹭鸶剪：……
Paper Heron: ...

鹭鸶剪看着这个半倚在床上的姑娘，嘴唇微微翕动，半晌后才吐出一句话。
Paper Heron gazes at the girl propped halfway up in bed. Her lips tremble faintly before she finally speaks.

鹭鸶剪：不是这样的，时间……它不慢，但也绝不是这样快的。
Paper Heron: It's not quite as fleeting as a blink of an eye.

惠姑：……鹭鸶剪，假如给你一年时间，你会去做哪些事？
Mayfly: What would you do over the course of a year?

鹭鸶剪：我——
Paper Heron: I—

惠姑：……像你这样的仙人，一定会慢悠悠地骑着你的骡子，去登那白云浮绕的山，踏进桃花飘落的小溪。
Mayfly: Wander the roads on your mule, through cloud-covered mountains, across gentle streams, beneath fragrant blooming peach trees.

惠姑：到了年尾，你便来涣州庙会，感受吐火人表演时拂过脸上的灼热，尝尝甜滋滋的桂花糯米糕。
Mayfly: And when the year ends, you'd go to Huanzhou for the temple fair, feeling the warmth of the flames dancing against your face, savoring the floral sweetness of sticky rice cakes.

惠姑：看完庙会，你还能计划来年去更新鲜、更远的地方，比如翻山越岭去看那长白雪，摸摸毛茸茸的驼鹿，品尝那温热辛辣的曲酒……
Mayfly: Next year you'll travel further still, to see snow-covered plains, brush the fur of a moose, taste wine so strong that it burns your throat.

惠姑：你不需要考虑路程远近，不需要担忧在这世间看不尽，玩不够……
Mayfly: You never worry about the days you spend on the road or whether you have enough time to experience all the world has to offer.

最后一句语毕时，鹭鸶剪听见床上女孩压抑的一声哭腔。
The words hang bitterly on her lips, soon accompanied by wet tears flowing down her face.

惠姑：……而我，连一个完整的春夏秋冬都活不完啊……
Mayfly: But I won't live a full cycle of seasons.

一滴，两滴，三滴……惠姑身上的被褥被打湿，眼泪从女孩的脸庞不受控制地滴落。
One drop, two drops, three drops. The bedding covering her grows damp with a steady flow of tears.

在这寂静的哭泣中，鹭鸶剪默默地站着，望着，直至那抽泣声渐渐止息。
Paper Heron can do nothing to stem their flow. So, she simply waits, watching her friend in tender silence.

惠姑：……所以，在你眼里，时间是最不重要的东西。
Mayfly: To you, a day, a month, a year, it means nothing.

惠姑：但我不是，我一生不过一稔。
Mayfly: But for Yao like me, a year is a lifetime—our only lifetime.

惠姑：我只想活下去，比别人多活一点，多看一点，多闻一点……一刻都等不得！
Mayfly: I want to live, even just a little longer, to see more, feel more. I can't allow myself to waste even a moment.

惠姑：你随手在石头上的刻痕能残留一万年……而我只剩这两个月。你为什么要来阻止我呢？
Mayfly: In a thousand years, my name could still be carved on that stone. But I won't live to know if it's there next spring. So, why must you stop me?

鹭鸶剪：……
Paper Heron: ...

鹭鸶剪沉默了，久久不再开口。
There are barbs on the question, too sharp to swallow, too true to ignore. She chews on it a long while, hoping to reach an answer.

鹭鸶剪：给你在石头上刻字的时候，我并没有想那么多……
Paper Heron: I didn't intend to hurt your feelings when I carved that stone.

鹭鸶剪：那么，你想和石头一样长久吗？
Paper Heron: Is it your wish then? To live as long as the stones?

惠姑：……像石头一样？
Mayfly: What? What do you mean?

鹭鸶剪笑着点了点头，那笑容中却有着一丝悲哀。
Paper Heron smiles, but a trace of sorrow lingers at the corners of her mouth.

鹭鸶剪：还有一种长生之法，这是白马派的秘密，也是在金丹术和任仙子的法门外的第三种长生。
Paper Heron: Besides Inner Alchemy and Rén's method, there is a third way to escape the flow of time, one that has been kept a secret.

鹭鸶剪：它不要求修炼者投入经年累月的时间，也不需要亏空先天俱来的气，只需失去一个门派，一把宝剑，在树中冰封近百年。
Paper Heron: It doesn't take hundreds of years of training, nor does it endanger your Qi. All it costs is your school, a sword, and a hundred years sealed in a tree.

鹭鸶剪：时过境迁，故人与敌人都逝去了。而那求得长生的人孑然独活，食不知味，无悲无喜。
Paper Heron: When the seal breaks, all you once knew will be gone—friends and enemies alike. You will no longer laugh nor hate, and your senses will dull.

鹭鸶剪：虽然走遍了东坊西头，但再也吃不出桂花糯米糕和椒盐麻饼的区别。
Paper Heron: Sweet or sour, salt or spice, it will all taste the same.

鹭鸶剪：明明那杂耍的火焰让众人欢呼，但却感受不到那火应有的热度，亦不知众人欢呼的原因。
Paper Heron: People will cheer at the blazing fire flowers, yet to you, the flames will be as mild as a passing breeze, their excitement like a language you no longer understand.

鹭鸶剪：摸不到云雾的凉爽，亦触不到流水的清冽，冷热软硬，一概消失，仿佛一具活尸……
Paper Heron: Your memories will stay. You'll always recall how the morning mist felt on your face, the crispness of spring water as it flowed through your fingers, but you will never feel them again.

鹭鸶剪：这就是那块石头的故事。现在，你还欣羡它么？
Paper Heron: You will become like a stone. Is that what you want?

惠姑：你……原来是这样的吗？
Mayfly: Is that how the world feels to you?

鹭鸶剪：……
Paper Heron: ...

一向潇洒的道人停了停，不再继续叙说。
She doesn't reply.

惠姑垂下头去，手指因心绪繁杂而交叉了起来。
Mayfly lowers her head, her fingers twisting together as if trying to hold the weight of her tangled thoughts.

一阵思索后，惠姑从口袋里拿出了一个物件。
After a moment's consideration, she takes something from her pocket.

那是当时她踩碎后，又被鹭鸶剪修好的那个草结护符。
It's the amulet she once trampled, now repaired.

惠姑：……鹭鸶剪，其实……当时你已经给我答案了。
Mayfly: But Heron, you've already shown me a way.

惠姑：这个护符，也是我花了全部身家买来的，只是为求通过城门的检查，有机会接触到长生而已……
Mayfly: This amulet—I spent every coin I had on it, just for a chance to get through the city gate.

惠姑：我恨自己被骗，甚至一度厌恶这护符……但你修好了它，告诉我它能用，我能够拿着它去看更多地方。
Mayfly: It didn't work like I'd hoped, and I felt so foolish for believing in it. But you repaired it, even improved it, so that I could make it through.

惠姑：即使我们弱小无力，但也有追求这世间善好的权利……这是你教我的，不是吗？
Mayfly: I may be just a wind-tossed reed, but that doesn't mean I'm unworthy of the wonders of this world. Isn't that what you wanted to tell me?

惠姑：所以……我依然欣羡这块石头。我依然想尽一切办法求得长生。
Mayfly: I'm willing to take the chance to lose everything or gain the world.

惠姑：鹭鸶剪，你讲过，每个人有自己的命内机缘。
Mayfly: You once said that fate presents an opportunity to every one of us.

惠姑：你有属于石头的机缘，而属于我的机缘，就是现在了。
Mayfly: You've had yours, and I need to take mine.

鹭鸶剪：……所以，你会继续追随任仙子？
Paper Heron: You mean that you want to follow Rén's method no matter the danger?

惠姑：……是的。
Mayfly: Yes.

惠姑：咳咳、咳……你们给了我们一条道路，一条跳出既定命数的路……
Mayfly: *cough* She-She has shown us a way to live beyond our years.

惠姑：那我，我要自己去试，去体会，这才是我要的生！
Mayfly: Even if it's dangerous, I want to take the chance to truly live.

鹭鸶剪：……
Paper Heron: ...

鹭鸶剪：……好。
Paper Heron: I understand.

鹭鸶剪不再反驳，她站起身来，拍了拍桌上的药材。
She knows it won't be useful to argue her point any longer. She rises to her feet and taps the herbs on the table.

鹭鸶剪：这药，你记得吃。
Paper Heron: Just remember to drink my herbal brew, eh?

门板虚掩，精怪们正好奇地向门内张望。鹭鸶剪不再理会它们。
The door stands ajar. Other Yao peer inside with curiosity. Paper Heron walks past them without a word.

在大片洒落的眩目晨光中，她径直向庭院走去。
In the dazzling morning light, she walks straight toward the courtyard.

SU-16 登天阶 / To Heaven!

晨光照得梅花花瓣半透，梅花之下，小精怪们正列队练功。
Morning light renders the Mei petals nearly translucent under the sun. Beneath the Mei tree, young Yao practice in formation.

鹭鸶剪：任仙子呢？
Paper Heron: Where is your master?

梅花教信徒Ⅰ：秉师祖，仙子她有事出去了。
School of Mei Believer I: Grandmaster Heron, I believe she left to attend to some personal matters.

鹭鸶剪：任仙子自创了一门功法，非我白马派的传承，我可不是你们师祖，以后叫我道人就行。
Paper Heron: Erm, I think it best you no longer call me that. Your master has taken a path away from my teachings. I am now nothing more than an ordinary Daoist to you.

梅花教信徒Ⅰ：啊……是！
School of Mei Believer I: Oh, I see.

小妖们惶恐地对视一眼，但瞧见鹭鸶剪笑意盈盈的表情，又按下了心中的疑问。
They exchange worried glances, but seeing the pain beneath her smile, they choose not to trouble her.

鹭鸶剪：我有话要在这里和你们师父说，能行个方便不？
Paper Heron: When she returns, please tell her that I want to have a word with her here. Is there a place we could speak?

梅花教信徒Ⅰ：是……师……不，道人！
School of Mei Believer I: Certainly, Grand, uh, I mean, Master Heron.

白云掠日，树影东斜。
White clouds drift past the sun, casting shadows eastward.

约莫半天，任仙子终于回到了教门。梅花树前，只有鹭鸶剪一人独立。
After roughly half a day, Master Rén returns to the school. Before the Mei tree, Paper Heron stands alone.

任仙子：鹭鸶剪，听说你找我？
Master Ren: You wish to speak with me?

鹭鸶剪：是啊，我今日得了闲趣，想在这梅花树前和你叙叙旧。
Paper Heron: I do. The day's been quiet, and I've found myself reminiscing on the old days. Would you join me for a chat beneath the Mei tree?

鹭鸶剪笑着指了一下院中的梅树。
She smiles as she gestures toward the tree in the courtyard.

任仙子：这棵树？
Master Ren: This tree?

任仙子瞧了一眼那棵再普通不过的红梅，瘦弱细小，不免引得她哂然一笑。
Master Rén glances at the red Mei tree. It's scrawny for its years. Staring up at it, she can't help but laugh coldly.

任仙子：虽都是红梅，但这棵有什么好聊的？假以千年，待它像城外那棵一般枝繁叶茂，还算有些意思。
Master Ren: Why? There isn't much to it. It could take a thousand years before it rivals the largest Mei tree in town.

鹭鸶剪：就聊聊往事。
Paper Heron: Let's just talk about the old days, eh?

鹭鸶剪：洪武年间，揽诸苏醒。白马派镇压揽诸期间遭他人围攻。致使满门皆灭，揽诸亦受重创。
Paper Heron: When the White Horse School attempted to subdue the Beast Lǎnzhū, they were taken by surprise by rival schools. We lost all our most capable masters in the battle.

鹭鸶剪：师祖为保众生，折断一把长生剑，放出剑中储藏先天之炁，将最后一名白马派弟子和揽诸之魄一并封于梅花树中，一去百年。
Paper Heron: Seeing no other way, my grandmaster shattered one of the two Longevity Swords, releasing the Qi within to create a seal. The last student of the school and the beast were frozen in that moment, sealed inside a Mei tree.

任仙子：直到一只画皮小妖渡劫时无意经过，引天雷劈开了梅花树，白马派传人方重新现世。
Master Ren: A hundred years later, a Painted-Skin Yao faced her celestial tribulation under the same tree. Lightning struck both her and the tree, and the seal was broken.

任仙子：而画皮小妖则被天雷击中，或将殒命。白马派弟子感叹因缘，遂传授这只小妖门派术法——后来的事，便不用说了。
Master Ren: The lightning nearly destroyed the Yao. The White Horse student, freed from the seal and surprised by such a turn of fate, saved the dying Yao and taught her the Daoist arts. We both know the story.

鹭鸶剪：是的，你记得很清楚。
Paper Heron: Yes, you remember every detail of it.

任仙子：——从未忘却。
Master Ren: I could never forget.

鹭鸶剪：你拿了长生剑，也学了金丹术。我并不要求你拜入白马派，因为白马派已去。
Paper Heron: I gave you the remaining sword and taught you the way of Inner Alchemy, but I never asked you to take the name of a White Horse student. I knew the school was lost to history.

任仙子：只是镇压险道兽一事，还需有人去做。
Master Ren: The school is gone, yes, but their duty to control the Xiǎndào Beast was unfinished.

任仙子：——鹭鸶剪，你究竟想说什么？
Master Ren: What's the purpose of this, Heron?

鹭鸶剪摇了摇头，看向远处，于此望不到的巨大梅花树。
She shakes her head, gazing out into the distance toward another giant Mei tree far beyond their sight—a sister of the school's own centerpiece.

鹭鸶剪：——任仙子，你究竟想干什么？
Paper Heron: What is your purpose, Rén?

鹭鸶剪：你让所有精怪将“气”存在那棵梅花树上……到底是在谋划什么？
Paper Heron: You told your students to channel their Qi into the Mei tree. Why?

听闻此言，任仙子忽地笑了出来。
Her old student looks at her and simply laughs.

任仙子：你发现了？
Master Ren: So you've found out about that.

鹭鸶剪：你骗不过我。
Paper Heron: I'm not easily fooled.

闻言，任仙子懒洋洋地在梅树前的石桌前坐下，并不在意鹭鸶剪投来的眼光。
Master Rén lets the words roll over her as she settles herself at the stone table beneath the tree's shadow.

任仙子：鹭鸶剪，我知你对我所授功法存有疑虑。但我跳过“易筋”，确是为了弟子们切身考量。
Master Ren: I know you disagree with my methods, but whether you agree or not, this is what is best for the students.

任仙子：教门的精怪们，没有哪个有你当初的资质，也没有寿命允许它们度过练习“易筋”的漫长岁月。
Master Ren: They're not like you. None of them have the talent or lifespan to properly cultivate longevity.

任仙子：相比你的无所作为，我至少给了它们一条能长生的路。
Master Ren: Had you been in my place, you likely wouldn't have taken them on at all. But I want to give them a chance.

任仙子：你不是精怪，又怎知精怪之心？我们别无选择！
Master Ren: After all, what would a talented master like you know of the life of a lowly Yao, of our struggles and desires?

鹭鸶剪：我问的不是“易筋”，任仙子。我问你的是你引导它们将气“存元”于梅树上，意欲何为？
Paper Heron: I do not mean to question your teachings, Rén. I only need to know why you've focused their Qi there, of all places.

任仙子：不要着急，我正要解释。你什么时候是这样着急的性格了？
Master Ren: My, my, when did you become so impatient, Heron?

“铮——”
*ching*

任仙子轻捏手诀，那柄通体莹白的剑便呈在了空中。
Master Rén casts a familiar incantation, and the white sword reappears in the air.

任仙子：当年你将长生剑托付于我，我便设法将它弘扬。我曾是短命精怪，自然想要造福同袍。
Master Ren: You trusted me with the sword, and I have endeavored to honor that trust by sharing it. I was once a short-lived Yao myself. It is only natural that I wish to help my kind.

任仙子：我授予它们的，便是结合了金丹术和长生剑的便捷法门。
Master Ren: Combining Inner Alchemy with the power of the Longevity Sword, I developed a method for our kind to overcome their disadvantages.

任仙子：长生剑可储存气，也可放出气。它能给予，也能收走。全靠这柄法器，才能使短命精怪速成长生之法。
Master Ren: The sword can hold and release Qi. It gives, and it takes. Through it, I work to bring the Yao the lives they deserve.

任仙子：如果它们成功，自然再好不过，世间又多了一个长生之法的传人，我将发自内心欢喜。
Master Ren: Should they succeed, there will be one more Daoist master to carry the Method forward.

任仙子：如果它们暴亡，我也能回收它们的气，投入镇压揽诸的大业之中，两全之事，岂不美哉？
Master Ren: And if they fail, their remaining Qi is gathered within the Mei tree to aid us in subduing the beast when it next awakens. Either way, the outcome is favorable.

任仙子：如此，它们的死也值了。
Master Ren: And either way, their deaths will not be in vain.

消剑

鹭鸶剪：你倒是毫不避讳，可你的徒弟们知道么？
Paper Heron: You lay it out so plainly. Do your students know?

鹭鸶剪：知道师父把自己带在身边，不过是一个丹炉的备用材料？
Paper Heron: Do they know their master sees them as mere fuel for her designs?

任仙子：哈哈！知道又如何？要想修得长生，怎能不付出代价！
Master Ren: Hahaha ... Does it matter? Each one of them knows longevity comes at a price.

任仙子：来到这里的精怪，哪个没有赌命的觉悟？
Master Ren: Do you think any of them would have joined me if they were not willing to risk their lives?

任仙子：和镇压揽诸的大业相比起来，这又算得了什么？！
Master Ren: Does any price we pay matter if it means subduing the beast?

任仙子疯狂地大笑起来，鹭鸶剪轻轻别过了头。
She laughs again, but there's no joy in it. Paper Heron turns her head away.

任仙子：我承诺过你，镇压揽诸将万无一失。这便是那万无一失的后手。
Master Ren: "No matter the cost," I said. I gave you my word. This is but a small portion of the sacrifices I am prepared to make.

鹭鸶剪：你也答应过我，尽可能护着你的弟子。
Paper Heron: You also promised to do your best to care for your students.

任仙子：此话怎讲？揽诸若是镇压失败，我们都会殒命，不如将这命聚在有用的地方。到了那天，我自会亲口告诉它们，让它们自行选择。
Master Ren: If the beast breaks free, every one of them will perish, whether on that fateful day or any other, they have the same choice: aid me, or else die a pointless death.

任仙子：我这么做并非皆是私心，实为你我之愿景。你再三叮嘱我镇压揽诸并非易事，我岂敢怠慢？
Master Ren: I should hope you know me well enough to trust that I do not undertake this selfishly. Do you not see that I am doing only what must be done?

鹭鸶剪：可镇压揽诸并不需要这么多气。
Paper Heron: Keeping Lǎnzhū subdued will not require nearly this much Qi.

鹭鸶剪：用这么多命堆出来的气，你甚至可以……
Paper Heron: With the Qi you've gathered, the lives you've sacrificed ...

鹭鸶剪：——杀死揽诸。
Paper Heron: You could kill the beast.

不知何时，庭院的风已经完全停了。
At some point, the wind in the courtyard had stilled completely.

任仙子抬起头来，戏谑地看向鹭鸶剪。
Master Rén raises her head and fixes Paper Heron with a mocking stare.

任仙子：手持长生剑，可感悟天地万物流转，甚至可影响生命之气的荣枯。
Master Ren: You were given a weapon of magnificent power—the capability to sense the cycle of all things and even manipulate the wax and wane of life itself.

任仙子：白马派多年来却只用它来打通揽诸气穴，不是浪费么？既有此等神器，何苦自甘为一方牧人？
Master Ren: Yet the White Horse School merely used it to clear the blockage of Qi in Lǎnzhū. An all-powerful sword reduced to a tamer's whip.

鹭鸶剪：揽诸不能杀。
Paper Heron: Because Lǎnzhū must not die.

任仙子：真没想到是你这么说，鹭鸶剪。你们白马派为这个早无侲子看管的活天灾全数折损，如今你还要为它说话？
Master Ren: Paper Heron, you of all people, are the last I expected to say such a thing. You lost your school, your friends, your masters, to this beast, and you would have it remain a threat forever?

任仙子：这种祸患不除，要留到什么时候？
Master Ren: What good would come of that?

鹭鸶剪：天行有常。险道兽是大道运行之象征。杀死险道兽，会引发更大的灾难，远非一个涣州陷落所能比拟。你不可能不知道。
Paper Heron: The Xiǎndào Beasts play a necessary part in the workings of Heaven. A far greater danger may come of its death, one that extends far beyond Huanzhou. Have I not taught you as much?

任仙子：那你就让我走你的老路吗？让所有徒子徒孙，都不断地折损于镇压险道兽的循环之中，永无止境？
Master Ren: And why should I follow your teachings, hm? Why should I bind my students, and their students alike, to an endless cycle of subduing the beast?

鹭鸶剪：——！
Paper Heron: ...!

任仙子：我并非人类，也无人类的传承观念。我只活这一世，也要活出这一世。
Master Ren: Humans have a strange attachment to their "legacies." But to be Yao is to be defined by one short life. I intend to make mine echo through the ages.

任仙子：我会花费比你们更小的牺牲，让揽诸在我这里完全断绝。
Master Ren: Lǎnzhū will perish and the cycle will end, and all for a small price.

任仙子：此战过后，再也不会有人为了揽诸而死，白马派的悲剧不会重演。
Master Ren: No more endless duties passed from hand to hand, no more deaths in service of legacy. Our school will never suffer as yours did.

任仙子：而我，也将带领我的徒弟们，吸取揽诸的气，成为真正的仙人！
Master Ren: As for me, I will share the power released from the dead beast with my students, and together, we will ascend to immortality!

鹭鸶剪：……
Paper Heron: ...

鹭鸶剪深呼吸一口气。再次睁开眼睛时，她的声音骤然冷了下来。
She takes a deep breath. As she opens her eyes again, her voice is cold as winter.

鹭鸶剪：你这是在逆天而行。
Paper Heron: This goes against the Way. It isn't natural.

任仙子：什么是天？
Master Ren: What does it mean for a thing to be natural?

任仙子：当年，我本该被雷劫劈死在那棵封住你的梅花树下，是你救了我。
Master Ren: Would it not have been natural for you to let me die under that Mei tree?

任仙子：我还活着站在这里，本就是逆天而行。
Master Ren: But you didn't. My very life is proof that the Way can be defied.

任仙子：这世间从来如此，有多大灾祸，便成就多大机缘！
Master Ren: Perhaps there is risk in diverting the cycles of Heaven. But how much greater are the rewards?

任仙子：所以，我来杀死揽诸，我来承受天道，我来拯救涣州。
Master Ren: If there is risk, I take it gladly. I will slay the beast and free Huanzhou and its people from its threat.

任仙子：我，将升仙。
Master Ren: Then, I will ascend.

鹭鸶剪：你若失败了，涣州的百姓该如何？
Paper Heron: And if you fail? What will happen to the people?

任仙子：我不会失败。
Master Ren: I won't fail.

良久无言，只有梅树的枝条沙沙作响。
Silence follows, broken by the returning wind as it rustles the Mei tree's branches.

任仙子成竹在胸，却只听鹭鸶剪诉出冷冷一句。
Master Rén doesn't betray a hint of doubt, but her former master's reply comes like a sharp cut.

鹭鸶剪：你太自负。
Paper Heron: Your pride has blinded you.

骤然间，术法的光芒已至任仙子眼前。
Suddenly, arcane light flashes before Master Rén's eyes.

攻击

任仙子提笔相抗，却被击退几丈。
She raises her brush in defense but is driven back a dozen steps.

任仙子：哈哈，我与你掏心掏肺，和盘托出，你却出招便下死手！
Master Ren: Hahaha. Are you really the same woman I called Master? All I have done is speak honestly, yet you answer with a lethal strike!

任仙子：究竟是谁太自负，鹭鸶剪！
Master Ren: You lecture me about pride, then dare to take my life?

任仙子：既然你执意要拦我……那便是你找死！
Master Ren: But if you choose to stand in my way, then I must take yours!

刀剑

任仙子：呃！呃！
Master Ren: Heh! Hah!

鹭鸶剪：拿命来！
Paper Heron: Have I trained you so poorly?

鹭鸶剪攻向任仙子死穴，岂料任仙子竟放弃了抵抗，仅以长生剑护在胸口。
Paper Heron strikes at Master Rén's weak point, but her opponent abandons resistance, instead raising the Longevity Sword like a hostage.

鹭鸶剪：什么！
Paper Heron: What?

换图

见势，鹭鸶剪只得半路撤劲，勉强将长生剑捞了回来，但也不免在剑鞘上留下了伤痕，自己也被来不及撤走的术法反伤。
Caught off guard, Paper Heron is forced to withdraw her attack mid-strike. She barely retrieves the Longevity Sword, leaving a scar on the sheath. Yet she cannot escape the backlash of her own arcane skill.

任仙子：哈哈哈哈……
Master Ren: Hahahaha ...

任仙子：鹭鸶剪，你不是要杀我吗，收手做什么？我就知道，你在乎的只有这把剑！
Master Ren: Why do you stay your hand, Heron? Strike me down, if you truly believe it to be just! Or is it that you care more for this sword than any living thing?

任仙子：你的心历来是石头做的。在你眼里，谁的命又能比得过“师门遗命”？我也不过是你用来完成遗命的工具。
Master Ren: You have lost more than your senses, Master. Make whatever claims you like, but I see your empty heart. All that matters to you is your legacy, your mission! And I was only a tool.

任仙子：还打着百姓的旗号……事到如今，何必再假惺惺？
Master Ren: Are you now too blind to see how deep your hypocrisy runs?

鹭鸶剪：住嘴。
Paper Heron: Enough.

瞬黑
打击

任仙子：咳……
Master Ren: *cough*

任仙子紧捂胸口，吐出了一口鲜血。
Master Rén clutches her chest and coughs up blood.

任仙子：鹭鸶剪，我谋划数十年……现只欠东风，怎么会败于你的临时起意？
Master Ren: All the decades I have given in preparation. You cannot stop me now, not when I am this close to success!

任仙子提笔蓄气，额头的青筋也暴起，狰狞着飞身扑将过去。
She raises her brush, gathering energy as veins bulge on her forehead. At last, she lunges at her in a furious charge.

毛笔

鹭鸶剪：不好——
Paper Heron: What?

鹭鸶剪后撤一步，却未能躲开，胸口一阵剧痛。
Paper Heron retreats a step but fails to evade the attack entirely. Sharp pain tears through her chest.

眼见任仙子毫无消停之意，鹭鸶剪只得反手掐出一诀。
Seeing that Master Rén shows no sign of relenting, Paper Heron has no choice but to cast another incantation.

替身术

任仙子：嗯？
Master Ren: Hmm?

烟雾散去，任仙子眼前只留下了一个抱着剑的小纸人。
The smoke clears. Before Master Rén stands only a paper figure clutching a sword.

任仙子：哼……
Master Ren: Hmph.

众妖：师父，要追吗？
All Yao: Master! Should we go after her?

任仙子：追。不管她人如何，长生剑必须完好无损地回来！
Master Ren: Go. Whether dead or alive, she must not escape with the Longevity Sword. Bring it to me intact!

众妖：是！
All Yao: Yes, Master.

众妖随即散去。
The Yao scatter.

任仙子最后看了一眼庭院中的梅树，而后拂袖离去。
She casts one final sneering glance at the scrawny Mei tree in the courtyard, then flicks her sleeves and leaves.

SU-17 东方式诺言 / An Eastern Promise

更夫：天干物燥，小心火烛！
Night Watch: The night is dry. Beware of fires!

更夫的铜锣声渐渐远去，程和光这才从树上跳下，凝神观察起眼前的巷子。
The night watch's gong reverberates into the night. Only then does Chéng Héguāng jump from the tree, studying the alley before him intently.

程和光：那游行的队伍，最后一次出现在这里……嗯？
Cheng Heguang: This is where that strange parade was last seen. Hm?

杨武：站住！三更半夜闲逛什么？
Yang Wu: Hey, you! What are you doing out here at this hour?

杜六：诶，杨武，她就是那个——
Du Liu: Wǔ! It's her.

程和光循声望去，杨武和杜六正堵住了一个受伤的女子盘问，语气颇为不善。
Chéng Héguāng turns toward the source of the sound. Yáng Wǔ and Dù Liù have cornered a wounded woman.

程和光：杨武，杜六，出什么事了？
Cheng Heguang: Yáng Wǔ, Dù Liù, what's going on?

看见程和光，杜六杨武二人极不自然地对视了一下。
Seeing him, the two exchange an awkward glance.

鹭鸶剪：哎……这可真是不是冤家不聚头啊。
Paper Heron: Well now, fate always finds a way to put enemies in your path, eh?

杨武：程巡检？我们在巡逻中碰见了那个梅花教的仙人……
Yang Wu: Chief! We were on patrol duty. We ran into the Daoist. She was the one with the School of Mei.

程和光把目光转向鹭鸶剪，右手自然而然地摸上了刀柄。
Chéng Héguāng narrows his eyes as he spots the woman. His right hand falling instinctively to his blade.

程和光：你怎么在这里？
Cheng Heguang: What are you doing here?

鹭鸶剪：说来话长。
Paper Heron: Long story.

程和光没接话茬，只是看着鹭鸶剪身上的血迹沉思。
He ignores her response, instead, sweeping his eyes over the woman's bloodstained robes.

杜六：小程巡检？
Du Liu: Chief?

程和光：……
Cheng Heguang: ...

程和光：把她交给我吧，之后我会带她回衙门。
Cheng Heguang: Return to your patrol. I will take her to the Yamen later.

杨武：可、程巡检，之前厉守备已经交代过我们……
Yang Wu: But Chief, the commander ordered us to—

杜六轻肘了杨武一下，接过了话头。
Dù Liù gives his partner a prod with his elbow and takes over the conversation.

杜六：这道人与梅花教关系匪浅，现在梅花教行事日益猖狂，甚至还有纵火之举……想必小程巡检是想问点什么吧。
Du Liu: Let's go, Wǔ. I'm sure the chief has his own score to settle with her.

杨武：纵火……
Yang Wu: His own score ... Aah.

杨武仿佛才想起来什么，也不再阻拦杜六。
Yáng Wǔ at last realizes what's going on and nods knowingly.

程和光：……确实有不少事情需要盘问清楚。
Cheng Heguang: Just a few questions. Is that alright?

杜六：小程巡检放心，往日的此刻，我俩正在别街巡逻，今日亦是这样。
Du Liu: Of course. Take your time, Chief. We were never here.

杜六杨武随意抱了抱拳，便匆匆离开了此处。
The two cup their fists in a salute and hurry away.

鹭鸶剪：多谢。没想到我落难关头，遇到的还是你……
Paper Heron: Much appreciated. Seems you and I just can't seem to avoid each other.

鹭鸶剪倚向墙壁，咳嗽两声，吐出一口血沫。
Paper Heron leans against the wall. She coughs, and a small trickle of blood escapes her lips.

鹭鸶剪：有件事关全城百姓生死的事得拜托你。你能稍微听一下么？
Paper Heron: Would you be willing to hear what I have to say? I need a favor. It's about the safety of this city.

教徒们手持火把，聚集在池塘边的广场。
The believers hold torches, gathering in the square beside the pond.

快切

任仙子：我知道大家不愿相信，可仙人的确背叛了我们。
Master Ren: As difficult as it is to believe, we must face the truth: Paper Heron has turned against us.

梅花教信徒Ⅱ：可她不是教授我们长生之法的仙人吗？长生在即，她为什么要这么做？
School of Mei Believer II: But wasn't she your guide to longevity? Why would she turn her back on us after all her efforts?

梅花教信徒Ⅲ：她对我们很好，我们对她也很好啊。她有什么背叛我们的理由？
School of Mei Believer III: She's been kind to us, and we have paid her our respect. How did it come to this?

任仙子：可她毕竟已然长生。
Master Ren: Her long life has hardened her heart to us.

任仙子：她不愿让我们飞升成仙，成就不世之功，以免危及自己仙人的地位！
Master Ren: But when we succeed and join her in longevity, her status and authority will be challenged.

惠姑：什么……
Mayfly: I can't believe this.

任仙子：自从她知道我们的打算，便开始百般阻挠。如今更是夺走了门中的长生剑，彻底做了我们的敌人！
Master Ren: The moment she learned of our goal, she chose to become an obstacle. Now that she has taken the Longevity Sword, her position is clear.

任仙子：大家应该记得，长生所需的“气”，正是由长生剑所传。若无长生剑，长生只是空谈。
Master Ren: Remember, the Qi from that sword is instrumental to our success. Without it, we will not survive.

台下的精怪骚动起来。各不相同的表情出现在教徒们的脸上，或是惊讶，或是悲伤，或是愤怒。
The Yao below the platform grow restless. Emotions flash across their faces—surprise, sorrow, and anger.

刺猬精：果然……当初她送我们那些法器，我还以为她是真心对我们……后来她说那些话时，我便知她只是表面如此……
Hedgehog: I knew it. At first, I thought she cared when she gave us those amulets, but when she challenged Master Rén, I realized it was all a farce.

獾子精：我早就看出那鹭鸶剪只是虚情假意！不然怎么会教授一些根本用不上的大道理呢！
Badger: All that talk about the "right path" and serving the Way, as if we had the time to do any of that!

獾子精：大家为了长生付出了一切，决不能功亏一篑！
Badger: We sacrificed so much for longevity. We can't fail now!

任仙子：少了长生剑，“镇殃大阵”的效力便会降低……我虽有仙丹和功法，但恐怕力有未逮，纵使降服了揽诸，也难护得所有精怪长生。
Master Ren: Without the sword, the Quelling Array will weaken. I can still subdue the beast with elixirs, but it will leave me without the strength to shield you from harm.

任仙子：但如今，大家还来得及夺回这把剑。她刚刚被我打伤，正是虚弱的时候。
Master Ren: But we still have a chance. I wounded her when she wrestled the sword from me. We must take it back before she recovers.

任仙子：你们现在便上街寻找她的踪迹，一旦发现，生死不论，只以夺剑为要！
Master Ren: So I bid you: go forth and find her. Secure the sword at any cost!

任仙子：我知今夜行动凶险异常，这天下还从未有人杀死过揽诸，原地升仙。你们谁现在就想离去的，我不会阻拦。
Master Ren: But before you risk your lives this night, hear these words: The path before us is set. We will slay Lǎnzhū and draw upon its power to ascend. If you do not share our purpose, you may still leave.

台下一下子炸开，热烈的吵嚷逐渐占了上风。
The crowd erupts, heated protests and arguments drowning out all else.

梅花教信徒Ⅳ：我家人都已经过世，只有我因修炼“长生之法”得活。我愿追随仙子长生，誓死夺回长生剑！
School of Mei Believer IV: My family is long gone, and I wouldn't have made it this far without Master Rén's teachings. I will stand with her and bring the sword back!

梅花教信徒Ⅴ：我从辽东而来，若不是仙子传授“长生之法”，上个月便已经死去。我愿夺回长生剑，追随仙子长生。
School of Mei Believer V: I traveled all the way from Liaodong, and I'd have died last month if not for Master Rén's help. I'll do whatever I can to return the sword!

梅花教信徒Ⅳ：今夜八成是死，不如放手一搏！我们愿追随仙子长生！
School of Mei Believer IV: Either we die tonight, or we live forever! I stand with Master Rén!

山药精：……看来，看来只能放手一搏了……
Yam: It seems this is the only path left for us.

小蝶虫：大家……大家这是……
Butterfly: Everyone else agrees.

惠姑和小蝶虫面面相觑，两人茫然地看着周围人陷入狂热，有些无措，但也迟疑地与它们齐声呐喊。
Mayfly and Butterfly exchange a meaningful glance. Lost amid the fervent crowd, they join their growing cries, hesitant and then wholeheartedly.

小蝶虫：我愿追随仙子长生！
Butterfly: Then, I, too, will stand with Master Rén!

惠姑：我……我愿追随仙子长生！
Mayfly: I-I stand with Master Rén!

众精怪：我们愿追随仙子长生！
All Yao: We all stand with Master Rén!

誓言和呼喊声如浪潮一般荡开，彻底打碎了园林的平静。
Oaths and shouts of support spread like waves in a stone-lined pond, pouring back over themselves until the once tranquil courtyard is a cacophony of sound.

任仙子摆了摆手，示意教徒安静片刻。
Then their master raises her hand, signaling the believers to quiet down.

任仙子：任仙子谢过各位！
Master Ren: You have my thanks.

任仙子：但诸位也不必太过惊慌。时辰将至，我已布好阵法，可以尽力一试。
Master Ren: Do not let fear get the better of you. The final hour approaches; the array is ready. I shall do all that is in my power to enact our plan.

任仙子：无论是否拿到法剑，诸位都务必于子时前往梅树之下，与我共待长生！
Master Ren: With or without the sword, meet me under the Mei tree at the first double-hour this night. Together, we will seek our ascension to longevity!

百年的故事，讲起来也不过寥寥几句。
A century-old tale can be told in mere sentences.

程和光有些震惊地看向鹭鸶剪，意识到一些散乱的碎片终于可以串联起来。
Chéng Héguāng looks at her in astonishment, fitting the scattered fragments of his investigation into a clear picture at last.

程和光：你是说，那些动物遗尸，是修炼“长生之法”失败的精怪……
Cheng Heguang: So then, those dead animals were the Yao who failed in their pursuit of the Method.

鹭鸶剪点点头。
Paper Heron nods.

鹭鸶剪：揽诸马上就会苏醒，若任仙子执意升仙，那时不光会乾坤失序，日月同天，整个涣州都会分崩离析，毁于一旦。
Paper Heron: Lǎnzhū will soon awaken. If we don't stop Rén, her actions may throw the balance of life out of order and put all of Huanzhou in danger.

鹭鸶剪：不可再耽搁，必须马上疏散民众……时间不够了。
Paper Heron: We need to evacuate the townsfolk as soon as we can. Time's running out.

鹭鸶剪：但我被任仙子打伤，此刻急需调气，难以行动。
Paper Heron: But I'm wounded. It will be a while before I can move again.

鹭鸶剪：你可愿助我？
Paper Heron: Will you aid me in this?

程和光惊异地张了张口，一时无声。思忖片刻，终是下了决心。
His mouth opens in surprise, but the words don't come. After a moment's deliberation, he makes his decision.

程和光：此事绝非儿戏。全城疏散，需要衙门通力配合。
Cheng Heguang: This is no small favor. It'll take the effort of every soldier and constable in town to evacuate the people in time.

程和光：空口无凭。纵使我信，光凭我一人之力，如何能够助你？
Cheng Heguang: Even if I believe you, my superiors won't be so easily convinced.

鹭鸶剪：……那这样如何？
Paper Heron: Then how about this?

鹭鸶剪微微低头，拿出怀中的长生剑，将一缕气注入其中。
She bows her head and draws the Longevity Sword from within her robes, channeling a thread of Qi into it.

白莹的剑身冒出幽幽寒光，一时间好似活物。
The white blade emanates a cold bright light. It seems almost alive for a moment.

鹭鸶剪：当年真人魂游世间，得大道所赐白马尾，炼为两柄白玉剑。
Paper Heron: Long ago, when His Eminence walked the land, two white horse tails were bestowed upon him as a reward for his service to the Way. Those tails were forged into a pair of jade swords.

鹭鸶剪：这是世间罕有的上古法器，也是白马派的师门遗物，梅花教的长生宝剑，我平生最重要之物。
Paper Heron: I carry only one of them. A rare Daoist implement passed down to me by my master, from his master before him. It means more to me than my life.

鹭鸶剪：我以此物起誓，我所说绝无一字虚言。
Paper Heron: I swear on it. I have told you nothing but the truth.

鹭鸶剪：你将此物示与他人，兴许……
Paper Heron: Were you to present this sword to your people, might they ...?

程和光：……足够了。
Cheng Heguang: It'll do.

程和光目光如炬地看着剑鞘上的梅花和八卦图样。
He fixes his sharp gaze over the Mei pattern and the Bagua array.

程和光：涣州高层中，不少官员机要都与梅花教有所来往。
Cheng Heguang: The high lords of this town have close ties with the School of Mei.

程和光：他们定识得此剑。
Cheng Heguang: They will recognize this sword.

鹭鸶剪：……那，此剑便托付于你了。
Paper Heron: Then take it. Look after it well.

鹭鸶剪收剑入鞘，小心翼翼地将长生剑放到程和光手中。
She sheathes the sword and offers it to him.

程和光双手接过，感受到了剑身厚重的分量。
He receives it with both hands, feeling the blade's weight.

程和光：它对你如此重要……你……就这样把它给我？
Cheng Heguang: You-You're leaving the sword to me, just like that?

鹭鸶剪垂下眼，虚弱地笑了一下。
She lowers her eyes, managing a weak smile.

鹭鸶剪：的确，它曾是我最看重的东西。我把它看得如此之重，以至于有时候忘记了，它也只是一把剑而已。
Paper Heron: This sword means more to me than my life, yes. But I once valued it so greatly that I lost sight of what is truly important. In the end, it's only a sword.

鹭鸶剪：若它不能护人，还算什么剑？
Paper Heron: And what purpose does a sword have if it is not used to protect?

特写

程和光：……好！
Cheng Heguang: Well said!

程和光：我答应你，我程和光，定会尽我所能，护好这把剑。
Cheng Heguang: You have my word. I will protect it with my life.

程和光：报信之后，定将它分毫无损地交还到你手上，如有差池，提头来见！
Cheng Heguang: Should anything go wrong, I will bring my head to you.

夜色深沉，鹭鸶剪看不清少年的面容，但听他决然的语气，脑中也能想出几分。
In the deep darkness of the night, Paper Heron cannot see the young man's face, but his resolute tone paints a picture the light could not.

她笑笑，宽慰似的拍了拍程和光的肩。
She lifts herself just enough to reach his shoulder.

鹭鸶剪：别头不头的，年轻人。我有望气之法，就算这剑丢到天涯海角，我也找得回。
Paper Heron: Now, what would I do with a young man's head, eh? Worry not. I'm a Qi reader. I can trace the sword wherever it goes.

鹭鸶剪：你快走吧，任仙子定不会放弃寻剑。我寻一僻静处调气，休养好后自会来找你。
Paper Heron: Now go. Rén won't give up the sword easily, so be careful. I'll find you once I'm back on my feet.

远处传来模糊的嘶鸣与哭喊声，城内已经燃起了隐隐的火光。
Distant screams and wails drift through the air. Across the county, fires burst and flicker against the night sky.

精怪的黑影在墙上一晃而过，鹭鸶剪所言非虚。
Yao shadows slide across the wall. Any doubt that Paper Heron speaks the truth vanishes from him.

程和光：你……
Cheng Heguang: What if ...

鹭鸶剪：——走！
Paper Heron: Just go!

程和光咬咬牙，终究还是拿上了长生剑，跳上了高墙。
Chéng Héguāng grits his teeth, takes the Longevity Sword to his side, and leaps onto the high wall.

鹭鸶剪：……有劳你了。
Paper Heron: Chéng! I owe you for this.

鹭鸶剪：你与梅花教有烧屋之仇，却仍愿鼎力相助。若涣州能幸免于难，我定帮你重建老屋。
Paper Heron: For setting aside grudges and helping me. I know the School of Mei burned down your home. If we survive this, I'll help you build a new one.

程和光：……烧屋之仇？
Cheng Heguang: The School of Mei?

闻言，墙顶上的青年转过身来，罕见地露出了一个笑容。
At these words, the young man atop the wall turns around, his usually stern face broken into a rare, wild-eyed smile.

程和光：实话告诉你吧！
Cheng Heguang: To tell you the truth ...

程和光：那夜——火是我自己放的。
Cheng Heguang: I set that fire myself.

鹭鸶剪：什么——？
Paper Heron: Wait, what?

鹭鸶剪错愕望去，但青瓦上已经空无一人。
Her eyes widen in surprise, but the tiles stand empty before she can respond.

眼前，一群显出原形的精怪于暗处涌来，眼睛在月色的照映下发着绿光。
Before her, Yao surge from the shadows in their true forms, eyes gleaming green beneath the moon.

鹭鸶剪：哎呀，真是人不可貌相……
Paper Heron: Well now, never judge a book by its cover, eh?

梅花教信徒Ⅳ：鹭鸶剪，还剑来！
School of Mei Believer IV: Heron! Return the sword at once!

鹭鸶剪：我若是不，又能如何？
Paper Heron: And if I refuse?

鹭鸶剪：来吧，让我试试任仙子的徒弟！
Paper Heron: Come, let me see how Rén trains her students!

衙门内十分安静。
The Yamen is silent. The bell beneath the roof's beastly guardians has not moved.

程和光跨过大门，几步掠到仍亮着灯的书房前，伸手便要推门。
Chéng Héguāng crosses over the gate. In a few strides, he reaches the still-lit study and extends his hand toward the door.

？？？：……守备……
???: Commander Lì ...

陌生的声音使他停下了动作。
The unfamiliar voice stops him in place.

程和光：有其他人在……？
Cheng Heguang: There's someone else inside?

思忖片刻后，程和光在门前蹲下，专心聆听门内的一举一动。
After a moment's consideration, he crouches and places his ear up to the door.

？？？：哈！守备真是好计策。
???: Haha! It truly was a masterstroke.

？？？：在厉守备下达抓捕的命令后，精怪们走投无路，果然都被迫逃入了教门。
???: Had it not been for your arrests, the Yao wouldn't have turned to me so quickly, or in such numbers.

厉晦锋：为渊驱鱼，为丛驱雀……我不过是反过来利用罢了。
Li Huifeng: As an otter drives fish into the lakes and the eagle leads birds into the woods, heh heh, the hunter must know where his prey will run.

？？？：你对我们梅花教助力颇多，陆总兵那边，我绝不会忘记我们之前的承诺。
???: You have honored your word. I will keep your efforts in mind when I next speak to your superiors.

？？？：只是如今，还有一事要拜托守备——
???: I have one more favor to ask.

后面的话渐渐听不清了，因为血气已在眼前翻涌。
The conversation grows indistinct as fury clouds Chéng Héguāng's focus.

回过神来时，大门已经被一脚踢开。
Clarity returns. But only after he finds himself standing resolutely behind a door that has been kicked wide open.

程和光：——厉晦锋！
Cheng Heguang: Lì Huìfēng!

SU-18 有舍有得 / Pain and Gain

程和光：——唔！
Cheng Heguang: Urgh!

程和光推开门扉，眼见几滴墨点直冲着自己面门飞来。
The door swings back toward him, and he instinctively pushes it aside. Ink droplets fly across his face.

他下意识侧身躲避，露出了系在身后的长生剑。
He sidesteps, revealing the Longevity Sword strapped to his back.

任仙子：哦……？厉守备真是手眼通天啊，我还没开口，这剑竟就自己送上门了。
Master Ren: You do indeed work wonders, Commander. My lost sword has shown up at your door before I even asked for it.

道士打扮的清丽女子戏谑地收回了笔，目光看向一边的厉晦锋。
The elegant woman in Daoist robes withdraws her brush mockingly, looking over to the commander.

对方并不表态，只是看着程和光出鞘一半的长刀。
He offers no response; instead, his eyes linger on the blade Chéng Héguāng now holds half-drawn.

厉晦锋：和光，坐下吧。
Li Huifeng: Héguāng, take a seat.

厉晦锋指了指屋内的一把椅子。程和光分毫未动，手因为握刀太紧而有些微颤。
He gestures toward a chair in the room. Chéng Héguāng doesn't budge, his hand trembling over the grip of the sword.

厉晦锋：仙子，我向你介绍。他便是程和光。本领高强，办事利落。在“高跷巡神”时，也出了大力气的。
Li Huifeng: Pardon the intrusion, Master Rén. This is Chéng, that subordinate I've mentioned, a promising young man. He has proven to be of great use.

见程和光并不领情，厉晦锋也不作坚持，只是扭头向二人介绍起来人。
Chéng Héguāng makes it clear he will not offer a greeting. Lì Huìfēng decides not to insist before introducing him to the woman as if his arrival had been nothing more than a social visit.

厉晦锋：和光，这位是任仙子，梅花教的掌教，也是陆总兵的座上宾。我曾和她提起过你家里的事，仙子甚是同情。
Li Huifeng: Héguāng, this is Master Rén, the head of the School of Mei and a respected friend of Lord Lù. I have told her of your hardships, and she has expressed her sympathies.

任仙子：原来你就是程巡检，我还没见过你的时候，就有人问过我是不是烧了你的房子。
Master Ren: Well met, Chief Constable Chéng. Your commander speaks highly of you. I hope you do not bear me any ill will. I understand some blame my school for your unfortunate fire.

任仙子：你父亲的事，我已知晓。你极力证明自己，却总被缚住手脚，真是可怜可怜！
Master Ren: You have suffered a great deal of troubles. I can only imagine how far your star would rise if it weren't for your unfortunate parentage.

任仙子：今日在此相见，也算你我有缘，我便助你一程。
Master Ren: If fate has led us to meet this day, it must have its reasons. I cannot do much, but I may offer some aid to your career.

任仙子解下腰间的一枚令牌，随手扔到程和光面前。
She removes a token from her waist and tosses it before the young constable.

任仙子：这是总兵给我的信物。你寻剑有功，长生剑给我，我自会替你去总兵面前美言。
Master Ren: A personal gift from the venerable Lord Lù. His influence carries quite far, I'm sure you know. I wonder how he might look upon the constable that returned my sword to me.

任仙子：届时，你想谋什么职位，都任你挑选。
Master Ren: With our recommendation, a promotion would certainly follow.

程和光仍是紧紧握着手里的长刀，目光并未看向地上的令牌。
Chéng Héguāng maintains his grip on the blade, not sparing the token on the ground even the courtesy of a glance.

程和光：原来你们早就串通好了……证据、上级、关系，都是借口。
Cheng Heguang: You-You've been conspiring all along. All that talk of evidence, hmph, it was just an attempt to stall me.

程和光：你一直都和梅花教狼狈为奸，从最开始……！
Cheng Heguang: You've been in their pocket from the start!

厉晦锋：和光。
Li Huifeng: Héguāng.

厉晦锋冷不丁地出声，打断了年轻巡检激动的陈辞。
His commander interjects, attempting to douse the young constable's fiery accusations.

厉晦锋：把陆总兵的令牌捡起来吧。你不是一直想要尽快擢升，用功名洗刷程家的耻辱吗？
Li Huifeng: Pick up the token. Is this not what you've always wanted? To redeem your family name?

厉晦锋：捡起它，你一直以来的心愿便达成了。
Li Huifeng: Take it. Your long-cherished wish can come true.

对方的声音不疾不徐，一如往常。
His voice drips out at a measured pace, as always.

程和光难以置信地望去，刀光在墙上的投影晃了一晃。
Chéng Héguāng stares in disbelief. The blade's shadow on the wall wavers.

程和光：厉晦锋！事到如今，你还和我说这些？！
Cheng Heguang: Lì Huìfēng! Have you lost your senses?

程和光：你知道你到底在做什么吗？若任仙子拿剑升仙，涣州将有大灾，城镇将全部陷落，百姓将流离失所！！！
Cheng Heguang: Do you hear yourself? If she takes this sword, she will bring calamity upon us all!

程和光：你身为守备，却助纣为虐，为虎作伥，任由梅花教草菅人命！现在你不去疏散百姓，却在这里为自己谋前程好处。你——
Cheng Heguang: Not only do you act as an agent of evil, allowing her to harm your people, but you even dare to profit from their suffering! You—

任仙子：——哈哈哈哈哈！
Master Ren: Hahaha ...

任仙子忽然爆发出阵阵大笑，打断了这场对话。
The Daoist woman begins to laugh, as if their exchange had only been an amusing story.

任仙子：助纣为虐，为虎作伥？为自己谋前程好处？程巡检，你在说谁啊？
Master Ren: "Agent of evil"? "Profit from their suffering"? Have you looked at yourself, Chief Chéng?

任仙子：最急着抓拿精怪，换取功名的，不就是你么？给这城中小妖带来最大恐惧，逼它们入我梅花教的，不也是你吗？
Master Ren: Haven't you been arresting Yao day and night for the sake of your own glory? Are you not the very reason they sought refuge at my door?

程和光：血口喷人！我早该想到，衙门怎会有振气铃这种道门法器……“高跷巡神”从一开始就是你们自导自演！
Cheng Heguang: That is a perversion of the truth! Hah! I should've seen it before—the Reversion Bell. How else could our town have come by a Daoist relic? The parade itself was your doing!

任仙子：哈哈？你当真能早想到？你抓捕精怪时，眼里当真有其他吗？
Master Ren: For all of the Yao you imprisoned and interrogated, you still had no knowledge of our designs, did you?

任仙子：那些短命精怪不过是想要给自己搏一条活路，却被你做了立功的筹码！
Master Ren: Those poor, pitiful Yao, only wanting another day to live, crushed beneath the chief's boots, in his hunger for power.

程和光：胡说！它们妖言惑众，诱拐百姓，本该受罚！
Cheng Heguang: Lies! They were arrested for deceiving the people, not for my benefit!

任仙子：笑话！自我建了教门，不知多少人想混入其中！口口声声说自己被精怪引诱，却私下削尖了脑袋，要与我等精怪为伍！
Master Ren: Hah! Deceiving the people! And what lie was it that drove them to beg for the Method of Longevity?

任仙子：究竟是遭遇蒙骗，还是怕传出去面上无光，信口胡说，你可有真问个清楚？你又可曾真正见过实证！
Master Ren: Were they deceived, or did they only accuse me out of spite after being turned away? Some "investigation"!

任仙子：你在班房巡检那一个个战果时，心中可有它想？！
Master Ren: As you strode through that prison, did it ever cross your mind that the truth may be the very opposite?

程和光：……！
Cheng Heguang: ...!

回忆

鸟妖：我们只是想通过别的法子活得久一点，程巡检，你何故为难我们？
Bird: We only want a little more time in this world, Chief Chéng. Why must you stand in our way?

鸟妖：我们从来都没有害过任何一个人！只是想活下去！
Bird: Only a few borrowed days! We never hurt anyone!

鸟妖：我什么都没有做！放我出去！我等不起了！
Bird: I've done nothing wrong! Release me! Every moment is precious!

消回忆

冷汗从程和光的额角上滴落，他忽地意识到任仙子确有实话。
Cold sweat drips over Chéng Héguāng's temples. He realizes with some pain that this woman speaks the truth.

任仙子：不过，我倒要谢谢你。
Master Ren: Hmph. You needn't trouble yourself, Chief Chéng. In fact, I should thank you.

任仙子：要不是你这般问心无愧，我未必能这么快攒到足够的气。
Master Ren: Were it not for your diligence, I'd have never gathered so much Qi in such a short time.

任仙子：涣州若是陷落，其中也有你一份力啊，程巡检。这令牌给你，值当。
Master Ren: Hmph. Whether Huanzhou is saved or meets its ruin this night, much of the credit shall be yours.

程和光：什么……？！
Cheng Heguang: You—

程和光怒而瞪目，任仙子全然不在意，飘至厉晦锋身侧。
He glares, eyes raging with fury, but the Daoist Master no longer seems willing to entertain him as she drifts to Lì Huìfēng's side.

任仙子：我真是不懂。你一生汲汲营营，所谋所求就在眼前，还要装什么？
Master Ren: You humans are odd indeed. Have you not spent your entire life attempting to cleanse yourself of your father's dishonor?

任仙子：畏葸不前，还不如那些坦荡小人来得痛快！
Master Ren: Why shy away from your actions now, when they might finally be rewarded?

程和光：不是这样的……！我不是为了这些——
Cheng Heguang: That's not why I did it! I didn't—

厉晦锋：——和光。
Li Huifeng: Héguāng.

不知不觉间，厉晦锋已捡起了地上的令牌。
Before he realizes it, Lì Huìfēng has already retrieved the token from the floor.

程和光第一次看清它。令牌镶金嵌银，明晃晃书写着总兵的名号。
Chéng Héguāng sees it clearly for the first time. A symbol of power, inlaid with gold and silver.

厉晦锋：拿走令牌。放下剑。
Li Huifeng: Pick up the token, and put down the sword.

厉晦锋：你知道太多，留不住你。离开涣州。自有广阔前程。
Li Huifeng: You have heard too much; you can't stay here any longer. Take the token and go. Find a new life for yourself elsewhere.

厉晦锋拂去令牌上的灰尘，将它递了过来。
He brushes away the dust and extends the token toward Chéng Héguāng.

厉晦锋：你忘了，你曾经在衙门堂下，是怎么立誓的吗？
Li Huifeng: Or have you forgotten the vow you made to me?

程和光：……我……
Cheng Heguang: I ...

厉晦锋：你想要什么？
Li Huifeng: What is it you want?

程和光：……我知家父与匪类同流合污，已成一桩耻辱。但我绝不会重蹈覆辙。
Cheng Heguang: My father brought shame not only upon himself, but upon those who placed their trust in him. I swear I will not make the same mistake.

程和光：兵就是兵，贼就是贼。我绝对会与我父亲划清界限，洗刷程家的污名，不让别人再嘲笑我的家人！
Cheng Heguang: It is said that a warrior is a warrior, and a bandit is a bandit. But I am not my father, and I will remove the stain on my family name!

程和光：请守备给我一个机会！
Cheng Heguang: Commander, all I ask is one chance!

消回忆

任仙子：唉，程巡检也不要太介怀小道那番话。
Master Ren: *sigh* Chief Chéng, I pray you would not hold my words against me. They were spoken in the heat of the moment.

任仙子：毕竟，妖就是妖。非我族类，其心必异。
Master Ren: *sneer* You are human, and we are Yao. Beings of different kinds are never of one mind. Our natures simply do not align.

任仙子：借此立功，更是人之常情。你何错之有啊？
Master Ren: So your interests clash with ours. Why blame yourself for what was bound to happen?

虚虚实实间，二人的声音忽远忽近，如钟摆轮回。
Between truth and lies, their voices grow distant, then near, back and forth like a swinging pendulum.

虽是秋末，却觉得置身于浓稠的热气里，几乎无法呼吸。
Though the autumn wanes outside, inside the air feels thick and stifling.

程和光：兵就是兵。贼就是贼。
Cheng Heguang: A warrior is a warrior, and a bandit is a bandit.

程和光：人就是人。妖就是妖。
Cheng Heguang: Beings of different kinds are never of one mind.

程和光：到头来，这竟是一回事……哈哈哈，哈哈哈哈……
Cheng Heguang: So that's how it is. Hahaha, hahahaha.

程和光已至角落。
He's been backed into the corner.

他已无路可退。
No escape remains.

程和光：……厉守备，我最后问你一次。
Cheng Heguang: Commander, for the last time—

程和光：涣州将有大灾，你不知道吗？
Cheng Heguang: Are you aware that Huanzhou now lingers at the edge of destruction?

灯火下，那人的表情却不分明。只是声音依然毫无波澜。
Under the lamplight, his mentor's expression remains unclear. But his voice holds steady and darkly calm.

厉晦锋：我知，或是不知……
Li Huifeng: Yes and no—

厉晦锋：又有什么分别？
Li Huifeng: Does it even matter?

程和光：……哈哈，好！好一个没有分别！
Cheng Heguang: Hahahaha, fair point! A fair point!

所有的愤怒、诧异和失望都化作了一声大笑。
All his rage, shock, and disappointment dissolve into a single bitter laugh.

言语间，刹那间，程和光长刀出鞘，墨点也直刺向了他的腰间。
In that instant, Chéng Héguāng's blade leaves its sheath as ink strikes toward his waist.

弹射间，屋内油灯的火光灭了数盏，令牌也被墨点击成废铁。
In a flash, several oil lamps are extinguished. The token shatters into worthless scrap under the ink's force.

程和光：我早该知道。
Cheng Heguang: I should have known.

程和光：我一心想在衙门谋求一个证明，一个关于我是何种人的证明。却忘了这里是哪里，也漏看了它的规矩。
Cheng Heguang: For years, I worked to prove myself to you, hoping my merits would prove the strength of my character. I was so fixated on my goal that I failed to see the truth.

程和光：在一个错误的地方谋求胜利，也许本身就是一种助纣为虐。最终徒增的，只有错误罢了。
Cheng Heguang: Now I see it clearly. Seeking favor from people like you only led me deeper into dishonor.

程和光轻轻摇了摇头。
He shakes his head ruefully, mourning years of wasted effort.

程和光：可到头来，我真正想要的，并不是功名。只是一份公正而已。
Cheng Heguang: I never cared about promotions or power. I only ever wanted to do what was right.

程和光：若拿这令牌意味着失去公正，我何须拿它？
Cheng Heguang: If I picked up that token, I would be betraying all that I believe in.

程和光扯下巡检的腰牌，扔到了厉晦锋的脚下。
He tears his Chief Constable's token from his waist and throws it to Lì Huìfēng's feet.

程和光：厉守备，你说没有分别，可兵就是兵，贼就是贼！！！
Cheng Heguang: Commander, you claim that it doesn't matter what you know. You think that I should be a soldier and follow what you say.

程和光：我是贼，我从来都是贼！
Cheng Heguang: But I see now, I am a bandit, and I always will be!

程和光：——这个官，我不做了！！！
Cheng Heguang: I want no place among your kind!

灯火摇曳时，厉晦锋的刀刃已至眼前。
In the flickering lamplight, Lì Huìfēng's blade flashes forward before his eyes.

厉晦锋：程道官和我有过交情。他出事后，我是真想帮帮他的儿子。
Li Huifeng: Your father was once my friend. After what happened, I took it upon myself to aid you through your difficulties.

厉晦锋：——可你实在油盐不进。
Li Huifeng: But it seems you're too stubborn to be helped.

二人缠斗在一起，将屋内劈砍得一片狼藉。
The two men meet in a furious clash of blades and incantations, reducing the room around them to shambles.

相持不下时，任仙子骤然出掌，将程和光震退几步。
But at the height of their deadlock, Master Rén intervenes, suddenly striking Chéng Héguāng with her palm, forcing him back several steps.

任仙子：凡夫俗子，着实恼人！还不把长生剑交出来！
Master Ren: You hopeless fool! Surrender the sword at once!

程和光：我答应过别人护好这把剑。
Cheng Heguang: I gave my word to protect it.

程和光：我已错了太多，好在如今，我还有一个承诺能守。
Cheng Heguang: I've made many mistakes. I will not make another.

程和光：——你若想得剑，便先杀了我！
Cheng Heguang: If you want the sword, you'll have to kill me first!

任仙子径直拂动衣袖，她的影子在墙面上如蛇一般蜕皮变形。
The Daoist flicks her sleeves dramatically as her shadow on the wall transforms like a serpent shedding its skin.

那副温和可亲的旧皮囊寸寸碎裂，顷刻便焚作灰烬。
Her gentle facade shatters, falling away like a cascade of ash.

程和光：——？！
Cheng Heguang: —?

任仙子甩出铁笔，几步之间再次攻到程和光身前。
Master Rén draws her iron brush and closes the distance in mere strides.

程和光：呃……！这般下去，坚持不了多久……！
Cheng Heguang: Ugh! Can't hold out much longer.

恍惚间，他看见空中飘过了一缕红纸。
Dazed by her assault, he nearly misses the slip of red paper drifting past him.

程和光：……！
Cheng Heguang: ...!

任仙子：你在看哪里？！
Master Ren: Eyes forward. There's no escape now!

视频

程和光：呃！
Cheng Heguang: Ugh!

鹭鸶剪：程和光！
Paper Heron: Chéng!

程和光：接剑！
Cheng Heguang: Take the sword!

鹭鸶剪：多谢！
Paper Heron: My thanks!

鹭鸶剪：希望我来得不算迟！
Paper Heron: I hope I'm not too late!

SU-19 区区 / Significance of the Insignificant

鹭鸶剪得了剑，顺势将剑锋一偏，挡下了斜刺里飞来的墨点。
Paper Heron catches the sword midair, using its edge to deflect the ink droplets surging toward her from the side.

见此架势，任仙子猛然往前半步，拦在门前。
Seeing this, Master Rén lunges forward half a step, barring the doorway.

任仙子：鹭鸶剪，把剑给我。
Master Ren: Return the sword to me.

鹭鸶剪：休想。
Paper Heron: Not while I yet breathe.

任仙子：好，好……！你如这般坦诚，倒也是一桩好事！
Master Ren: So be it. It will spare me from listening to another of your worthless lectures.

任仙子：你既已将一切托付给我，何不爽快将剑拿来，继续过你的逍遥日子？
Master Ren: You entrusted that sword to me long ago. Why not simply hand it over and return to your carefree wandering?

任仙子：哈，鹭鸶剪，你究竟不是真仙人！
Master Ren: Perhaps you aren't so free from desire!

火场之中，刀光剑影，鹭鸶剪仍在与任仙子缠斗。
Amid the flames, blades flash. Paper Heron and Master Rén remain locked in combat.

房梁在大火中熊熊燃烧，程和光警惕躲避着坍塌的木条，而厉晦锋早已不见踪影。
Beams blaze above them. Chéng Héguāng dodges as collapsing timbers fall nearby, only now realizing that his commander has vanished within the smoke and fled into the night.

突然间，如万人擂鼓，伴随着巨大的响动之声，地面如鼓面般震动起来。
Suddenly, as if ten thousand drums were struck at once, the earth trembles and quakes.

程和光：怎么了？!
Cheng Heguang: What's going on?

鹭鸶剪急忙望向书院天井那角天幕。
Paper Heron whips around toward the patch of sky visible through the study's courtyard.

鹭鸶剪：……是揽诸。
Paper Heron: Lǎnzhū.

鹭鸶剪：险道兽醒了。
Paper Heron: The beast has awakened.

任仙子：终究是我的时辰到了。鹭鸶剪，以你现在负伤的程度，甚至无法为揽诸调气——你什么都做不了了。
Master Ren: The moment has come at last. You are weak, Heron. Your Qi will not be enough to contend with Lǎnzhū.

任仙子：你便抱着这把剑，看我如何成就大业吧。
Master Ren: Keep the sword if you must. I will ascend with or without it!

任仙子振臂大笑，提步跃出了火场。
Her triumphant laughter rings out as she leaps away over the growing fires.

程和光：她！
Cheng Heguang: She—

鹭鸶剪：程巡检，别追了……咳……
Paper Heron: Don't, Chéng. *cough*

鹭鸶剪：来不及了。
Paper Heron: It's too late.

昏天黑地，月光被浓雾吞噬，大地如微鼾般颤抖，无措的民众涌上街头。
Darkness engulfs half the sky, devouring the moonlight. The earth trembles as if it were breathing. Panicked civilians flood the streets.

烈火烧融了半边天际，房梁坍塌，砖石崩解，灾劫已至。
Fire-lit columns of smoke rise over the other half. Beams collapse, bricks crumble. The calamity has arrived.

祝县县民Ⅱ：地震！大地震！
County Resident II: Earthquake! It's an earthquake!

祝县县民Ⅱ：地裂开了——救命！有人掉进地缝里去了！救命啊！
County Resident II: The ground is splitting apart! I saw someone fall into it. Help! Get help!!

祝县县民Ⅲ：房子塌了——我的房子——
County Resident III: My house!

程和光：这……这就是揽诸带来的灾殃……
Cheng Heguang: This-This is Lǎnzhū's power.

鹭鸶剪：任仙子开始便打算激化揽诸，夺气升仙。揽诸造成的浩劫将更甚往日。
Paper Heron: Rén has agitated it, forcing its Qi to surge just so she can siphon it for herself. She is inviting a disaster greater than any known before.

而在混乱无措的民众中，一列行队整齐的游行队伍正喊着洪亮的口号走来。
Against the swirling trample of the helpless civilians, a parade advances, chanting above the panicked din around them.

梅花教信徒众：黑绒吞白骨，寒原鬼泣呜。
School of Mei Believers: Withered grass devours bone. On icy plain the spirits moan.

梅花教信徒众：城覆仙人现，长生免祸殃。
School of Mei Believers: When the city falls, the Immortal descends. Longevity granted, no death, no end.

祝县县民Ⅱ：这到底是怎么了……
County Resident II: What-What on earth is happening?

梅花教信徒Ⅱ：命数未尽！末日已至！
School of Mei Believer II: The path lies untraveled, but the end has begun!

梅花教信徒Ⅱ：唯有长生可得救赎！
School of Mei Believer II: Seek salvation in longevity!

祝县县民Ⅱ：救赎？如何长生？
County Resident II: Salvation? Longevity? How?

强震动

祝县县民Ⅱ：仙人救我！
County Resident II: Help us, Immortal One!

程和光：呸……那妖怪，现在倒真成百姓眼中的救世仙人了！
Cheng Heguang: Hmph. They think Rén is here to save them. Ridiculous!

鹭鸶剪站在这混乱的街头，一时间也有点无措。
Paper Heron stands amid the wreckage of a street, feeling strangely helpless despite herself.

她抱着手中的剑，低下头，深深地叹了一口气。
She holds the Longevity Sword, bows her head, and lets out a deep sigh.

鹭鸶剪：归根结底，这一切是因我而起。
Paper Heron: This is all because of me. I brought all of this upon us.

鹭鸶剪：我知白马派已亡，却不忍心师门术法失传，竟以为广传此法能造福众生，也是一桩好事。
Paper Heron: When the White Horse School collapsed, I couldn't bear to see the Method of Longevity disappear. I believed that sharing it with Rén would be for the benefit of all.

鹭鸶剪：可我忘记了祸兮福所倚，福兮祸所伏，天大的好里自然带着天大的恶。
Paper Heron: But I forgot that with fortune comes disaster, and how easily a well-intended deed can lead to peril.

鹭鸶剪：法门无错，众生所求亦无错。是我轻视了人心，忤逆了天道，托付错了人，方才酿下此等大祸。
Paper Heron: The Method itself is not wicked, and those who put their faith in Rén are not evil in nature, but I-I entrusted a dangerous tool to the wrong person.

鹭鸶剪：错全在我。
Paper Heron: I am the one to blame.

程和光看不清鹭鸶剪的神情，但清楚生灵涂炭的景象已映在鹭鸶剪眼底。
It's difficult to read her expression. He cannot help but see the hellish disaster reflected in the depths of her eyes.

鹭鸶剪：事情因我而起，也应因我而终。
Paper Heron: And I must be the one to end it.

鹭鸶剪缓缓地环视着这场灾劫。
Paper Heron surveys the scene ahead of her.

鹭鸶剪：你快走吧，离开这里。
Paper Heron: You need to leave.

程和光：去哪儿？
Cheng Heguang: Leave? Where to?

鹭鸶剪：去哪儿都行，以你的脚力，日夜兼程奔离涣州，兴许能躲过这次灾殃。
Paper Heron: Anywhere but here. If you go now and run day and night, you may yet survive.

程和光：凭什么？
Cheng Heguang: Why?

鹭鸶剪有些惊讶地抬头，程和光的语气是毫不掩饰的愤怒。
She looks up, surprised at the fury in Chéng Héguāng's tone.

程和光：大灾当前，我若是见死不救，只顾自己，与那些贪图名利、弃城而走的高官又有何分别？！
Cheng Heguang: If I flee now, how am I any different from those cowardly lords?

程和光：我程和光从来只想不昧本心，求得一个公正。如今我已不是巡检，更不必在意什么名利规矩！
Cheng Heguang: I may no longer be Chief Constable, but I still answer to my conscience!

鹭鸶剪：你不求生路？
Paper Heron: You don't fear death?

程和光：我只求无悔。
Cheng Heguang: I fear living in regret.

程和光握紧了他的双拳，火光在他的双目中熠熠生辉。
He clutches his fists. The fire in his eyes burns brighter than any mere reflection.

程和光：你曾借剑助我，我尚未回报。此时离去，便是无信无义。
Cheng Heguang: You trusted me with your sword. I cannot repay you with abandonment.

程和光：厉晦锋虽弃城而走，但我仍可用他的腰牌暂时调度巡捕，营救灾民。
Cheng Heguang: Lì Huìfēng has fled, but I still have his token to command the other constables.

程和光：我会留在这里，做我力所能及之事。
Cheng Heguang: I will aid you in any way I can.

鹭鸶剪：此事非同小可，你若要来，九死一生。
Paper Heron: But this is no ordinary crisis. I cannot guarantee your safety.

程和光：我会来。
Cheng Heguang: All the more reason.

程和光：安排好这边，我便会去找你，你要保重。
Cheng Heguang: I'll come find you once I instruct the other constables to evacuate the townsfolk.

面前的青年字字决绝，鹭鸶剪便也不再劝诫。
Seeing the young man's resolve, Paper Heron nods.

鹭鸶剪：保重。
Paper Heron: Be careful.

短暂的相视过后，程和光毅然转身踏入了废墟与火焰，而鹭鸶剪伸手掐诀，消失在了原地。
They exchange a quick glance. Chéng Héguāng turns and leaps back into the burning ruins. Paper Heron casts an incantation and vanishes from the spot.

SU-20 不复还 / No Turning Back

道道闪电劈开厚重的云雾，激得大地战栗。
Lightning tears through the thick clouds, shaking the earth with each strike.

即使天地变色，任仙子仍挺立于梅花树前，而以惠姑为首的梅花教众则安然围坐于梅花树下。
Master Rén stands before the Mei tree, unmoved by the clashing of earth and sky. Her students sit around her in a ring with muted, fearful reverence. Mayfly is among them, sitting at the front.

任仙子：立教以来，这棵梅花树便是本派之根基，也是你们长生之寄托！
Master Ren: This Mei tree has ever been the root of our school, and now, it is the key to our greatest triumph.

任仙子：你们要不惜一切代价看护好它。
Master Ren: We must protect it at all costs.

任仙子：现在，听我号令——起阵！
Master Ren: Now, on my command: Form the array.

梅花教信徒众：天地自然！秽气分散！
School of Mei Believers: By nature's might, evil be purged!

随着信徒们催动法阵，大地猛然颤动，随后凹陷成天坑，砂石如被巨口吞没，天坑内竟显出一个湖。
As the believers channel their energy into the array, the ground shakes violently and a massive sinkhole opens around them, swallowing sand and stones. Soon after, water wells up from the pit, forming into a lake.

那湖射出金光，如在云上又映出了一个太阳。
Golden rays shoot out from the lake, projecting daylight onto the clouds like a rising sun.

任仙子：哈哈，日月同天，原来是这么回事。
Master Ren: Ahahahaha. "The balance will be broken, and the sun and moon shall share the sky," so that's what the warning was about.

任仙子：揽诸与那白马派缠斗千年，何曾想到今日会了结于我手！
Master Ren: The beast has battled with the White Horse School for a millennium. But today, it will die by my hand.

山药精：可……揽诸，在哪里呢？
Yam: But where is the beast?

任仙子：那揽诸早与涣州大地融为一体，这个湖便是它的瞳孔，是我们唯一可以接触它的地方。
Master Ren: Its body has long merged with the land. This very lake is its eye, the only part we may yet reach.

任仙子：时候到了！起阵！
Master Ren: The time has come. Let it begin.

任仙子：八方威神，以气化形！
Master Ren: Through the might of all eight powers, we harness the flow of Qi!

任仙子神秘术

任仙子掐诀念咒，飓风骤起，吹得湖面掀起涟漪。
Master Rén begins an incantation and chants. A typhoon erupts around her, whipping their new lake into a frothing whirlpool.

金光熠熠，湖的外围现出一个八卦阵，如天罗地网般死死地扣住了湖。
Beneath the golden shimmer, a Bagua array appears at the lake's edge, locking it down like a cage of light.

阵法
震动

任仙子：我花数十年研究出这“镇殃大阵”，只要阵成，揽诸便会毙亡！
Master Ren: This Quelling Array has been the work of decades. Once it begins, there will be no escape for Lǎnzhū. Its death is certain.

任仙子：无需长生剑，我也有万无一失的后手！
Master Ren: With it, I will reach my goal, even without the sword.

山药精兀然消失，烟雾之中，一道红光破空袭来。
Suddenly, Yam vanishes. In the smoke, a red light breaks through.

鹭鸶剪：开！
Paper Heron: Begone!

鹭鸶剪神秘术特效

任仙子身形一跃，但鹭鸶剪的剪纸骤然散开，仍有几片割破了她的衣角。
Master Rén leaps to dodge the attack, but Paper Heron's paper slips prove faster, and a few pieces tear at her robe's hem.

任仙子：拦住她！
Master Ren: Stop her.

獾子精：是！
Badger: Yes, Master.

言罢，几名弟子施剑摆出防御的法阵，数柄长剑刺向两人。
Several students form a defensive line. Long swords pointing out at the two.

刺猬精：我们不会让你们妨碍任仙子！
Hedgehog: You'll have to get past us first, Heron.

鹭鸶剪：退下，我无意伤害你们！
Paper Heron: Stand back. I'm not here to fight you.

但精怪们纹丝不动，只是紧盯着鹭鸶剪。
Yet the Yao don't move. They stare at Paper Heron expectantly.

程和光：——还有我！
Cheng Heguang: Take this!

对峙间，数道银光射来，精怪们反应不及，即使拨落大部分的铁针，还是漏了几根。
Silver streaks flash in, breaking the standoff. The Yao are helpless to deflect the sudden barrage of needles.

任仙子：呃啊！
Master Ren: Aghh!

刺猬精：仙子！
Hedgehog: Master!

仅是分神一瞬，任仙子便觉得身上猛然负压千钧之力。
Though it was only a brief moment of distraction, Master Rén staggers against the immense pressure crushing down on her.

獾子精：固防！
Badger: Hold the line!

趁群妖还没回过神来，程和光操纵着铁刃刺穿“镇殃大阵”的阵型，寻机靠近阵眼。
Before the Yao can react, Chéng Héguāng drives his blade into the Quelling Array, seeking an opening to strike its core.

任仙子：啊————护阵！
Master Ren: Agh! Protect the array!

鹭鸶剪：任仙子，收手吧！若是阵破……
Paper Heron: Stop this now, Rén! If the array shatters ...

鹭鸶剪：你只会被反噬，神形俱灭！
Paper Heron: It will bring about your annihilation.

任仙子：闭嘴！
Master Ren: Enough talk.

任仙子：鹭鸶剪，你不能理解我等之伟望，就别来坏事！
Master Ren: There's nothing you can do to stop me. Get out of my way!

破天的长啸中，任仙子的身形急速地萎缩。染血的碎屑如梅花般漫天飘散，风吹出了她人类的模样，也埋葬了逝去的教徒们。
With an earth-shattering scream, Master Rén's body shrivels up like a burst grape. Blood-stained fragments scattering apart like Mei petals. The wind reveals her human form and buries the fallen believers.

鹭鸶剪勉力近到惠姑身旁。
Paper Heron struggles to reach Mayfly.

鹭鸶剪：惠姑！你的气已接近亏空，再渡下去，会透支你自己的性命！你会死！
Paper Heron: Mayfly, you mustn't feed any more of your Qi to the array. You're draining yourself away.

惠姑：我……
Mayfly: I ...

鹭鸶剪急切地伸过手去，想将惠姑带离。
She reaches out desperately, trying to pull her little friend to safety.

惠姑却仍是立在原地。
Yet Mayfly doesn't move.

惠姑：……太晚了，鹭鸶剪。
Mayfly: I can't turn back now, Heron.

她艰难地从口袋里掏出草结护符，和那张皱巴巴的纸条一同放在了身侧。
Struggling, she pulls the amulet from her pocket and lays it beside her along with that wrinkled note.

惠姑：这一路上，谢谢你曾经帮过我。
Mayfly: Thank you for helping me get this far.

惠姑：我……求仁得仁，不后悔走上这条路。
Mayfly: I-I wanted this. I wanted to try. I have no regrets.

惠姑几近支撑不住，但依旧坚持抬起头，望向鹭鸶剪的方向。
She slumps over, unable to even pull herself up, yet she raises her head and looks toward Paper Heron.

任仙子：——走吧，孩子，你已求得了长生。
Master Ren: Good, sister. Let go now. Your wish has been fulfilled.

任仙子挣扎起身，却仍是不愿放弃成仙，苦苦维持着阵法。
Master Rén struggles to her feet, clinging to the array, unwilling to abandon her chance at ascension.

湖周围的飓风愈加猛烈，在气被渡尽的瞬间，惠姑身子一晃，倒下了。
The wind whips and howls around the lake. Then, as her Qi at last runs out, Mayfly's body collapses.

护符和纸条被尽数卷入飓风中，撕得粉碎。
The amulet and note are swept up in the typhoon and torn to shreds.

鹭鸶剪：……惠姑！
Paper Heron: Mayfly!

程和光：鹭鸶剪！
Cheng Heguang: Heron, watch out!

在鹭鸶剪闪神的瞬间，数把剑围攻了过来。程和光反身，以刀鞘扛下这击。
She loses focus for only a moment, but it's enough time for several blades to strike at her. Chéng Héguāng whirls around and blocks them with the sheath of his blade.

望着这一切，鹭鸶剪觉得自己手中的剑仿佛千斤沉重，再也抬不起来。
Her strength fails her. Paper Heron suddenly feels as if the sword in her hand were as heavy as a mule.

鹭鸶剪：我……
Paper Heron: I ...

黑云压境，天雷滚滚，地面裂开又合上，砂土如面粉般被扬起，涣州已涣。
Black clouds press down against the sky. Thunder rolls. The earth tears open and slams shut. Sheets of coarse sand billow through the air. Huanzhou is lost.

哀鸿遍野，巡检们亦自顾不暇，这世间早已无一处是安宁之地。
Cries of anguish fill the streets. Even the constables can barely protect themselves. There is no place left to run.

任仙子的身后不停地有人在倒下，狐妖、兔女、小蝶虫……
Behind Master Rén, more Yao fall. Fox, Hare, Butterfly ...

鹭鸶剪望向惠姑倒下的地方，那里早已没了人形，只剩下一根芦草，被无序的众妖踩踏着。
Paper Heron looks to Mayfly's spot. Nothing remains there but a tuft of reeds, trampled by other frantic Yao.

一切生死，都已无可回转。
What is lost can never be recovered.

鹭鸶剪：……
Paper Heron: ...

在席卷天地的飓风中，飘荡着无数的、被撕裂的碎片。
Countless torn fragments swirl around, caught in the raging typhoon.

这些碎片像往常一样自她的世界飘过，却没有在石头上留下任何波澜。
They drift past her like everything in the world always has, leaving nothing marked on her stone heart.

鹭鸶剪：为何？
Paper Heron: Why?

鹭鸶剪：为何你们要到这里来……？为何你们如此孤注一掷，本是追求长生，又反而为此抛却性命？
Paper Heron: Why come all this way in seeking to extend your life, only to give it up so easily?

鹭鸶剪：为何你们要短暂热烈地来到世上，然后又如疾风骤雨一般死去……？
Paper Heron: Why must you come to this world, only to leave it so soon?

天地万物。芸芸众生。
A question that might as well be asked to all living things.

她静默地抱着长生剑，独立于空中。四下皆是空濛的虚无。
She stands alone in the air, holding the Longevity Sword. The world around her has become a void of darkness.

鹭鸶剪：我在那株梅树中待得太久，久到退化成了一颗石头。人间的声色，从此与我无关。
Paper Heron: I spent so long trapped inside that tree that I forgot what it felt like to be a part of the world.

鹭鸶剪：可石头应是无喜无悲、无知无觉的。
Paper Heron: Joy, sorrow, and pain became like distant memories.

鹭鸶剪：若我真是一颗石头，我为何总是感到如此痛苦，以至于一刻都不能忍受？
Paper Heron: But what is this bitterness that racks my heart now?

鹭鸶剪低下头，看向手中莹莹的白玉剑。
She lowers her head and examines the sword in her hands.

储存在长生剑中的气，此刻也在术阵中逸散了一些，如蚕茧抽丝般浮在空中。
Some of the Qi stored inside the Longevity Sword flows out into the array, pulled through the air like silk drawn from a cocoon.

渐白

师姐：来来来，师妹！看你关禁闭这么久，特地给你留的一碗桂花糖芋头……千万别告诉师父！
Pearl Finch: Come, Heron, come. You must be starved after that detention. I've saved you some taro. Best not let the master see it.

师父：顽劣！到时出外游历，闯出祸来，可莫把师父和几位师兄师姐说出去！
Master: Cheeky little rascal. I hope no one finds out you were my student on your travels.

任仙子：……是，是您从天雷中救了我……恩人！我将永生永世报答……
Master Ren: You-You saved my life. I swear I will repay you. I'll do whatever it takes.

鹭鸶剪：……
Paper Heron: ...

惠姑：怎…怎么样，鹭鸶剪？这桂花糯米糕好吃吗……对吧！我就讲，一定很甜吧？
Mayfly: So? How is it? Amazing, right? I told you it's delicious.

惠姑：我……求仁得仁，不后悔走上这条路……
Mayfly: I-I wanted this. I wanted to try. I have no regrets.

白马派众人：快过来，到梅树边来——！
White Horse School Students: Over here, Heron. Under the Mei tree.

师父：鹭鸶剪，记住。我辈问心无愧。
Master: Remember, Paper Heron. In the end, we need only answer to our conscience.

诸多画面，她曾在这百年间反复回想，如今不过一瞬，便云散烟消。
The scenes she replayed countless times over a hundred years now vanish from her in a single moment.

鹭鸶剪感慨地仰起头，一滴泪水撞碎在剑鞘之上。
Paper Heron tilts her head back, and a single tear shatters against the sheath.

鹭鸶剪：我明白了……
Paper Heron: I understand now.

鹭鸶剪：困住我的并非石头，而是极度的悔恨。
Paper Heron: It wasn't my isolation that numbed my senses. It was regret.

鹭鸶剪：因为这悔恨是我被封在树里的百年中，唯一切实拥有的东西。
Paper Heron: For a hundred years, it was the only thing I knew.

她轻轻地抽去了长生剑的剑鞘，露出了白玉的剑身。
She draws the Longevity Sword from its sheath, her hand slow and deliberate, revealing the white jade blade.

鹭鸶剪：揽诸已被激怒。任仙子升仙无论成败，涣州城都将分崩离析。除非……
Paper Heron: The beast's rage has grown beyond control. Whether Rén ascends or not, Huanzhou will fall to ruin. Unless ...

除非一切由何而起，便由何而终。
All things return to their beginning.

鹭鸶剪：师父、师姐、师兄。现在我终于明白，为何是我从你们中活下来。
Paper Heron: Master, now I understand why I survived.

鹭鸶剪：因为我还有未竟之命，而那一刻就是现在。
Paper Heron: I have an unfinished purpose. And now, I will realize it.

鹭鸶剪双手用力握住剑身，长生剑现出了裂痕。
She grips the Longevity Sword with both hands. A crack forms across the blade.

鹭鸶剪：只有见证过当年灭门的白马派弟子，才能重现那一日的封印，结束这场天地浩劫。
Paper Heron: Only one who witnessed the first seal as it was forged long ago can see this done.

天幕下，任仙子第一时间注意到了鹭鸶剪的异样。
Far beneath her, Master Rén takes notice of the change in her former teacher.

任仙子：住手！鹭鸶剪，你想干什么？！
Master Ren: Heron, what do you think you're doing?

任仙子：你想让他们白死吗？你难道没有长进吗！？你可知此剑一折，世间再无白马派？！
Master Ren: If you shatter the sword, those Yao will have died for nothing, and the White Horse School will be gone forever.

呼啸而过的烈风盖过了任仙子的呼喊。
Yet the howling wind drowns out her cry.

鹭鸶剪：百年后见。
Paper Heron: See you in a hundred years.

熟悉的声音在风中低了下去。百年前的风声散去后，梅树前浮出一道身影。
That familiar voice from a hundred years ago fades in the wind. Before the Mei tree, a figure materializes.

这影像越发凝实，生动，与芦草结在故事中所见的如出一辙。
The image grows more solid and vivid, exactly as Reed saw in the memories.

芦草结：……鹭鸶剪！
Reed: Heron!

看到那道身影时，芦草结不禁惊呼出声。
As her form solidifies, Reed can't suppress a gasp.

芦草结：难怪她会让我解开所有系结，难怪城里会有风网扰动！这些系结，是当年被长生剑凝滞的风！
Reed: I-I get it now. Those Wind Knots were frozen by the power of the Longevity Sword, that's why the Windweave's been experiencing so much interference.

芦草结：这就是长生之法的真相……难道她从此之后就一直被封在此地？
Reed: And Heron, she's been trapped here for all these years?

骡子：咴……！
Mule: Bray!

骡子欣喜地小跑两步，迫不及待地想引领两位老朋友在现实中的首次会面。
The mule trots out happily, eager to bring its friends, old and new, together at last.

见芦草结半天不动，便叼住她头顶草叶，轻轻拉扯起来。
Seeing Reed frozen in place, it gently tugs at her, taking a blade of grass on her head into its mouth.

鹭鸶剪：去。她可不是你的食物。
Paper Heron: Stop that. She's not a snack.

主人家笑了笑，老骡不情愿地朝一旁退去，小跑到梅树后。
She laughs. The old mule reluctantly trots aside and lingers behind the Mei tree.

鹭鸶剪：——终于见面了，“小小草”。
Paper Heron: It is good to finally see you in person, Reedit.

鹭鸶剪：因为阵法阻隔的缘故，让你辛苦了。很高兴你看起来过得还不错。
Paper Heron: I sincerely apologize for the trouble. There was little I could do from within the seal. You look well, though. I'm glad.

芦草结：你说你自会找我……没想到是以这种形式见面。
Reed: When you said you'd find me, I didn't think you meant like this.

芦草结：如果我没猜错，那些风，还有给我指明方向的纸页，应该都是你做的？
Reed: It was you, wasn't it? The wind, the paper notes, you used them to guide me here, didn't you?

鹭鸶剪：嗯，多亏了望气的小把戏，你应该见过很多次。
Paper Heron: I did. I believe you've seen this little Qi trick a few times by now.

鹭鸶剪：那场大战之后，我就一直被封在这梅花树中，无法与外界沟通。直到几年前，人们来这里拉了一些奇怪的线。
Paper Heron: Within the seal, I was unable to communicate with the outside world, until those curious strings were put up.

鹭鸶剪抬手指了指头顶的老梅树，以及树冠不远处的水泥电线杆。
She raises her finger and points first at the old Mei tree and then at the telephone pole standing next to its canopy.

鹭鸶剪：这些黑色的线里游走着一股股特殊的“气”，我的神秘术可以御使它们，所以才能在论坛上和你联系。
Paper Heron: An odd Qi runs through them, one I found I could control. That's how I got on the forum.

芦草结一头雾水地听着，随后忽然明了了什么。
Reed listens, making mental notes of her questions, until she arrives at a realization.

芦草结：你是说电流和信号？你的神秘术……可以让你通过这些光缆连接互联网？
Reed: Strings? You mean the cables? You're telling me you can connect to the Internet through Qi?

鹭鸶剪：或许吧？我不确定。不过，毕竟是受困于此，这些气有时候会忽然消失。
Paper Heron: It is a remarkable technology. Though at times, the Qi would disappear.

鹭鸶剪：这些时候我就没法看到你，也没法和你交流。
Paper Heron: When that happened, I could no longer reach you.

芦草结：好吧，虽然我很想采访你，但那估计是另一篇报道了——抱歉，我的时间真的很紧迫。
Reed: Well, as much as I'd like to dive into it—I really, really would—let's save it for another time, kinda on a deadline here.

她站定了脚步，认真地望着鹭鸶剪。
She stops and stares at Paper Heron.

芦草结：鹭鸶剪，按照我们说好的，我解开了所有风结。
Reed: I did what you asked, Heron. I untied all the knots.

芦草结：该轮到你履行承诺，给我答案了。
Reed: Now it's time for you to hold up your end of the deal.

芦草结：你亲口说过，长生剑折断，长生之法也随之断绝。那你先前在论坛上说的什么传法、什么线索，都是在骗我吗？

芦草结：还是说，这些风结里的故事……就是你想告诉我的全部？
Reed: Or by "teach me," did you mean showing me your story in the Wind Knots?

鹭鸶剪打量着她，笑容和语气都像芦草结曾看到的那样，轻快而温和。
She studies Reed. Her smile and tone are just as Reed remembers—light and warm.

Paper Heron: You are so very much like her.

芦草结：……和她？
Reed: Her?

鹭鸶剪：我知道的，你就像惠姑一样，是短生之种。春生冬死，命数极短。
Paper Heron: Mayfly. She too was a reed, sprouting in spring, withering by winter.

鹭鸶剪：你果然也像她一样急切。
Paper Heron: And just like her, you move with haste in every single moment.

那个她们都很熟悉的名字引出了编辑眼中的怀念和怅惘。
A name that they both know lingers in the air, stirring up memories and melancholy.

芦草结：惠姑……她……

Paper Heron: That's why I reached out when I saw your post. Fate really seems determined to bring your kind to me.

鹭鸶剪：这段长达四百年的因果，还要由你来解开。

芦草结：解开……？可是风结不是全部已经……
Reed: Another one? But didn't I already ...

鹭鸶剪：不是的，一切还未真正结束。长生之法，也并未真正断绝。
Paper Heron: The story has yet to come to an end. The Method of Longevity didn't truly die with the sword.

鹭鸶剪：当年我以为自己将永久沉眠于梅花树中，便以为长生之法也将随我一同消失。
Paper Heron: When I shattered it, I truly didn't expect I'd ever wake again. I thought the Method of Longevity would die with me.

鹭鸶剪：没想到世事更新，多亏了你和人类的新发明，我才能重现于世。
Paper Heron: And even less that I'd be awakened by this new Qi.

她感慨地抚上落灰的老梅树。

鹭鸶剪：长生剑只是器物，只要我在，便仍有长生之法。

鹭鸶剪：这也是我真正要予以你的报答。
