芦草结：…………！！！
Reed: ...!!!

她听到自己的心跳骤然分明了起来。
Her heartbeat quickens in her chest.

芦草结：这……
Reed: I ...

鹭鸶剪：别怕，这法门听着玄妙，实际上不过一瞬而已。
Paper Heron: Don't be afraid. It sounds complicated, but it only takes a moment to grasp.

鹭鸶剪：我在梅树中等了四百年，是你给了我重生的希望。我知道，你一直执着于长生的故事，就是在寻求这个答案。
Paper Heron: You've returned me to life. Please, allow me to extend yours.

她微笑着伸出手，向芦草结点了点头。
She smiles and extends her hand, then nods to Reed.

鹭鸶剪：来吧，我将法门传授于你。
Paper Heron: Now, give me your hand.

一直以来追寻的答案马上就要落入掌中。
The answer she has pursued across lifetimes finally within reach.

面对此情此景，芦草结忽然感到了没来由的惶惑。
Yet now that it's here, Reed feels an inexplicable panic.

芦草结：我……真的可以吗？
Reed: Are you ... Are you for real, like, really real?

鹭鸶剪：害怕了？你会后悔吗？
Paper Heron: Having second thoughts?

芦草结用力抓了抓头发，比几天前更枯黄的苇叶因此摇落一地。
Reed touches her own hair with anxiety. More blades of grass, each one growing yellower with each passing day, fall to the ground.

鹭鸶剪：也是……对我来说，那是四百年前的过往。对你来说，却只是方才的幻境。
Paper Heron: I would never wish to pressure you. An offer like this could take time to process.

鹭鸶剪：看完了这样的故事，知道了惠姑最后的命运……也许你会有新的想法。
Paper Heron: Perhaps you feel differently about longevity now, after seeing what happened to Mayfly.

鹭鸶剪收回了手，静静地等待着芦草结的回答。
Paper Heron withdraws her hand and waits for Reed's answer.

鹭鸶剪：小小草，在知晓了这一切后，你还会继续追寻长生吗？
Paper Heron: Do you still wish for more time in this world, little reed?

芦草结沉默了一会儿，而后，她缓慢而坚定地抬起头来。
She reflects on the question for a long while. A moment later, she raises her head slowly and firmly.

芦草结：我会。
Reed: I do.

芦草结：尽管我们的时间不过一个四季，但生命都予以了我和我的族群尽情去追求它的权利。我们乐于这样做，也勇于这样做。
Reed: I know my time's short, but I still have a life to live, just like anyone else, and I have the right to live as long as I can.

芦草结：无论长生是真正存在，或只是一个骗局。我都不会因为未知的结果和恐惧，就放弃这份追寻本身。
Reed: Even if it's hard, even if it's impossible, I can't stop just because I'm scared.

芦草结：我想要活下去，我想见更多未曾见过的景象，写出更好的报道，想成为众多“芦草结”中取得成功的那一个。
Reed: I want to live, to see more, write more, experience more.

芦草结：这是只属于我的生命旅程。我当然也希望能延长它，哪怕只是多一小时，一分钟！
Reed: I'll do anything to have one more day, one more hour, even one more minute to live.

芦草结向前一步。
She steps forward with growing certainty.

芦草结：即使寻求的事物一致，即使走上同一条路，我的经历，我的思想，我写下的报道也永远不会与谁全然相同。
Reed: I know that the "me" who sprouts next spring will be "me" in some way, but she'll never be "me." My goals, my experiences, my thoughts, my work ... They'll be lost forever.

芦草结：世上有许多苇草，而我也只是我。
Reed: And even if that Reed continues sprouting across a thousand lives, it will never be me again.

芦草结：所以我仍会继续追寻长生，直到抵达旅途的终点。
Reed: So I'll keep looking, till my last leaves have withered away.

芦草结：无论结局为何，我都不会后悔。
Reed: At least then, I can go without any regrets.

鹭鸶剪微微讶异，继而面露赞许。
Paper Heron's response begins with surprise, but soon, her face adopts that familiar smile, serene and wistful.

鹭鸶剪：好！
Paper Heron: Well said!

鹭鸶剪：这世上瞻前顾后举棋不定的庸类太多了，已经很少见你这样有志气的精怪。
Paper Heron: Many have held back for fear of the risks. It's rare to see someone with such remarkable courage.

鹭鸶剪：你能不昧本心，这很好，我没有看错人。
Paper Heron: I am glad to have at last found the right person.

她向着芦草结二次伸出了手，递过一个相当诚挚的邀请。
She extends her hand a second time, offering Reed a sincere invitation.

鹭鸶剪：跟我念——天地无极，任我裁量。
Paper Heron: Then repeat after me: In the vastness between heaven and earth, all things will bow to my measure.

芦草结向着她渴望的结局和答案伸出手。她的手指往前，碰触到了粗糙的树干。
Reed reaches for the ending and answer she has yearned for. Her fingers meet the rough bark.

芦草结：天地无极，任我裁量。
Reed: In the vastness between heaven and earth, all things will bow to my measure.

凝固的风在她指尖重重下坠，而后开始缓缓流动。
Frozen wind cascades from her fingertips, then begins to flow.

眼前的幻影倏然散开，另一道未曾设想的凝实身影大笑着从中走出。
Suddenly, the illusion before her eyes shatters. Another unexpected figure emerges from within, laughing.

？？？：终于让我等到了这一天！
???: Ahahaha ... Finally, after all this time!

梅树下的人随意拍了拍肩头，拂去了一丁点儿尘土。
The figure beneath the Mei tree brushes away the ash from her shoulder.

芦草结下意识地朝后退去。她万分惊异，以至于无法立刻从一片空白的脑海中找出那个名字。
Reed steps back in shock. The name falters on her tongue, as if she's unable to believe it herself.

芦草结：你是——任仙子？
Reed: You-You're Rén!

任仙子：不错。你倒是与他们不同，尚且讲几分情义，还识得允诺你传法的恩人。
Master Ren: Indeed. Now, come and pay respect to your master.

芦草结：你骗我？！在论坛上一直联系我的人，并不是鹭鸶剪……
Reed: So it was you who sent those messages on the forum, not Heron?

芦草结：天啊，那我——
Reed: And I've, I've just ...

编辑震惊地后退一步，意识到自己犯了一个天大的错误。
Reed staggers, the depth of her mistake striking her with the force of a heavy blow.

任仙子微微一笑，似乎对她的惊惶全不在意。
Master Rén's smile grows mad and overwide, unconcerned by her fear.

任仙子：我虽假借了她的名号，但授法一事却从无欺瞒。你既助我脱困，我这便带你长生。
Master Ren: There's no need to be afraid. I may have used Paper Heron's name to bring you here, but I did not lie about the Method of Longevity. I will guide you to it, if you wish.

她向芦草结额前伸出手去。
She reaches for Reed's forehead.

这只手落空了。
But her hand meets nothing but air.

芦草结：……我做了什么，值得你这样大费周章？！
Reed: You-You did all this to bring me here, just to make me your student? Why?

芦草结：你又在策划些什么阴谋？!
Reed: What're you trying to do?

她的质问换来了一声嗤笑。
Her question is met with a mocking laugh.

任仙子：呵，又是一个一生所求近在眼前，却畏葸不前的鼠辈。
Master Ren: Hmph. I had hoped you were wise enough to not mistake my kindness for malice.

任仙子：事到如今，你何须在意细枝末节？无论何人，赐法于你之人，才能应你所求！
Master Ren: All this fuss over a borrowed name, and yet you overlook the truth. I am your only hope to attain longevity.

任仙子：凡有所求，又怎会没有代价！既有所求，为何又在此刻畏首畏尾？
Master Ren: Everything has a price. If longevity is what you desire, you must take the risk and pay it.

任仙子：百年前那一次谋求，我本就已聚得了足够的气，重伤揽诸。没想到鹭鸶剪一意孤行，全然不顾此地众生。
Master Ren: I came so close back then. Lǎnzhū would have been long dead if Heron hadn't stood in my way.

任仙子：她折了法剑，救下揽诸，令此地气息滞涩，令我与她沉睡至今，整整四百年！
Master Ren: I never thought she would be mad enough to shatter her school's legacy just to seal me away.

呼啸的风声几乎压过了她的声音。
The rising wind nearly swallows up her words.

任仙子：……四百年过去，当年其他人早已化作飞灰。
Master Ren: So much time has passed. None who remember those days now live. Only you and I.

但这风声很快又被土地崩裂、震颤的响动盖去。
But now even the howl of the wind is lost beneath the roar of cracking earth.

任仙子：你当知晓，若鹭鸶剪未曾横加阻拦，诸多小妖的牺牲本不会被白白浪费！
Master Ren: All those lives wasted because of her!

芦草结：你难道想……
Reed: You're not gonna ...

罔顾芦草结的惊愕，任仙子猛然拂动衣袖，梅树根系附近的一小片地面陷落下去。
Ignoring Reed's shock, Master Rén flicks her sleeve sharply, and a patch of ground near the Mei tree's roots sinks.

从岩层与泥土的缝隙中涌出水流，甚至偶有几条惊慌的游鱼。
Water surges from the cracks between rock and soil, carrying panicked fish along with it.

任仙子：祝县众人，于此地铺设法宝，无意间引了一线生机给我，我便收敛些力道，不至于毁伤他们的屋舍。
Master Ren: If those "cables" hadn't been built, I wouldn't have awoken so soon. For that, I am grateful.

任仙子：你解开风结，打通揽诸身上的气穴。天地气顺，我也得了解脱——我自然要谢你！
Master Ren: Ahahaha ... I should thank you, too, for untying those knots and freeing me from the seal.

任仙子：忘恩负义之辈，岂能假称仙人！
Master Ren: You see, unlike Master Heron, I ensure those who aid me are properly repaid.

任仙子：过来！
Master Ren: Come here.

她拉过芦草结，右手聚起气息，对准了眼前凭空生出的湖泊。
She yanks Reed close. Qi gathers in her right hand as she aims at the newly formed lake.

树叶摇落，土地震颤，水面荡起一圈圈波纹。
Leaves fall like rain from the tree as the earth buckles. Ripples bounce across the water.

湖水仍在上涨。
And the water continues to rise.

任仙子：今日诛杀这揽诸，我便夺了它的气，谋得长生！
Master Ren: Today the beast will fall, and I will ascend triumphant.

芦草结：——！
Reed: ...!

湖水如同芦草结的恐惧一般满溢而出，澄澈的清水无情地淹过干黄的枯草，而大地的颤动使它们抖得都如筛子一般。
The lake overflows, soaking the parched yellow grass around it. The chaos of the scene matches the mounting panic surging through Reed's body.

顾不得其他，编辑猛地拽住任仙子的胳膊。
Forgetting everything else, she grabs at Master Rén's arm.

芦草结：停下，这里的人是无辜的！
Reed: Stop! You can't do this!

芦草结：任仙子——
Reed: Rén!

她打了个趔趄，险些跌落到湖中。
She stumbles, almost falling into the lake.

和过往影像所示的一般，揽诸的眼睛本是此地的一片湖水。
Just as the visions showed, Lǎnzhū's eyes were once a lake at this very spot.

在数百年的沉睡后，它终于要醒来了。
Now after centuries of slumber, it awakens.

芦草结：等等……！
Reed: I can't let her ...

风声。
The wind cries.

芦草结：不能……灾难……
Reed: ... destroy the city.

风朝湖面中心席卷而去。
A gale rushes toward the center of the lake.

周遭的万事万物都被呼啸而过的劲风撕扯着。
Signs and awnings, bikes and roof shingles, everything the wind touches is pulled up in the rush.

芦草结：我必须……拦住……
Reed: I have to do something.

但她根本无法再次抵达任仙子近旁。
But she can't reach her.

一切已无可挽回。
It's too late now.

？？？：不必忧心。
???: No need to worry.

芦草结：……谁？
Reed: Huh?

在猎猎作响的风中，她捕捉到了细微的，熟悉的声音。
Somewhere in the groaning of the wind, she catches a faint, familiar voice.

？？？：凡有生者，大多渴望存续。追求长生，亦是万物本能。
???: Every creature, whether beast or man, wishes for more time in this world.

？？？：过盛则衰，枯后则荣。揽诸想活下去，是它的本能。它苏醒时伴随灾难，却也自在这套规律流转之中，能平衡世间气的流动。
???: But know this: Those at their peak will decline, and those that have fallen will rise, for it is the Way to take from those in excess and give to those who lack. When Lǎnzhū sleeps, the world around it thrives; when it awakens, the world falls into ruin. All is in balance.

？？？：天行有常。你无须阻拦她。
???: The workings of Heaven remain constant. There is no need to stop her.

芦草结并未应答。她艰难地向前去，头上的草叶在狂风中弯折。
Reed doesn't answer. She forces herself forward, the grass blades on her head bending flat against the fierce wind.

她试图尽一点微小的气力，但任仙子已经抬起手，准备击下最后一掌。
She strains with all her might, but Master Rén has already raised her hand, ready to strike.

任仙子：再要分辨是非对错，为时已晚！后世之事，与你我何干！
Master Ren: It's too late. The beast ends today, and your mission with it.

任仙子：喝！
Master Ren: Haaah!

开视频

芦草结：揽诸……睁眼了……
Reed: Lǎnzhū has awakened.

任仙子：我已准备万全，这揽诸如此虚弱……为何气竟在流失……？
Master Ren: The beast is weak. But my Qi, it flows out from me.

任仙子：——鹭鸶剪，你欺我至此！
Master Ren: What have you done, Heron?

任仙子：我……定不会……
Master Ren: I will never ...

任仙子：——！
Master Ren: ...!

鹭鸶剪：八景冥合，炁入玄玄。
Paper Heron: Eight views merge, the mystery of Qi.

鹭鸶剪：三光无明，皆失其路。
Paper Heron: Three lights darken, and all lose their way.

SU-22 别来无恙 / Long Time No See

腾起的水雾模糊了所有人的视线，也包括慌张逃窜的魔精。
The rising mist blurs everyone's vision, including that of a terrified, fleeing Critter.

一只手伸来，轻松地拎起了它，使它不至于跌入地面裂缝里。
A hand reaches in and lifts it up with ease, saving it from falling into the growing cracks.

鹭鸶剪：……
Paper Heron: ...

她想起了第一次与它见面的时刻。她们和现在一样狼狈。
She remembers when they first met. She had been just as miserable then as she is now.

回忆

焦煳味弥漫在空气中。鹭鸶剪坐在梅树边，望了望头顶。
A burning ozone smell hangs in the air. Paper Heron sits beneath the Mei tree and looks up.

雷光早已隐去了。她松了口气，又看向脚边。
The lightning is gone. She sighs in relief, then glances toward her feet.

魔精：……呜。
Critter: *whimper*

望着这挨了几记雷，有气无力的黑黝黝一团，鹭鸶剪思索片刻，随便捡了个跑到嘴边的称呼。
A black fuzzball, weakened from multiple lightning strikes. Paper Heron looks down at her, pity welling up in her for the creature, despite everything.

鹭鸶剪：咪咪，过来，过来。
Paper Heron: Psps, come here, little one, come.

魔精：……？
Critter: ...?

鹭鸶剪：我师门有言，行走于世，绝不可沦为忘恩负义之辈。
Paper Heron: My master always said we should remember the good done to us and find ways to repay it.

鹭鸶剪：你救我一命，引雷劈开了梅树，放我出来。虽是无意，我也应还你恩情。
Paper Heron: You drew that lightning to the Mei tree and freed me from my seal. Though it was an accident, I have reaped its benefits, and for that, I must give you my thanks.

鹭鸶剪：既身无他物，就授一法门与你。
Paper Heron: I have nothing of value save the Method. Here.

消回忆

鹭鸶剪：你走吧。
Paper Heron: Now, be on your way.

她放下挣扎的魔精。它飞快地消失在了远处的草丛里。
She releases the struggling Critter, and it runs swiftly into the distant grass before vanishing from sight.

鹭鸶剪抬起头，另一个身影正穿过水雾，朝她靠近。
Paper Heron raises her head. Another figure is walking toward her through the mist.

芦草结：……
Reed: ...

编辑谨慎地打量着她。
The editor studies this new woman with a familiar face, cautious not to make the same mistake.

芦草结：……鹭鸶剪？
Reed: Paper Heron? Is that you?

芦草结：我应该不会再认错人吧……
Reed: Is it really you?

骡子：咴……
Mule: Whinny ...

刚才不知躲去何处的老骡小跑过来，亲昵地唤了几声。
The old mule, inexplicably safe despite all the calamity, trots over and whinnies affectionately.

鹭鸶剪拍了拍它的脑袋，朝芦草结露出一个微笑。
Paper Heron pats its head and smiles at Reed.

鹭鸶剪：小小草，这次真的是我。
Paper Heron: Yes, Reedit. It's the real me, this time.

湖边的餐馆刚开业不久，生意却异常火爆。
The restaurant by the lake has only just opened for the day, but it's already packed with customers.

来县里旅游的客人，大都也愿意多花些钱，近距离瞧瞧这片一夜间现出的湖水。
Visitors are willing to pay extra to see this new lake that appeared overnight.

街坊Ⅰ：早说了，咱这里是风水宝地，是出神仙状元的地方！
Neighbor I: What did I tell you? This place is blessed. So many bright talents!

街坊Ⅰ：看看看看，上头来调查了对不？都上电视了！
Neighbor I: See those reporters? We're gonna be on TV.

街坊Ⅱ：弄得吵死喽！那么多人！一个湖，一棵树，有啥好看的？
Neighbor II: So much for peace and quiet. I don't get it. What's so special about an old tree and a lake, anyway?

服务员：哎，别这么说。李叔这些天做梦也想着餐馆经营，人多了，生意好，他好盖大楼房！
Waiter: Look on the bright side. Uncle Lǐ's been thinking about getting into the food business lately. With all these visitors, I bet he'll be moving into a big new house in no time. Isn't that right, Lǐ?

街坊Ⅰ：买了叫你们上屋里打麻将！
Neighbor I: Haha, sure is. When I've got the place settled, I'll have all of you over for a night of mahjong.

服务员：好啊，可要赢你钱的，说话得算数！
Waiter: We'll be there, and we won't go easy on you at the table.

街坊Ⅰ：算，怎么不算！
Neighbor I: Do your worst. Hah-hah!

角落的餐桌边，有人朝这边频频张望着。
Guests at the corner tables take turns stealing conspicuous glances in their direction.

服务员赶紧加快步子走来，放下一盘符离集烧鸡。
The waiter hurries over and sets down a plate of Fuliji Roast Chicken.

芦草结：谢谢。
Reed: Thank you.

服务员：别客气。对了，你们是来旅游的吧？
Waiter: Here on a visit? You don't look like you're from around here.

服务员：镇上最近来了不少人，做小生意的也多，不要乱买工艺品啦，不划算的。
Waiter: We've been getting a lot of visitors lately. Just a heads-up: Watch out for the tourist traps, eh? Some of the souvenirs in the gift shops are pure rubbish.

服务员：这把剑质量就不行，这都断了。省几个钱，还能多加道菜呢。
Waiter: Ah, just look at that sword. Exactly what I mean. What a shame. Better off spending your money on local cuisine, I'd say.

鹭鸶剪：那太好了，这次还尝了青螺炖鸭，下次就尝尝招牌的包公鱼！
Paper Heron: Appreciated! We just tried the duck and snail stew. Maybe Bāo Zhěng's fish next?

脚步声远去，餐馆里的谈话声盖过了鹭鸶剪轻叩剑身的声响。
The waiter turns away. Paper Heron taps the sword gently, but any sound it might make doesn't rise above the chatter of the restaurant.

她抚了抚那道断口，捡起被搁置的话题。
She lets her hand linger over the fractured blade, then picks up their conversation.

鹭鸶剪：小小草，你刚才要和我说什么来着？
Paper Heron: So, what did you want to tell me, Reedie?

芦草结：不算特别重要的事。但我还是得当面告诉你才好。
Reed: Err, it's not a big deal really. I just wanted to say it in person.

芦草结：对不起，鹭鸶剪。
Reed: I'm sorry, Heron.

编辑郑重地开口。
The words pour out bitter and regretful.

芦草结：我不应该上任仙子的当，放她出来……我本来已经发现了你们语气的不同，最后却还是相信了她。
Reed: I shouldn't have fallen for Rén's trick. I knew something was off about her, but I-I guess I got greedy.

芦草结：如果不是你……
Reed: If you hadn't come to my rescue in time, I ...

鹭鸶剪：好了，好了。事情都结束了，为何还要苛责自己？
Paper Heron: There, there. It's over now. We needn't worry about what's in the past?

她玩笑般拿起那把剑，在手中掂了掂，又小心放下。
She picks up the sword playfully, weighs it in her hand, then sets it down.

鹭鸶剪：过去，天地之中的气像浪潮一般涌动。如今四百年过去，它们已成了平缓的细流。
Paper Heron: Long ago, Qi flowed strong in the world, surging and rolling like ocean waves. But now, it has quieted.

鹭鸶剪：摇山撼海的场面不会再有啦。那些术法也早就不复当初的威力。
Paper Heron: It no longer has the force to shake the plains or topple mountains, and the spells drawn from its power have lost much of their might.

鹭鸶剪：时过境迁，揽诸早已不复从前。任仙子贸然打通气穴，但此时情景早已今非昔比。
Paper Heron: Lǎnzhū's power is much the same. That's why things didn't go Rén's way, even though she awakened the beast.

鹭鸶剪：曾经，揽诸强盛，而她不过一画皮小妖，方可吸取揽诸之气，强化自身。
Paper Heron: When Lǎnzhū was strong, Rén could draw out its Qi to strengthen herself.

鹭鸶剪：如今揽诸虚弱，气的流势已然改变。当初她从揽诸身上抽得的气，如今加倍还了回去。
Paper Heron: But the flow of its Qi changed course. It draws in Qi rather than letting it flow out. A necessary balance. This is the Way.

鹭鸶剪：此后，揽诸的苏醒不会再造成灾难。你尽可放心。
Paper Heron: Lǎnzhū is unlikely to cause any disasters for a long time to come. You needn't worry.

鹭鸶剪向前探身，拍拍芦草结的肩膀。
She leans forward and offers a hand of comfort to Reed.

鹭鸶剪：而且，多亏你如我所料，解开了最后的系结，这一切才得以圆满。也不枉我中途一直提示你。
Paper Heron: Thanks to you, everything's finally settled. Though I can't help but take a little of the credit. I did do my best to guide you here.

芦草结：咦……？
Reed: Hm?

芦草结：你一直在默许我解开系结，放出揽诸和任仙子……？
Reed: Hold on, so, then you really were the one who guided me here? You wanted me to set Rén free from the seal?

鹭鸶剪却没有立刻回答，而是微笑着望向她。
Paper Heron lets the question hang in the air, offering only a knowing smile at first.

似乎是斟酌了一会儿词句，最后，她开口了。
Then she speaks, her answer delicately pruned and insightful.

鹭鸶剪：我刚联系上你时，便隐约有了猜测。在你来到祝县之后，便用望气一法加以确认，知道了你本是苇草。
Paper Heron: When I saw your post on the forum, I knew that you were a Yao, but I couldn't be sure of what you'd do until you showed up in person.

鹭鸶剪：我料到你不会放弃长生线索，也料到了任仙子会利用这一点。
Paper Heron: Just like Mayfly, I knew you would take any risk to find the Method, and I realized Rén would seize on your desire and exploit it.

鹭鸶剪：我也预料到，你即使知道了所有的事，也依然会做出自己的选择。
Paper Heron: You wouldn't be put off by what you saw in the Wind Knots; I knew you'd see it through to the end.

鹭鸶剪：所以我任由任仙子顶替我，与你联系，也放任了她先我一步出现在你面前，令揽诸苏醒。
Paper Heron: So when Rén took my name to approach you on the forum, I didn't stop her, just like I didn't stop her from releasing Lǎnzhū.

鹭鸶剪：而后，天地之气，重回流通。一切因果前缘，亦随风消解。
Paper Heron: She would only be returning Qi to its rightful place, not disturbing it.

鹭鸶剪的声音稍稍低了下去。略作停顿之后，她接续上未尽的话题。
Her voice drops. After a brief pause, she continues.

鹭鸶剪：每个人的欲望互相交织，然后此消彼长，达成平衡，世事便如此延续。
Paper Heron: One gains, and the other loses. In the end, what's lost returns to where it is needed, and thus balance is maintained.

鹭鸶剪：是你的坚持，让一切来到了这里。
Paper Heron: Were it not for your resolve, none of this would have come to pass.

鹭鸶剪：正因为你、我、任仙子，每个卷入其中的人，都不曾后悔，再来千百次，也还会如此选择。
Paper Heron: And because all who took part in this—you, Rén, me—stood by each of our choices to the end ...

鹭鸶剪：诸般因果，才能消却。这个故事才会迎来它最合适的结局。
Paper Heron: What started hundreds of years ago could at last come to its rightful end.

鹭鸶剪：你从来无需道歉。
Paper Heron: So you see, there's no need to apologize. All unfolded as fate intended.

芦草结：……我知道啦。
Reed: I see.

编辑如释重负地松了一口气，那些草叶也因此抖落了几分。
Reed lets out a long breath. Her grass blades wilt on her head.

芦草结：虽然没有得到长生之法，却能参与这一切，留下一篇很好的报道……
Reed: I haven't found longevity, but at least I found a story worth telling.

芦草结：对我来说，现在的结局也已经足够圆满。
Reed: That's good enough for me.

她的语气中仍有一丝遗憾。但它们很快就轻轻地隐没了。
She can't hide the sting of regret in her voice, but she buries it as best she can.

鹭鸶剪难得地捕捉到了这点儿变化。
Yet Paper Heron seizes on it.

鹭鸶剪：小小草，我还没说完呢。
Paper Heron: There's a little more to it, actually.

鹭鸶剪：百年前，惠姑倒下的土壤之上，生出了一丛新绿。
Paper Heron: In the spring after Mayfly's death, a green shoot grew from the place where she last stood.

鹭鸶剪：其后，她的同族虽然春生冬死，却年年都能从干枯的身躯之中再度抽芽。
Paper Heron: When winter came, it withered, but in each following spring, a sprout grew anew.

芦草结：——！
Reed: ...!

芦草结：你是说，现在的我——
Reed: You mean I'm ...?

鹭鸶剪：惠姑的所求，确有收获。
Paper Heron: In a way, Mayfly's wish has been fulfilled.

芦草结：这样……
Reed: Yeah.

芦草结：我很喜欢这个答案。
Reed: I like this little epilogue.

芦草结微笑着合上自己的笔记本。
Reed smiles as she closes her notebook.

芦草结：接下来的时间里，我打算扩充一些别的选题。
Reed: I'm planning to write a couple more stories before winter comes.

芦草结：希望以后的“芦草结”们读到我留下的记录，也会由衷地称赞它。
Reed: I hope the "Reed" that sprouts next year likes them too.

鹭鸶剪：唔……
Paper Heron: Hmm.

鹭鸶剪皱起眉头。
She frowns playfully.

鹭鸶剪：我早就想说……你是一株苇草，却格外擅长思考。
Paper Heron: I must say, you're quite inquisitive for a reed.

鹭鸶剪：放在我拜师的年代，就是大家争着抢的修道好苗子。
Paper Heron: You'd likely make an excellent Daoist. Were you born in my time, many would have wanted you as their student.

鹭鸶剪：不如我来教——
Paper Heron: How about I—

芦草结：不了不了，我的规划是一直努力到成为责任编辑！
Reed: Thanks for the offer, but I've always wanted to be a commissioning editor. I think I've had enough of Daoism for one lifetime!

两人笑了一阵，芦草结先收敛了声音。
They both laugh for a long while. Reed composes herself first.

她想了一想，向鹭鸶剪发出邀请。
She thinks for a moment, then extends an invitation.

芦草结：再去那棵梅树边走走，怎么样？
Reed: But how about we take a walk around the Mei tree again?

梅树下多了两个身影，一个矮着身子，一个立在一旁。
Two figures approach the Mei tree. One crouches low; the other stands nearby.

鹭鸶剪仰望着满树红梅，鼓励般拍了拍树干。
Paper Heron looks up at the tree full of red blossoms and pats the bark as if greeting an old friend.

鹭鸶剪：过一段时间，这棵梅树大概也会因为开花太勤登上新闻吧。
Paper Heron: This old thing will soon bloom more beautifully than ever.

旁边的编辑端详着树边铺设的砖石。当地人告诉过她，这些石块是早些年从塌了的老房子里捡来的，也算颇有年头。
The editor examines the stone bricks arranged around the tree, apparently recovered from some old houses that collapsed years ago.

一块半埋在土中的石头吸引了她的注意。
A half-buried stone catches her attention.

芦草结：这是……
Reed: This is ...

她弯腰想去拨开石头上的泥土。
She bends down and brushes away the layer of dirt covering its face.

鹭鸶剪：走了，小小草。
Paper Heron: Come on, Reedie.

鹭鸶剪：从这湖边抄近路去街上，我们还有空逛一会儿呢——
Paper Heron: We'll still have some time if we take a shortcut to the streets.

芦草结：噢，来啦！
Reed: Oh, sure!

编辑小跑几步，跟上了同伴的步子。
The editor runs a few steps to keep up with her companion.

芦草结：明天或者后天，我打算回编辑部一趟。
Reed: I've gotta report back to the office soon, tomorrow or at least by the day after.

芦草结：你呢？你之后准备去做什么？
Reed: What about you? What're you gonna do?

鹭鸶剪扬扬脑袋，示意她望向远处的高楼。
Paper Heron tilts her head, gesturing toward a tall building in the distance.

鹭鸶剪：继续游历，去见识这几百年错过的东西。
Paper Heron: I'll keep traveling. I seem to have missed a great deal over these last centuries.

鹭鸶剪：最近，我能尝出更多菜的味道了。所以我会先挑个好吃的最多的地方，住上十天半个月……
Paper Heron: And, you know, my taste seems to have restored a little. Perhaps I'll search for a place with good food and stay there for a half-month.

芦草结：要是有空，我们还可以同行。
Reed: I'd love to join you, if I still have time, that is.

芦草结：你还会继续用那个论坛账户吧？
Reed: You'll still be on the forum, right? The same account?

鹭鸶剪：当然了，我还有一位朋友要介绍给你……嗯？
Paper Heron: Of course, and there's a friend I'd like you to meet, hm?

猫：喵。
Cat: Meow.

湖边安静，风也温和，常有些小动物在附近出没。
The lake lies quiet as the wind laps gently over it. Now a place where small creatures can gather to rest beneath the shade.

鹭鸶剪一把将这团绒球提溜了起来，毫不客气地摸着它油光水滑的毛。
Paper Heron scoops up the fur ball and strokes its sleek coat.

鹭鸶剪：喂，咪咪，你是在这里安家了吗？
Paper Heron: Hey, little one. Are you from around here?

鹭鸶剪：既然有缘，我一会儿帮你抓几条鱼来……
Paper Heron: How about some fish for supper, hm?

见这只猫一副心安理得的模样，编辑也将手掌落在了它背上。
Seeing the cat lounge contentedly beside them, Reed rests her hand on its back as well.

她还没忘记最后的问题。
She remembers her last question.

芦草结：你说的朋友也是你的网友吗？也会……五感缺失吗？
Reed: A friend, huh? Someone else you met on the forum? Who are they?

芦草结：要是这样，就选几个菜色不那么清淡的餐馆……
Reed: Any idea what kinda food they like? There's a couple restaurants around here that look good.

鹭鸶剪：别担心，不全是网友，这个人你也认识。
Paper Heron: You needn't worry. He'll be grateful to eat anything, and in fact, you already know him.

鹭鸶剪：那五感缺失的毛病，是我第一次被匆忙封入树中落下的。我是一时半会儿好不了啦，但他应当没事。
Paper Heron: Last time, the seal took away my sense of taste, but his, at least, seems fine.

鹭鸶剪：我猜他眼下总该醒了。剩下的事情可以待会儿论坛上商量。
Paper Heron: He will have awakened by now. We can discuss it on the forum later.

鹭鸶剪：尽管天大地大，但现在联系比往日方便太多，总能说上话、见上面的。
Paper Heron: I have to say, the Internet is quite amazing, connecting people from all corners of the globe.

芦草结：天大地大吗……
Reed: It sure is.

编辑望着湖面与天际相接的那一线银色。
The editor gazes at the silver line where the lake meets the sky.

芦草结：呼——
Reed: *blow*

她高举起手臂，舒展着紧绷许久的肢体。
She raises her arms, stretching her tense body.

芦草结：好像白费了很多紧张的心情……但这阵风真好。
Reed: So I got all worked up for nothing. But I guess I shouldn't complain.

芦草结：到头来，末日和灾难都没发生，多大的天地之间也只是多了片能散步的地方。
Reed: There's no cataclysm, no raging beast, just a tree, a lake, and a gentle breeze over a quiet little path.

鹭鸶剪：是啊。
Paper Heron: Indeed.

她注视着湖中的游鱼。看它们时而上浮，时而潜入更深处。
She watches the fish as they bob up from the lake, surfacing one moment, diving deep the next.

池鱼入水，顷刻便会隐没踪迹。
One jumps up and vanishes away the moment it hits the water.

鹭鸶剪：不过一方鱼池而已。
Paper Heron: It was all but a splash in the pond.
